🔍 2️⃣ DISCOVERY SECTION (BENTO + LAYERED)
tsx
// components/landing/Discovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

const restaurants = [
  { name: 'Sakura Hills', cuisine: 'Japanese', rating: 4.8, trend: '+12%', signal: 92, vibe: 'Romantic', price: '$$$' },
  { name: 'La Piazza', cuisine: 'Italian', rating: 4.7, trend: '+8%', signal: 88, vibe: 'Casual', price: '$$' },
  { name: 'Spice Route', cuisine: 'Indian', rating: 4.9, trend: '+15%', signal: 96, vibe: 'Vibrant', price: '$$' },
  { name: 'The Grill', cuisine: 'Steakhouse', rating: 4.6, trend: '+5%', signal: 82, vibe: 'Upscale', price: '$$$$' },
  { name: 'Oceanside', cuisine: 'Seafood', rating: 4.8, trend: '+10%', signal: 90, vibe: 'Relaxed', price: '$$$' },
  { name: 'Bistro Moderne', cuisine: 'French', rating: 4.7, trend: '+7%', signal: 86, vibe: 'Intimate', price: '$$$' },
]

export function Discovery() {
  const [rankedRestaurants, setRankedRestaurants] = useState(restaurants)
  const [hoveredCard, setHoveredCard] = useState<number | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    // Continuous re-ranking simulation
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      const shuffled = [...rankedRestaurants]
      for (let i = shuffled.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
        const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1))
        ;[shuffled[i], shuffled[j]] = [shuffled[j], shuffled[i]]
      }
      setRankedRestaurants(shuffled)
      
      // Animate reorder
      gsap.to('.discovery-card', {
        y: () => gsap.utils.random(-8, 8),
        duration: 0.5,
        stagger: 0.03,
        ease: 'back.out(0.5)',
      })
    }, 7000)
    
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [rankedRestaurants])

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden -mt-20">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#0a0a0b] via-transparent to-transparent" />
      <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-primary/30 to-transparent" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 w-full h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-secondary/30 to-transparent" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/4 right-0 w-96 h-96 bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-1/3 left-0 w-80 h-80 bg-tertiary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/4 w-64 h-64 bg-secondary/5 rounded-full blur-[80px]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        {/* Header with bento layout */}
        <div className="grid lg:grid-cols-12 gap-12 mb-16">
          <div className="lg:col-span-5">
            <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-primary/10 text-primary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
              MULTI-SIGNAL RANKING
            </span>
            <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
              Discovery that <br />
              <span className="gradient-text">understands</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-lg text-white/60">
              Not just keywords. Intent, context, trends, and your preferences.
              Every search teaches the system.
            </p>
            
            {/* Learning indicator */}
            <div className="mt-6 flex items-center gap-3 p-4 glass-panel">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                <span className="text-sm">🧠</span>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium">System learning</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40">+2.3% accuracy this week</p>
              </div>
              <div className="ml-auto text-primary text-sm">↑ 12%</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              <div className="glass-panel p-5">
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">6</p>
                <p className="text-sm text-white/40">ranking signals</p>
                <div className="mt-3 flex gap-1">
                  {[...Array(6)].map((_, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="flex-1 h-1 bg-primary/30 rounded-full" />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="glass-panel p-5">
                <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">98.7%</p>
                <p className="text-sm text-white/40">relevance score</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Restaurant grid - Dense Bento */}
        <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {rankedRestaurants.map((rest, i) => (
            <div
              key={rest.name}
              className={`discovery-card glass-panel overflow-hidden cursor-pointer transition-all duration-300
                         ${i === 0 ? 'ring-1 ring-primary/30' : ''}
                         hover:-translate-y-2 hover:bg-white/[0.08]`}
              onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredCard(i)}
              onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredCard(null)}
            >
              <div className="h-32 bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-secondary/20 relative overflow-hidden">
                <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/40" />
                <div className="absolute bottom-3 left-3">
                  <span className="px-2 py-1 bg-black/60 text-xs rounded-full">{rest.vibe}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="absolute top-3 right-3 flex gap-1">
                  <span className="text-yellow-400">★</span>
                  <span className="text-sm text-white">{rest.rating}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="p-5">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                  <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                  <span className="text-sm text-green-400">{rest.trend}</span>
                </div>
                <p className="text-white/60 text-sm mb-2">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                
                {/* Signal bars */}
                <div className="mt-3">
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mb-1">
                    <span>Match score</span>
                    <span>{rest.signal}%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                    <div 
                      className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
                      style={{ width: `${rest.signal}%` }}
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>
                
                {/* Hover reveal */}
                <div className={`mt-3 overflow-hidden transition-all duration-300 ${hoveredCard === i ? 'max-h-20 opacity-100' : 'max-h-0 opacity-0'}`}>
                  <button className="w-full py-2 bg-primary/20 text-primary text-sm rounded-lg hover:bg-primary/30 transition-all">
                    View details →
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        
        {/* Bottom CTA - Integrated */}
        <div className="mt-12 text-center">
          <button className="px-8 py-3 glass-panel hover:bg-white/10 transition-all">
            Explore all restaurants →
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
📅 3️⃣ RESERVATION SECTION (FULL CINEMATIC FLOW)
tsx
// components/landing/ReservationFlow.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'

const timeSlots = [
  { time: '6:00 PM', available: true, popular: false, demand: 45 },
  { time: '6:30 PM', available: true, popular: false, demand: 52 },
  { time: '7:00 PM', available: true, popular: true, demand: 89 },
  { time: '7:30 PM', available: true, popular: true, demand: 94 },
  { time: '8:00 PM', available: false, popular: false, demand: 100 },
  { time: '8:30 PM', available: true, popular: false, demand: 78 },
  { time: '9:00 PM', available: true, popular: false, demand: 65 },
  { time: '9:30 PM', available: true, popular: false, demand: 42 },
]

export function ReservationFlow() {
  const [selectedSlot, setSelectedSlot] = useState<number | null>(null)
  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false)
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false)
  const [partySize, setPartySize] = useState(2)

  const handleSelect = (index: number) => {
    if (!timeSlots[index].available) return
    
    gsap.to(`#slot-${index}`, {
      scale: 0.95,
      duration: 0.1,
      yoyo: true,
      repeat: 1,
    })
    
    setSelectedSlot(index)
  }

  const handleConfirm = () => {
    if (selectedSlot === null) return
    
    setIsLoading(true)
    
    const tl = gsap.timeline({
      onComplete: () => {
        setConfirmed(true)
        setIsLoading(false)
        setTimeout(() => {
          setConfirmed(false)
          setSelectedSlot(null)
        }, 2500)
      },
    })
    
    tl.to('.reservation-container', { scale: 0.96, duration: 0.2 })
    tl.to('.reservation-container', { scale: 1.03, duration: 0.4, ease: 'back.out(1.2)' })
    tl.to('.reservation-container', { scale: 1, duration: 0.2 })
  }

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_center,rgba(163,166,255,0.05),transparent_70%)]" />
      </div>
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/4 w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-tertiary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 right-1/3 w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[80px]" />
      
      {/* Floating particles for booking animation */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 pointer-events-none">
        {[...Array(30)].map((_, i) => (
          <div
            key={i}
            className="absolute w-1 h-1 bg-primary/20 rounded-full"
            style={{
              left: `${Math.random() * 100}%`,
              top: `${Math.random() * 100}%`,
              animation: `float ${Math.random() * 5 + 3}s ease-in-out infinite`,
            }}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="grid lg:grid-cols-12 gap-12 items-start">
          {/* Left column - Text */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-5 sticky top-32">
            <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-tertiary/10 text-tertiary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
              ZERO FRICTION
            </span>
            <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
              Book in <br />
              <span className="gradient-text">seconds</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-lg text-white/60 mb-6">
              Real-time availability. Instant confirmation. Zero clicks wasted.
            </p>
            
            {/* Stats */}
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center p-3 glass-panel">
                <span>Average booking time</span>
                <span className="font-mono gradient-text">2.3s</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center p-3 glass-panel">
                <span>Confirmation rate</span>
                <span className="font-mono gradient-text">99.8%</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* Right column - Reservation UI */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="reservation-container glass-panel p-6 md:p-8">
              {/* Restaurant preview */}
              <div className="flex gap-4 mb-6 pb-6 border-b border-white/10">
                <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-secondary/20 shimmer flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                  🍽️
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">Nobu Malibu</h3>
                  <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">Japanese • $$$$</p>
                  <div className="flex gap-1 mt-1">
                    <span className="text-yellow-400">★★★★★</span>
                    <span className="text-white/40 text-sm">(2.3k reviews)</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <p className="text-sm text-white/40">Today, Mar 23</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-green-400">● Available</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              {/* Time slots */}
              <div className="mb-6">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-3">SELECT TIME</p>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2">
                  {timeSlots.map((slot, i) => (
                    <button
                      key={slot.time}
                      id={`slot-${i}`}
                      onClick={() => handleSelect(i)}
                      disabled={!slot.available}
                      className={`relative py-3 rounded-xl font-medium transition-all text-sm
                        ${selectedSlot === i 
                          ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20' 
                          : slot.available 
                            ? 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-white' 
                            : 'bg-white/5 text-white/30 cursor-not-allowed line-through'
                        }`}
                    >
                      {slot.time}
                      {slot.popular && slot.available && (
                        <span className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 text-[9px] bg-tertiary text-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">
                          HOT
                        </span>
                      )}
                      {slot.demand > 80 && slot.available && (
                        <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 h-0.5 bg-orange-500/50 rounded-full" 
                             style={{ width: `${slot.demand}%` }} />
                      )}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              {/* Party size */}
              <div className="mb-6">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">PARTY SIZE</p>
                <div className="flex gap-2">
                  {[2, 4, 6, 8].map(size => (
                    <button
                      key={size}
                      onClick={() => setPartySize(size)}
                      className={`px-5 py-2 rounded-lg transition-all text-sm
                        ${partySize === size 
                          ? 'bg-white text-black' 
                          : 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10'
                        }`}
                    >
                      {size}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              {/* Special requests */}
              <div className="mb-6">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">SPECIAL REQUESTS</p>
                <textarea
                  placeholder="Dietary restrictions, allergies, special occasions..."
                  className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 
                           text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-sm resize-none
                           focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  rows={2}
                />
              </div>
              
              {/* Confirm button */}
              <button
                onClick={handleConfirm}
                disabled={selectedSlot === null || isLoading}
                className="w-full py-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                         font-semibold hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 transition-all 
                         disabled:opacity-50 disabled:hover:shadow-none active:scale-95"
              >
                {isLoading ? 'Confirming...' : confirmed ? '✓ Confirmed!' : `Book for ${timeSlots[selectedSlot]?.time || ''}`}
              </button>
              
              {/* Guarantee */}
              <p className="text-center text-xs text-white/40 mt-4">
                Free cancellation up to 2 hours before
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Success overlay */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {confirmed && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none z-50"
          >
            <div className="bg-black/95 backdrop-blur-xl rounded-2xl p-8 text-center border border-white/20 shadow-2xl">
              <motion.div
                initial={{ scale: 0 }}
                animate={{ scale: 1 }}
                transition={{ type: 'spring', delay: 0.1 }}
                className="w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4"
              >
                <svg className="w-10 h-10 text-green-500" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
                  <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
                </svg>
              </motion.div>
              <p className="text-2xl font-semibold">Reservation Confirmed!</p>
              <p className="text-white/60 mt-2">Check your email for details</p>
              <div className="mt-4 text-sm text-primary">
                Table reserved for {partySize} at {selectedSlot !== null ? timeSlots[selectedSlot].time : ''}
              </div>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ AI CONCIERGE (FULL STREAMING + BENTO)
tsx
// components/landing/AIConcierge.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  cards?: RestaurantCard[]
  streaming?: boolean
}

interface RestaurantCard {
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
}

export function AIConcierge() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm your AI concierge. Tell me what you're craving — I'll find the perfect spot." },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [streamingText, setStreamingText] = useState('')
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, streamingText])

  const streamResponse = (text: string, cards?: RestaurantCard[]) => {
    setStreamingText('')
    let i = 0
    
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (i < text.length) {
        setStreamingText(prev => prev + text[i])
        i++
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval)
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: text, cards }])
        setStreamingText('')
        setIsTyping(false)
      }
    }, 25)
  }

  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return

    // Add user message
    const userMessage: Message = {
      id: messages.length + 1,
      type: 'user',
      content: input,
    }
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMessage])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)

    // Simulate AI thinking
    setTimeout(() => {
      const responses: Record<string, { text: string; cards: RestaurantCard[] }> = {
        sushi: {
          text: "I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks for fresh, authentic Japanese cuisine:",
          cards: [
            { name: 'Sushi Nakazawa', cuisine: 'Omakase', rating: 4.9, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Intimate' },
            { name: 'Nobu', cuisine: 'Japanese Fusion', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Trendy' },
            { name: 'Sushi Yasuda', cuisine: 'Edomae', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$', vibe: 'Authentic' },
          ],
        },
        italian: {
          text: "Craving Italian? Here are the best authentic Italian restaurants near you, from cozy trattorias to upscale dining:",
          cards: [
            { name: 'La Piazza', cuisine: 'Tuscan', rating: 4.7, price: '$$', vibe: 'Romantic' },
            { name: 'Carbone', cuisine: 'Italian-American', rating: 4.9, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Vintage' },
            { name: 'Via Carota', cuisine: 'Northern Italian', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$', vibe: 'Cozy' },
          ],
        },
      }

      const lowerInput = userInput.toLowerCase()
      let responseText = "I found several great options based on your request. Here are my top recommendations:"
      let cards: RestaurantCard[] = [
        { name: 'Sakura Hills', cuisine: 'Japanese', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$', vibe: 'Romantic' },
        { name: 'La Piazza', cuisine: 'Italian', rating: 4.7, price: '$$', vibe: 'Casual' },
        { name: 'Spice Route', cuisine: 'Indian', rating: 4.9, price: '$$', vibe: 'Vibrant' },
      ]

      if (lowerInput.includes('sushi') || lowerInput.includes('japanese')) {
        responseText = responses.sushi.text
        cards = responses.sushi.cards
      } else if (lowerInput.includes('italian') || lowerInput.includes('pasta')) {
        responseText = responses.italian.text
        cards = responses.italian.cards
      } else if (lowerInput.includes('romantic')) {
        responseText = "Looking for a romantic dinner? These spots are perfect for date night, with intimate ambiance and exceptional cuisine:"
        cards = [
          { name: 'One if by Land', cuisine: 'American', rating: 4.9, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Romantic' },
          { name: 'River Cafe', cuisine: 'Italian', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Scenic' },
          { name: 'The Modern', cuisine: 'Contemporary', rating: 4.8, price: '$$$$', vibe: 'Elegant' },
        ]
      }

      streamResponse(responseText, cards)
    }, 1200)
  }

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0e0e0f] via-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]" />
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_top,rgba(163,166,255,0.08),transparent_60%)]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/3 left-0 w-96 h-96 bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[120px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-1/4 right-0 w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-tertiary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="grid lg:grid-cols-12 gap-12">
          {/* Left column */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-4">
            <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-primary/10 text-primary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
              AI CONCIERGE
            </span>
            <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
              Just <br />
              <span className="gradient-text">ask</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-lg text-white/60 mb-6">
              Natural language. Intelligent recommendations. Instant booking.
            </p>
            
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <div className="glass-panel p-3">
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40">TRY THESE</p>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2">
                  {['romantic dinner', 'best sushi', 'vegan options', 'rooftop bar'].map(example => (
                    <button
                      key={example}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setInput(example)
                        setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                      }}
                      className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                    >
                      {example}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="glass-panel p-3">
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40">LEARNING</p>
                <div className="mt-2">
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                    <span>Preference accuracy</span>
                    <span>94%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[94%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* Right column - Chat */}
          <div className="lg:col-span-8">
            <div className="glass-panel overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <motion.div
                    key={msg.id}
                    initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                    className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}
                  >
                    <div
                      className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                        msg.type === 'user'
                          ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                          : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {/* Restaurant cards */}
                      {msg.cards && (
                        <div className="mt-4 space-y-2">
                          {msg.cards.map((card, i) => (
                            <motion.div
                              key={card.name}
                              initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}
                              animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                              transition={{ delay: i * 0.1 }}
                              className="bg-white/10 rounded-xl p-3 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all"
                            >
                              <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                                <div>
                                  <p className="font-medium">{card.name}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{card.cuisine} • {card.price} • {card.vibe}</p>
                                </div>
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                  <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {card.rating}</span>
                                  <button className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg font-medium hover:bg-primary/90 transition-all">
                                    Book
                                  </button>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </motion.div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </motion.div>
                ))}
                
                {/* Streaming response */}
                {streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]">
                      <p className="text-sm">{streamingText}<span className="animate-pulse">▊</span></p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                
                {/* Typing indicator */}
                {isTyping && !streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              {/* Input area */}
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    ref={inputRef}
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder="Ask me anything..."
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50
                             transition-all"
                  />
                  <button
                    onClick={handleSend}
                    disabled={isTyping}
                    className="px-6 py-3 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                             font-medium hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 transition-all 
                             disabled:opacity-50 active:scale-95"
                  >
                    Send
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
🧑‍🍳 5️⃣ OWNER PREVIEW (LIVE DASHBOARD + AI AUTOMATION)
tsx
// components/landing/OwnerPreview.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

interface Booking {
  name: string
  time: string
  guests: number
  status: 'confirmed' | 'pending' | 'seated'
  avatar?: string
}

export function OwnerPreview() {
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState<Booking[]>([
    { name: 'Emma Watson', time: '7:00 PM', guests: 4, status: 'confirmed', avatar: 'EW' },
    { name: 'James Chen', time: '7:30 PM', guests: 2, status: 'confirmed', avatar: 'JC' },
    { name: 'Sofia Rodriguez', time: '8:00 PM', guests: 6, status: 'pending', avatar: 'SR' },
    { name: 'Michael Lee', time: '8:30 PM', guests: 3, status: 'confirmed', avatar: 'ML' },
  ])
  const [occupancy, setOccupancy] = useState(68)
  const [revenue, setRevenue] = useState(4280)
  const [suggestionIndex, setSuggestionIndex] = useState(0)

  const suggestions = [
    { title: 'No-Show Risk', description: 'High probability at 8 PM (42%)', action: 'Overbook by 10%', risk: 42 },
    { title: 'Demand Spike', description: 'Weekend evenings up 35% vs last week', action: 'Adjust pricing', risk: 35 },
    { title: 'Waitlist Optimization', description: 'Current wait time exceeds target by 12min', action: 'Send notifications', risk: 28 },
  ]

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate live updates
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      const newBooking: Booking = {
        name: ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim', 'Lisa Wong'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:${Math.random() > 0.5 ? '00' : '30'} PM`,
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        status: 'confirmed',
        avatar: ['DP', 'SK', 'LW'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
      }
      
      setBookings(prev => [newBooking, ...prev.slice(0, 5)])
      setOccupancy(prev => Math.min(95, prev + Math.random() * 4))
      setRevenue(prev => prev + Math.floor(Math.random() * 150))
      setSuggestionIndex(prev => (prev + 1) % suggestions.length)
      
      // Animate new booking
      gsap.to('.booking-item:first-child', {
        scale: 1.02,
        duration: 0.3,
        yoyo: true,
        repeat: 1,
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)',
      })
      
      // Animate occupancy bar
      gsap.to('.occupancy-bar', {
        width: `${occupancy + Math.random() * 4}%`,
        duration: 0.5,
      })
    }, 6000)
    
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [occupancy])

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_bottom,rgba(163,166,255,0.05),transparent_70%)]" />
        <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-primary/30 to-transparent" />
      </div>
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 right-0 w-[600px] h-[600px] bg-secondary/5 rounded-full blur-[120px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-1/4 w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[80px]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="text-center mb-16">
          <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-secondary/10 text-secondary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
            OWNER OS
          </span>
          <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
            Control, not <span className="gradient-text">chaos</span>
          </h2>
          <p className="text-xl text-white/60 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Real-time operations. AI automation. Complete visibility.
          </p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="grid lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          {/* Live Metrics Card */}
          <div className="glass-panel p-6">
            <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
              Live Metrics
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-5">
              <div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm mb-2">
                  <span>Occupancy</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">{Math.floor(occupancy)}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="h-2 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                  <div 
                    className="occupancy-bar h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full transition-all duration-500"
                    style={{ width: `${occupancy}%` }}
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center py-2 border-b border-white/10">
                <span className="text-white/60">Active Bookings</span>
                <span className="text-2xl font-semibold gradient-text">{bookings.length}</span>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center py-2 border-b border-white/10">
                <span className="text-white/60">Waitlist</span>
                <span className="text-2xl font-semibold text-yellow-400">8</span>
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center py-2">
                <span className="text-white/60">Revenue Today</span>
                <div className="text-right">
                  <span className="text-2xl font-semibold text-green-400">${revenue.toLocaleString()}</span>
                  <span className="text-xs text-green-400 ml-1">↑ 12%</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* Live Bookings Card */}
          <div className="glass-panel p-6">
            <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4">Recent Bookings</h3>
            <div className="space-y-2 max-h-[320px] overflow-y-auto">
              {bookings.map((booking, i) => (
                <div
                  key={i}
                  className="booking-item flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all group cursor-pointer"
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/30 to-secondary/30 flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-medium">
                      {booking.avatar}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className="font-medium text-sm">{booking.name}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{booking.guests} guests</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-sm">{booking.time}</p>
                    <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                      booking.status === 'confirmed' 
                        ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' 
                        : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'
                    }`}>
                      {booking.status}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* AI Automation Card */}
          <div className="glass-panel p-6">
            <h3 className="font-semibold mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-primary">🤖</span>
              AI Automation
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-4">
              {suggestions.map((suggestion, i) => (
                <div
                  key={suggestion.title}
                  className={`p-4 rounded-xl transition-all cursor-pointer
                    ${i === suggestionIndex 
                      ? 'bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20 shadow-lg shadow-primary/10' 
                      : 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10'
                    }`}
                >
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">{suggestion.title}</p>
                    {suggestion.risk && (
                      <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                        suggestion.risk > 40 ? 'bg-red-500/20 text-red-400' : 'bg-orange-500/20 text-orange-400'
                      }`}>
                        {suggestion.risk}% risk
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/60 mb-3">{suggestion.description}</p>
                  <button className="w-full py-2 bg-primary/20 text-primary text-sm rounded-lg hover:bg-primary/30 transition-all">
                    {suggestion.action}
                  </button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Additional metrics row */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4 mt-6">
          <div className="glass-panel p-4 text-center">
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">94%</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Table utilization</p>
          </div>
          <div className="glass-panel p-4 text-center">
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">28min</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Avg turn time</p>
          </div>
          <div className="glass-panel p-4 text-center">
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">$89</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Avg cover</p>
          </div>

            <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">4.8★</p>

          </div>
        </div>

/* Floating particles animation */
@keyframes float-particle {
  0%, 100% {
    transform: translateY(0px) translateX(0px);
  }
  50% {
    transform: translateY(-20px) translateX(10px);
  }
}

.float-particle {
  animation: float-particle 8s ease-in-out infinite;
}

/* Continuous shimmer for loading states */
@keyframes continuous-shimmer {
  0% {
    background-position: -200% 0;
  }
  100% {
    background-position: 200% 0;
  }
}

.shimmer {
  background: linear-gradient(90deg, transparent, rgba(255,255,255,0.1), transparent);
  background-size: 200% 100%;
  animation: continuous-shimmer 2s infinite;
}

/* Gradient border animation */
@keyframes border-flow {
  0%, 100% {
    border-image-source: linear-gradient(90deg, #a3a6ff, #ff6daf);
  }
  50% {
    border-image-source: linear-gradient(270deg, #a3a6ff, #ff6daf);
  }
}

.gradient-border {
  border: 2px solid;
  border-image-slice: 1;
  animation: border-flow 3s ease infinite;
}

/* Breathing glow */
@keyframes breathe {
  0%, 100% {
    opacity: 0.2;
    transform: scale(1);
  }
  50% {
    opacity: 0.4;
    transform: scale(1.05);
  }
}

.breathing-glow {
  animation: breathe 4s ease-in-out infinite;
}

/* Text gradient animation (already defined but enhanced) */
@keyframes gradient-shift {
  0% {
    background-position: 0% 50%;
  }
  50% {
    background-position: 100% 50%;
  }
  100% {
    background-position: 0% 50%;
  }
}

.gradient-text {
  background-size: 200% auto;
  animation: gradient-shift 6s ease infinite;
}

tsx
// components/landing/Hero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export function Hero() {
  const [metric, setMetric] = useState(1.61)
  const cardsRef = useRef<(HTMLDivElement | null)[]>([])

  useEffect(() => {
    // Continuous metric update
    const metricInterval = setInterval(() => {
      setMetric(prev => {
        const newVal = prev + 0.0003
        return newVal > 1.89 ? 1.61 : newVal
      })
    }, 80)

    // Floating card animation
    gsap.to('.float-card', {
      y: "random(-15, 15)",
      duration: "random(3, 5)",
      repeat: -1,
      yoyo: true,
      stagger: 0.2,
      ease: "sine.inOut"
    })

    return () => clearInterval(metricInterval)
  }, [])

  return (
    <section className="relative h-screen overflow-hidden">
      {/* LAYER 1: Deep background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-br from-[#0a0a0b] via-[#0e0e0f] to-[#121213]" />
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_top,rgba(163,166,255,0.08),transparent_60%)]" />
      </div>

      {/* LAYER 2: Floating orbs - fills empty corners */}
      <div className="absolute w-[600px] h-[600px] bg-primary/20 rounded-full blur-[120px] top-[-200px] left-[-200px] animate-pulse-slow" />
      <div className="absolute w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-tertiary/20 rounded-full blur-[100px] bottom-[-150px] right-[-150px] animate-pulse-slow" />
      <div className="absolute w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-secondary/15 rounded-full blur-[80px] top-1/2 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2" />
      
      {/* Grid overlay for texture */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_1px_1px,rgba(255,255,255,0.02)_1px,transparent_0)] bg-[size:40px_40px]" />
      
      {/* Watermark text - fills empty spaces */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-10 right-10 text-[120px] font-black opacity-[0.015] whitespace-nowrap rotate-12 pointer-events-none">
        SUFI OS
      </div>
      <div className="absolute top-20 left-[-80px] text-[180px] font-black opacity-[0.01] -rotate-12 pointer-events-none">
        INTELLIGENCE
      </div>

      {/* LEFT LABEL - fills top-left corner */}
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <div className="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
          <p className="text-xs tracking-wider">
            <span className="text-primary">●</span> SUFI / Intelligence Layer v2.0
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* RIGHT FLOATING CARDS - fills right side */}
      <div className="absolute right-12 top-1/3 -translate-y-1/2 z-20 space-y-4">
        {[1, 2, 3].map((_, i) => (
          <div
            key={i}
            ref={el => { cardsRef.current[i] = el }}
            className="float-card glass-panel w-56 p-4 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/[0.08] transition-all group"
          >
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/30 to-secondary/30 flex items-center justify-center">
                <span className="text-sm">{i === 0 ? '🍣' : i === 1 ? '🍝' : '🍛'}</span>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="font-medium text-sm">{i === 0 ? 'Sakura Hills' : i === 1 ? 'La Piazza' : 'Spice Route'}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{i === 0 ? 'Japanese' : i === 1 ? 'Italian' : 'Indian'}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-3 flex gap-1">
              {[...Array(5)].map((_, j) => (
                <div key={j} className="h-1 flex-1 bg-primary/30 rounded-full" />
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* CENTER - Main hero content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center">
        {/* Animated metric badge */}
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full inline-flex items-center gap-2">
            <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">SYSTEM ACTIVE</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono gradient-text">{metric.toFixed(3)}</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          Intelligence for
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text bg-[length:200%_auto] animate-gradient">real-world decisions</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl">
          SUFI OS is a living system that understands intent, predicts preferences,
          and evolves with every interaction.
        </p>

        {/* Input + CTA */}
        <div className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder="romantic dinner with wine..."
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                             bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                             font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                             transition-all duration-300">
              →
            </button>
          </div>
          <div className="flex justify-center gap-3 mt-3">
            <span className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 text-white/40 text-xs rounded-full">semantic search</span>
            <span className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 text-white/40 text-xs rounded-full">AI ranking</span>
            <span className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 text-white/40 text-xs rounded-full">real-time</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* BOTTOM - Scroll hint + logos - fills bottom */}
      <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-0 right-0 z-20">
        <div className="flex justify-center items-center gap-8 text-xs text-white/40">
          <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <span className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-primary/20 animate-bounce" />
            SCROLL
          </span>
          <div className="w-px h-4 bg-white/20" />
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            {['Michelin Guide', 'James Beard', 'Eater'].map(logo => (
              <span key={logo} className="opacity-40">{logo}</span>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
🔍 2️⃣ DISCOVERY — BENTO + SIDE CONTENT (NO EMPTY SPACE)
tsx
// components/landing/Discovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

const restaurants = [
  { name: 'Sakura Hills', cuisine: 'Japanese', rating: 4.8, trend: '+12%', match: 92, vibe: 'Romantic' },
  { name: 'La Piazza', cuisine: 'Italian', rating: 4.7, trend: '+8%', match: 88, vibe: 'Casual' },
  { name: 'Spice Route', cuisine: 'Indian', rating: 4.9, trend: '+15%', match: 96, vibe: 'Vibrant' },
  { name: 'The Grill', cuisine: 'Steakhouse', rating: 4.6, trend: '+5%', match: 82, vibe: 'Upscale' },
]

export function Discovery() {
  const [hoveredCard, setHoveredCard] = useState<number | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    // Drift animation for cards
    gsap.to('.bento-card', {
      y: "random(-8, 8)",
      duration: "random(2, 4)",
      repeat: -1,
      yoyo: true,
      stagger: 0.1,
      ease: "sine.inOut"
    })
  }, [])

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden -mt-20">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#0a0a0b] via-transparent to-transparent" />
      <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-primary/30 to-transparent" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating grid dots - fills empty space */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-10 bg-[radial-gradient(circle,rgba(255,255,255,0.1)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px]" />
      
      {/* Floating particles */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/4 right-0 w-96 h-96 bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-1/3 left-0 w-80 h-80 bg-tertiary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />

      {/* LAYER 3: Content - 12-col grid for density */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-8">
          
          {/* LEFT COLUMN - Text content (5 cols) */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-primary/10 text-primary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
              MULTI-SIGNAL RANKING
            </span>
            <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
              Search that <br />
              <span className="gradient-text">understands</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-lg text-white/60">
              Not just keywords. 6 signals combine to deliver the perfect match.
            </p>
            
            {/* Signal bars - fills left column */}
            <div className="mt-6 space-y-3">
              {['Quality', 'Engagement', 'Trending', 'Location', 'Personalization'].map((signal, i) => (
                <div key={signal} className="flex items-center gap-3">
                  <span className="text-xs text-white/40 w-24">{signal}</span>
                  <div className="flex-1 h-2 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                    <div 
                      className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full"
                      style={{ width: `${85 - i * 8}%` }}
                    />
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-xs text-white/40">{85 - i * 8}%</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">✨ "Because you liked wine-heavy menus"</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-1">Personalization active</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* RIGHT COLUMN - Bento grid (7 cols) */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              {/* Large featured card */}
              <div className="col-span-2 glass-panel p-5 relative overflow-hidden group cursor-pointer">
                <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/10 to-transparent opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" />
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                  <div>
                    <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                      🍣
                    </div>
                    <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">Sakura Hills</h3>
                    <p className="text-sm text-white/40">Japanese • $$$ • Romantic</p>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-yellow-400">★ 4.8</span>
                </div>
                <div className="mt-4">
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                    <span>Match score</span>
                    <span className="text-primary">92%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[92%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-green-400 mt-2">↑ Trending +12% this week</p>
              </div>
              
              {/* Small cards */}
              {restaurants.slice(1, 3).map((rest, i) => (
                <div
                  key={rest.name}
                  className="bento-card glass-panel p-4 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/[0.08] transition-all group"
                  onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredCard(i)}
