                >
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
                    <div>
                      <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-white/10 mb-2 flex items-center justify-center">
                        <span className="text-sm">{i === 0 ? '🍝' : '🍛'}</span>
                      </div>
                      <h4 className="font-semibold text-sm">{rest.name}</h4>
                      <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{rest.cuisine}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-3 flex gap-0.5">
                    {[...Array(5)].map((_, j) => (
                      <div 
                        key={j} 
                        className="h-1 flex-1 bg-primary/40 rounded-full" 
                        style={{ opacity: j < Math.floor(rest.match / 20) ? 1 : 0.3 }}
                      />
                    ))}
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-green-400 mt-2">{rest.trend}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
              
              {/* Bottom wide card */}
              <div className="col-span-2 glass-panel p-4 flex items-center justify-between">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">+ 1,247 restaurants near you</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Updated in real-time</p>
                </div>
                <button className="px-4 py-2 bg-white/10 rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-white/20 transition-all">
                  Explore all →
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
📅 3️⃣ RESERVATION — FULL WIDTH + OVERLAP
tsx
// components/landing/ReservationFlow.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'

const timeSlots = [
  { time: '6:00 PM', available: true, demand: 45 },
  { time: '6:30 PM', available: true, demand: 52 },
  { time: '7:00 PM', available: true, demand: 89, popular: true },
  { time: '7:30 PM', available: true, demand: 94, popular: true },
  { time: '8:00 PM', available: false, demand: 100 },
  { time: '8:30 PM', available: true, demand: 78 },
  { time: '9:00 PM', available: true, demand: 65 },
  { time: '9:30 PM', available: true, demand: 42 },
]

export function ReservationFlow() {
  const [selectedSlot, setSelectedSlot] = useState<number | null>(null)
  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false)

  const handleSelect = (index: number) => {
    if (!timeSlots[index].available) return
    gsap.to(`#slot-${index}`, { scale: 0.95, duration: 0.1, yoyo: true, repeat: 1 })
    setSelectedSlot(index)
  }

  const handleConfirm = () => {
    if (selectedSlot === null) return
    setConfirmed(true)
    setTimeout(() => setConfirmed(false), 2500)
  }

  return (
    <section className="relative -mt-32 pt-40 pb-32 overflow-hidden">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating glow - fills empty space */}
      <div className="absolute w-[700px] h-[700px] bg-primary/15 rounded-full blur-[120px] left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2" />
      <div className="absolute w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-tertiary/10 rounded-full blur-[100px] bottom-0 right-0" />
      <div className="absolute w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-secondary/10 rounded-full blur-[80px] top-20 left-0" />
      
      {/* Grid overlay */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(rgba(255,255,255,0.02)_1px,transparent_1px),linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.02)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:50px_50px]" />

      {/* LAYER 3: Content - centered with density */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-5xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="text-center">
          <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-tertiary/10 text-tertiary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
            ZERO FRICTION
          </span>
          <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4">
            Book in <span className="gradient-text">seconds</span>
          </h2>
          <p className="text-lg text-white/60 mt-2 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Real-time availability. Instant confirmation.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Restaurant card preview */}
        <div className="mt-12 glass-panel p-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-secondary/20 shimmer flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
              🍽️
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1">
              <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">Nobu Malibu</h3>
              <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">Japanese • $$$$</p>
              <div className="flex gap-1 mt-1">
                <span className="text-yellow-400">★★★★★</span>
                <span className="text-white/40 text-sm">(2.3k reviews)</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="text-right">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/40">Today</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-green-400">● Available</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Time slots grid - full width */}
        <div className="mt-8 grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
          {timeSlots.map((slot, i) => (
            <button
              key={slot.time}
              id={`slot-${i}`}
              onClick={() => handleSelect(i)}
              disabled={!slot.available}
              className={`relative py-3 rounded-xl font-medium transition-all text-sm
                ${selectedSlot === i 
                  ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20' 
                  : slot.available 
                    ? 'glass-panel hover:bg-white/10' 
                    : 'glass-panel text-white/30 cursor-not-allowed line-through'
                }`}
            >
              {slot.time}
              {slot.popular && slot.available && (
                <span className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 text-[9px] bg-tertiary text-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">
                  HOT
                </span>
              )}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Party size + confirm */}
        <div className="mt-8 max-w-md mx-auto">
          <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mb-6">
            {[2, 4, 6, 8].map(size => (
              <button key={size} className="px-5 py-2 glass-panel rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-white/10 transition-all">
                {size}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
          
          <button
            onClick={handleConfirm}
            disabled={selectedSlot === null}
            className="w-full py-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                     font-semibold hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 transition-all 
                     disabled:opacity-50 active:scale-95"
          >
            {confirmed ? '✓ Confirmed!' : 'Confirm Booking'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Success overlay */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {confirmed && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none z-50"
          >
            <div className="bg-black/95 backdrop-blur-xl rounded-2xl p-8 text-center border border-white/20">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                <svg className="w-8 h-8 text-green-500" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
                  <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
                </svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-xl font-semibold">Reservation Confirmed!</p>
              <p className="text-white/60 mt-2">Check your email for details</p>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ AI CONCIERGE — SIDE CHAT + BACKGROUND
tsx
// components/landing/AIConcierge.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { motion } from 'framer-motion'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
}

export function AIConcierge() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm your AI concierge. Tell me what you're craving." },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [streamingText, setStreamingText] = useState('')
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, streamingText])

  const streamResponse = (text: string) => {
    setStreamingText('')
    let i = 0
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (i < text.length) {
        setStreamingText(prev => prev + text[i])
        i++
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval)
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: text }])
        setStreamingText('')
        setIsTyping(false)
      }
    }, 25)
  }

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return

    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)

    setTimeout(() => {
      if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('sushi')) {
        streamResponse("I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks: Sushi Nakazawa (4.9★), Nobu (4.8★), and Sushi Yasuda (4.8★). Would you like me to book a table?")
      } else if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('romantic')) {
        streamResponse("Looking for a romantic dinner? These spots are perfect: One if by Land (4.9★), River Cafe (4.8★), and The Modern (4.8★). All have intimate ambiance and exceptional cuisine.")
      } else {
        streamResponse("I found several great options based on your request. Sakura Hills (Japanese, 4.8★), La Piazza (Italian, 4.7★), and Spice Route (Indian, 4.9★) are top-rated near you. Want me to show you more details?")
      }
    }, 1200)
  }

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0e0e0f] to-[#0a0a0b]">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_top,rgba(163,166,255,0.08),transparent_60%)]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements - fills empty space */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/3 left-0 w-96 h-96 bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[120px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-1/4 right-0 w-[500px] h-[500px] bg-tertiary/5 rounded-full blur-[100px]" />
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-1/4 w-64 h-64 bg-secondary/5 rounded-full blur-[80px]" />
      
      {/* Grid pattern */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.02)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:60px_60px]" />

      {/* LAYER 3: Content - 12-col grid with side chat */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-8 items-center">
          
          {/* LEFT COLUMN - Text content (5 cols) */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-primary/10 text-primary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
              AI CONCIERGE
            </span>
            <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4 mb-4">
              Just <span className="gradient-text">ask</span>
            </h2>
            <p className="text-lg text-white/60 mb-6">
              Natural language. Intelligent recommendations. Instant booking.
            </p>
            
            {/* Example queries - fills left column */}
            <div className="space-y-2">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mb-2">TRY THESE:</p>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {['romantic dinner', 'best sushi', 'vegan options', 'rooftop bar'].map(example => (
                  <button
                    key={example}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setInput(example)
                      setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                    }}
                    className="px-3 py-1.5 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                  >
                    {example}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
            
            {/* Learning indicator */}
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span className="text-sm">🧠</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">System learning</p>
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mt-1">
                    <span>Preference accuracy</span>
                    <span>94%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-1 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[94%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* RIGHT COLUMN - Chat interface (7 cols) */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="glass-panel overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-[450px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]">
                      <p className="text-sm">{streamingText}<span className="animate-pulse">▊</span></p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                
                {isTyping && !streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder="Ask me anything..."
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <button
                    onClick={handleSend}
                    disabled={isTyping}
                    className="px-6 py-3 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                             font-medium hover:shadow-lg transition-all disabled:opacity-50 active:scale-95"
                  >
                    Send
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
🧑‍🍳 5️⃣ OWNER SYSTEM — DASHBOARD + SIDE INFO
tsx
// components/landing/OwnerPreview.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export function OwnerPreview() {
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState([
    { name: 'Emma Watson', time: '7:00 PM', guests: 4, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'James Chen', time: '7:30 PM', guests: 2, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'Sofia Rodriguez', time: '8:00 PM', guests: 6, status: 'pending' },
  ])
  const [occupancy, setOccupancy] = useState(68)
  const [revenue, setRevenue] = useState(4280)

  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setBookings(prev => [{
        name: ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 2)],
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:00 PM`,
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        status: 'confirmed',
      }, ...prev.slice(0, 4)])
      setOccupancy(prev => Math.min(95, prev + Math.random() * 3))
      setRevenue(prev => prev + Math.floor(Math.random() * 120))
      
      gsap.to('.booking-item:first-child', {
        scale: 1.02,
        duration: 0.3,
        yoyo: true,
        repeat: 1,
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)',
      })
    }, 5000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [])

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden bg-gradient-to-b from-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(ellipse_at_bottom,rgba(163,166,255,0.05),transparent_70%)]" />
      <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full h-px bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-primary/30 to-transparent" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating elements */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 right-0 w-[600px] h-[600px] bg-secondary/5 rounded-full blur-[120px]" />
      <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-1/4 w-[400px] h-[400px] bg-primary/5 rounded-full blur-[80px]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div className="text-center mb-12">
          <span className="px-3 py-1 bg-secondary/10 text-secondary text-sm rounded-full inline-block">
            OWNER OS
          </span>
          <h2 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-bold mt-4">
            Control, not <span className="gradient-text">chaos</span>
          </h2>
          <p className="text-lg text-white/60 mt-2 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
            Real-time operations. AI automation. Complete visibility.
          </p>
        </div>
        
        <div className="grid grid-cols-12 gap-6">
          {/* DASHBOARD - Main area (8 cols) */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8">
            <div className="glass-panel p-6">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
                <h3 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                  Live Dashboard
                </h3>
                <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Updated in real-time</span>
              </div>
              
              {/* Metrics row */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6">
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">{Math.floor(occupancy)}%</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Occupancy</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">{bookings.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Active Bookings</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold gradient-text">${revenue.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Revenue Today</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              {/* Booking timeline preview */}
              <div className="mt-4">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-3">Recent Bookings</p>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {bookings.map((booking, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="booking-item flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all">
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">{booking.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{booking.guests} guests</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-sm">{booking.time}</p>
                        <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                          booking.status === 'confirmed' ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'
                        }`}>
                          {booking.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* SIDE INFO - AI Suggestions (4 cols) - fills right side */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
            <div className="glass-panel p-5">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
                <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                <h3 className="font-semibold">AI Automation</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="p-3 bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary mb-1">⚠️ No-Show Risk</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">High probability at 8 PM (42%)</p>
                  <button className="mt-2 w-full py-1.5 bg-primary/20 text-primary text-xs rounded-lg">Overbook by 10%</button>
                </div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-tertiary/10 border border-tertiary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-tertiary mb-1">📈 Demand Spike</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">Weekend evenings up 35% vs last week</p>
                  <button className="mt-2 w-full py-1.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary text-xs rounded-lg">Adjust pricing</button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div className="glass-panel p-5">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-3">Quick Stats</h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Table utilization</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">94%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg turn time</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">28min</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg cover</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">$89</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
💎 6️⃣ FINAL CTA — INTEGRATED (NOT EMPTY)
tsx
// components/landing/CTASection.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export function CTASection() {
  useEffect(() => {
    gsap.to('.cta-glow', {
      scale: 1.2,
      opacity: 0.8,
      duration: 3,
      repeat: -1,
      yoyo: true,
      ease: 'sine.inOut'
    })
  }, [])

  return (
    <section className="relative py-32 overflow-hidden">
      {/* LAYER 1: Background with animated glow */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-t from-[#0a0a0b] to-[#0e0e0f]" />
      <div className="cta-glow absolute w-[800px] h-[800px] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary/20 to-tertiary/20 rounded-full blur-[120px] left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2" />
      
      {/* LAYER 2: Floating particles */}
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_center,rgba(163,166,255,0.05),transparent_70%)]" />
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.02)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:60px_60px]" />
      
      {/* LAYER 3: Content - integrated, not empty */}
      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 text-center">
        {/* Trust indicators above CTA - fills space */}
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-8 mb-12">
          {['Michelin Guide', 'James Beard', 'Eater'].map(logo => (
            <div key={logo} className="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
              <span className="text-xs text-white/60">{logo}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        
        <h2 className="text-5xl md:text-6xl font-bold">
          Start using <span className="gradient-text">SUFI</span>
        </h2>
        <p className="text-xl text-white/60 mt-4 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          Join thousands of restaurants and diners using the intelligence layer for real-world decisions.
        </p>
        
        <div className="mt-8 flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 justify-center">
          <button className="px-8 py-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-2xl font-semibold text-lg hover:shadow-xl hover:shadow-primary/20 transition-all active:scale-95">
            SUFI AI — For Diners
          </button>
          <button className="px-8 py-4 glass-panel rounded-2xl font-semibold text-lg hover:bg-white/10 transition-all active:scale-95">
            SUFI OS — For Restaurants
          </button>
        </div>
        
        {/* Additional info - fills bottom */}
        <div className="mt-8 flex justify-center gap-6 text-xs text-white/40">
          <span>✓ No credit card required</span>
          <span>✓ 14-day free trial</span>
          <span>✓ Cancel anytime</span>

    </section>
  )
}

// components/layout/Container.tsx

  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  maxWidth?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl' | '2xl' | 'full'
}

const maxWidths = {
  sm: 'max-w-screen-sm',
  md: 'max-w-screen-md',
  lg: 'max-w-screen-lg',
  xl: 'max-w-screen-xl',
  '2xl': 'max-w-screen-2xl',
  full: 'max-w-full',
}

export default function Container({ children, className = '', maxWidth = 'xl' }: ContainerProps) {
  return (
    <div className={`relative z-10 mx-auto px-6 ${maxWidths[maxWidth]} ${className}`}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

        bg-white/[0.04] backdrop-blur-xl border border-white/[0.08] rounded-2xl
        ${paddingClasses[padding]}

      `}

    </div>

tsx
// components/ui/Button.tsx
'use client'

import { ReactNode, forwardRef } from 'react'
import Magnetic from '@/components/core/Magnetic'

interface ButtonProps {
  children: ReactNode
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline'
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
  className?: string
  onClick?: () => void
  disabled?: boolean
  magnetic?: boolean
}

const variantClasses = {
  primary: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20 hover:shadow-xl hover:shadow-primary/30',
  secondary: 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/20',
  outline: 'border border-white/20 text-white hover:bg-white/10',
}

const sizeClasses = {
  sm: 'px-4 py-2 text-sm',
  md: 'px-6 py-3 text-base',
  lg: 'px-8 py-4 text-lg',
}

export default forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(function Button(
  { children, variant = 'primary', size = 'md', className = '', onClick, disabled = false, magnetic = true },
  ref
) {
  const button = (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      onClick={onClick}
      disabled={disabled}
      className={`
        rounded-xl font-semibold transition-all duration-200
        active:scale-95 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
        ${variantClasses[variant]}
        ${sizeClasses[size]}
        ${className}
      `}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  )

  if (magnetic) {
    return <Magnetic>{button}</Magnetic>
  }

  return button
})

// components/ui/Heading.tsx
'use client'

import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface HeadingProps {
  title: string | ReactNode
  subtitle?: string | ReactNode
  align?: 'left' | 'center'
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
  className?: string
  gradient?: boolean
}

const sizeClasses = {
  sm: { title: 'text-2xl md:text-3xl', subtitle: 'text-base' },
  md: { title: 'text-3xl md:text-4xl', subtitle: 'text-lg' },
  lg: { title: 'text-4xl md:text-5xl', subtitle: 'text-xl' },
}

export default function Heading({
  title,
  subtitle,
  align = 'left',
  size = 'md',
  className = '',
  gradient = false,
}: HeadingProps) {
  return (
    <div className={`${align === 'center' ? 'text-center' : ''} ${className}`}>
      <h2
        className={`
          font-bold tracking-tight
          ${sizeClasses[size].title}
          ${gradient ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary bg-clip-text text-transparent' : ''}
        `}
      >
        {title}
      </h2>
      {subtitle && (
        <p className={`mt-4 text-white/60 ${sizeClasses[size].subtitle}`}>
          {subtitle}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

tsx
// components/core/MotionProvider.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger'

export default function MotionProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  useEffect(() => {
    gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger)

    gsap.defaults({
      ease: 'power3.out',
      duration: 0.6,
    })

    ScrollTrigger.defaults({
      scrub: 1.2,
      ease: 'power2.out',
    })
  }, [])

  return <>{children}</>
}
tsx
// components/core/Magnetic.tsx
'use client'

import { useRef, ReactNode } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function Magnetic({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  const handleMove = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!ref.current) return
    const rect = ref.current.getBoundingClientRect()
    const x = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2
    const y = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2

    gsap.to(ref.current, {
      x: x * 0.2,
      y: y * 0.2,
      duration: 0.3,
    })
  }

  const reset = () => {
    if (!ref.current) return
    gsap.to(ref.current, { x: 0, y: 0, duration: 0.3 })
  }

  return (
    <div ref={ref} onMouseMove={handleMove} onMouseLeave={reset}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}
tsx
// components/core/CursorSystem.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function CursorSystem() {
  const cursorRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  const cursorDotRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    const onMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, {
        x: e.clientX,
        y: e.clientY,
        duration: 0.2,
        ease: 'power2.out',
      })
      gsap.to(cursorDotRef.current, {
        x: e.clientX,
        y: e.clientY,
        duration: 0.05,
      })
    }

    const onHover = () => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 2.5, duration: 0.2 })
    }

    const onLeave = () => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 1, duration: 0.2 })
    }

    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)

    const interactiveElements = document.querySelectorAll('button, a, .interactive')
    interactiveElements.forEach(el => {
      el.addEventListener('mouseenter', onHover)
      el.addEventListener('mouseleave', onLeave)
    })

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)
      interactiveElements.forEach(el => {
        el.removeEventListener('mouseenter', onHover)
        el.removeEventListener('mouseleave', onLeave)
      })
    }
  }, [])

  return (
    <>
      <div
        ref={cursorRef}
        className="fixed w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary rounded-full pointer-events-none z-50 mix-blend-difference"
        style={{ left: -16, top: -16 }}
      />
      <div
        ref={cursorDotRef}
        className="fixed w-2 h-2 bg-primary rounded-full pointer-events-none z-50"
        style={{ left: -4, top: -4 }}
      />
    </>
  )
}
tsx
// components/core/BackgroundOrbs.tsx
'use client'

interface BackgroundOrbsProps {
  count?: number
  variant?: 'default' | 'gradient'
}

export default function BackgroundOrbs({ count = 3, variant = 'default' }: BackgroundOrbsProps) {
  const orbs = [
    { color: 'primary', size: 500, top: -100, left: -100, blur: 120 },
    { color: 'tertiary', size: 400, bottom: -100, right: -100, blur: 100 },
    { color: 'secondary', size: 300, top: '50%', left: '50%', blur: 80 },
  ].slice(0, count)

  return (
    <>
      {orbs.map((orb, i) => (
        <div
          key={i}
          className={`absolute rounded-full blur-3xl bg-${orb.color}/20`}
          style={{
            width: orb.size,
            height: orb.size,
            top: orb.top,
            left: orb.left,
            bottom: orb.bottom,
            right: orb.right,
            filter: `blur(${orb.blur}px)`,
            transform: orb.top === '50%' ? 'translate(-50%, -50%)' : undefined,
          }}
        />
      ))}
    </>
  )
}
tsx
// components/core/IntelligenceField.tsx
'use client'

import { Canvas, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber'
import { useRef, useMemo } from 'react'
import * as THREE from 'three'

function EnergyField() {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Points>(null)

  const particles = useMemo(() => {
    const positions = new Float32Array(1500 * 3)
    for (let i = 0; i < 1500; i++) {
      positions[i * 3] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20
      positions[i * 3 + 1] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15
      positions[i * 3 + 2] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 - 5
    }
    return positions
  }, [])

  useFrame((state) => {
    if (meshRef.current) {
      meshRef.current.rotation.y = state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.03
      meshRef.current.rotation.x = Math.sin(state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.02) * 0.1
    }
  })

  return (
    <points ref={meshRef}>
      <bufferGeometry>
        <bufferAttribute
          attach="attributes-position"
          count={1500}
          array={particles}
          itemSize={3}
        />
      </bufferGeometry>
      <pointsMaterial color="#a3a6ff" size={0.05} transparent opacity={0.3} />
    </points>
  )
}

export default function IntelligenceField() {
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 -z-20 pointer-events-none">
      <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0, 5] }}>
        <ambientLight intensity={0.5} />
        <EnergyField />
      </Canvas>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-transparent via-background/50 to-background pointer-events-none" />
    </div>
  )
}

// components/landing/Hero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

const queries = ['romantic dinner with wine', 'rooftop sushi near me', 'quiet italian restaurant']

export default function Hero() {
  const [currentQuery, setCurrentQuery] = useState(queries[0])
  const [metric, setMetric] = useState(1.61)
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    const metricInterval = setInterval(() => {
      setMetric(prev => (prev > 1.89 ? 1.61 : prev + 0.0003))
    }, 80)

    let queryIndex = 0
    const queryInterval = setInterval(() => {
      queryIndex = (queryIndex + 1) % queries.length
      const tl = gsap.timeline()
      tl.to('.hero-query', { opacity: 0, y: 10, duration: 0.2 })
      tl.call(() => setCurrentQuery(queries[queryIndex]))
      tl.to('.hero-query', { opacity: 1, y: 0, duration: 0.3 })
    }, 5000)

    return () => {
      clearInterval(metricInterval)
      clearInterval(queryInterval)
    }
  }, [])

  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <BackgroundOrbs count={2} />

      {/* Left label */}
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md">SUFI / Intelligence Layer v2.0</Badge>
      </div>

      {/* Right cards */}
      <div className="absolute right-12 top-1/3 -translate-y-1/2 z-20 space-y-4">
        {['Sakura Hills', 'La Piazza', 'Spice Route'].map((name, i) => (
          <GlassPanel key={name} hover padding="sm" className="w-56">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/30 to-secondary/30 flex items-center justify-center">
                <span>{i === 0 ? '🍣' : i === 1 ? '🍝' : '🍛'}</span>
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="font-medium text-sm">{name}</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{i === 0 ? 'Japanese' : i === 1 ? 'Italian' : 'Indian'}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </GlassPanel>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Main content */}
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">SYSTEM ACTIVE</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{metric.toFixed(3)}</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          Intelligence for
          <br />
          <span className="bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary bg-clip-text text-transparent">
            real-world decisions
          </span>
        </h1>

        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          SUFI OS is a living system that understands intent, predicts preferences,
          and evolves with every interaction.
        </p>

        <div className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              ref={inputRef}
              type="text"
              placeholder={currentQuery}
              className="hero-query w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                             bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                             font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                             transition-all duration-300">
              →
            </button>
          </div>
          <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
            <Badge>semantic search</Badge>
            <Badge variant="secondary">AI ranking</Badge>
            <Badge variant="tertiary">real-time</Badge>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Bottom scroll hint */}
        <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-0 right-0 flex justify-center gap-4 text-xs text-white/40">
          <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <span className="w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-primary/20 animate-bounce" />
            SCROLL
          </span>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>

import { useState } from 'react'
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'

import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

const timeSlots = [
  { time: '6:00 PM', available: true, demand: 45 },
  { time: '6:30 PM', available: true, demand: 52 },
  { time: '7:00 PM', available: true, demand: 89, popular: true },
  { time: '7:30 PM', available: true, demand: 94, popular: true },
  { time: '8:00 PM', available: false, demand: 100 },
  { time: '8:30 PM', available: true, demand: 78 },
  { time: '9:00 PM', available: true, demand: 65 },
  { time: '9:30 PM', available: true, demand: 42 },
]

export default function Reservation() {
  const [selectedSlot, setSelectedSlot] = useState<number | null>(null)
  const [confirmed, setConfirmed] = useState(false)

  const handleConfirm = () => {
    if (selectedSlot === null) return
    setConfirmed(true)
    setTimeout(() => setConfirmed(false), 2500)
  }

  return (
    <Section className="-mt-32 pt-40 text-center">
      <BackgroundOrbs count={1} />

      <Container maxWidth="lg">
        <Badge variant="tertiary">ZERO FRICTION</Badge>

            <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary/20 to-secondary/20 shimmer flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
              🍽️
            </div>
            <div className="flex-1 text-left">
              <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">Nobu Malibu</h3>
              <p className="text-white/60 text-sm">Japanese • $$$$</p>
              <div className="flex gap-1 mt-1">
                <span className="text-yellow-400">★★★★★</span>
                <span className="text-white/40 text-sm">(2.3k reviews)</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="text-right">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/40">Today</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-green-400">● Available</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </GlassPanel>

        {/* Time slots */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3 mt-8 max-w-3xl mx-auto">
          {timeSlots.map((slot, i) => (
            <button
              key={slot.time}
              onClick={() => slot.available && setSelectedSlot(i)}
              disabled={!slot.available}
              className={`
                relative py-3 rounded-xl font-medium transition-all text-sm
                ${selectedSlot === i
                  ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20'
                  : slot.available
                    ? 'glass-panel hover:bg-white/10'
                    : 'glass-panel text-white/30 cursor-not-allowed line-through'
                }
              `}
            >
              {slot.time}
              {slot.popular && slot.available && (
                <span className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 text-[9px] bg-tertiary text-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">
                  HOT
                </span>
              )}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Confirm button */}
        <div className="mt-8 max-w-md mx-auto">
          <Button
            onClick={handleConfirm}
            disabled={selectedSlot === null}
            size="lg"
            className="w-full"
          >

            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none z-50"
          >
            <div className="bg-black/95 backdrop-blur-xl rounded-2xl p-8 text-center border border-white/20">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                <svg className="w-8 h-8 text-green-500" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
                  <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
                </svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-xl font-semibold">Reservation Confirmed!</p>
              <p className="text-white/60 mt-2">Check your email for details</p>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </Section>
  )
}

// components/landing/AI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
}

export default function AI() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm your AI concierge. Tell me what you're craving." },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [streamingText, setStreamingText] = useState('')
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, streamingText])

  const streamResponse = (text: string) => {
    setStreamingText('')
    let i = 0
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (i < text.length) {
        setStreamingText(prev => prev + text[i])
        i++
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval)
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: text }])
        setStreamingText('')
        setIsTyping(false)
      }
    }, 25)
  }

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return

    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)

    setTimeout(() => {
      if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('sushi')) {
        streamResponse("I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks: Sushi Nakazawa (4.9★), Nobu (4.8★), and Sushi Yasuda (4.8★). Would you like me to book a table?")
      } else if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('romantic')) {
        streamResponse("Looking for a romantic dinner? These spots are perfect: One if by Land (4.9★), River Cafe (4.8★), and The Modern (4.8★). All have intimate ambiance and exceptional cuisine.")
      } else {
        streamResponse("I found several great options based on your request. Sakura Hills (Japanese, 4.8★), La Piazza (Italian, 4.7★), and Spice Route (Indian, 4.9★) are top-rated near you. Want me to show you more details?")
      }
    }, 1200)
  }

  return (
    <Section>
      <BackgroundOrbs count={2} />

      <Container>
        <Grid>
          {/* Left column - Chat */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-[450px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}

                {streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]">
                      <p className="text-sm">{streamingText}<span className="animate-pulse">▊</span></p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}

                {isTyping && !streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>

              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder="Ask me anything..."
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>

          {/* Right column - Text content */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">AI CONCIERGE</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Just ask"
              subtitle="Natural language. Intelligent recommendations. Instant booking."
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />

            <div className="mt-6 space-y-2">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mb-2">TRY THESE:</p>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {['romantic dinner', 'best sushi', 'vegan options', 'rooftop bar'].map(example => (
                  <button
                    key={example}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setInput(example)
                      setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                    }}
                    className="px-3 py-1.5 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                  >
                    {example}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span>🧠</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">System learning</p>
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mt-1">
                    <span>Preference accuracy</span>
                    <span>94%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-1 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[94%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
tsx
// components/landing/Owner.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

interface Booking {
  name: string
  time: string
  guests: number
  status: 'confirmed' | 'pending'
}

export default function Owner() {
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState<Booking[]>([
    { name: 'Emma Watson', time: '7:00 PM', guests: 4, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'James Chen', time: '7:30 PM', guests: 2, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'Sofia Rodriguez', time: '8:00 PM', guests: 6, status: 'pending' },
  ])
  const [occupancy, setOccupancy] = useState(68)
  const [revenue, setRevenue] = useState(4280)

  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      setBookings(prev => [{
        name: ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 2)],
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:00 PM`,
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        status: 'confirmed',
      }, ...prev.slice(0, 4)])
      setOccupancy(prev => Math.min(95, prev + Math.random() * 3))
      setRevenue(prev => prev + Math.floor(Math.random() * 120))

      gsap.to('.booking-item:first-child', {
        scale: 1.02,
        duration: 0.3,
        yoyo: true,
        repeat: 1,
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)',
      })
    }, 5000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [])

  return (
    <Section>
      <BackgroundOrbs count={2} />

      <Container>
        <div className="text-center mb-12">
          <Badge variant="secondary">OWNER OS</Badge>
          <Heading
            title="Control, not chaos"
            subtitle="Real-time operations. AI automation. Complete visibility."
            align="center"
            size="lg"
            className="mt-4"
          />
        </div>

        <Grid>
          {/* Dashboard - Main area */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8">
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
                <h3 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                  Live Dashboard
                </h3>
                <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Updated in real-time</span>
              </div>

              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6">
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{Math.floor(occupancy)}%</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Occupancy</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{bookings.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Active Bookings</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">${revenue.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Revenue Today</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-3">Recent Bookings</p>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {bookings.map((booking, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="booking-item flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all">
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">{booking.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{booking.guests} guests</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-sm">{booking.time}</p>
                        <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                          booking.status === 'confirmed'
                            ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400'
                            : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'
                        }`}>
                          {booking.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>

          {/* Side info - AI Suggestions */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
                <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                <h3 className="font-semibold">AI Automation</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="p-3 bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary mb-1">⚠️ No-Show Risk</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">High probability at 8 PM (42%)</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Overbook by 10%
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-tertiary/10 border border-tertiary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-tertiary mb-1">📈 Demand Spike</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">Weekend evenings up 35% vs last week</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Adjust pricing
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>

            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-3">Quick Stats</h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Table utilization</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">94%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg turn time</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">28min</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg cover</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">$89</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}

      scale: 1.2,

  return (

// app/layout.tsx
'use client'

import { Lenis as ReactLenis } from '@studio-freight/react-lenis'
import MotionProvider from '@/components/core/MotionProvider'
import CursorSystem from '@/components/core/CursorSystem'
import IntelligenceField from '@/components/core/IntelligenceField'
import '@/styles/globals.css'

export default function RootLayout({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <html lang="en">
      <body>
        <ReactLenis root options={{ lerp: 0.08, wheelMultiplier: 0.8 }}>
          <MotionProvider>
            <CursorSystem />
            <IntelligenceField />
            {children}
          </MotionProvider>
        </ReactLenis>
      </body>
    </html>
  )
}

  { name: 'Pro', price: '$29', features: ['AI concierge', 'Unlimited bookings', 'Priority support', 'Analytics'] },

                <h3 className="text-2xl font-bold">{plan.name}</h3>

/* styles/globals.css */
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:opsz,wght@14..32,400;14..32,500;14..32,600;14..32,700&display=swap');

@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

@layer base {
  * {
    @apply border-white/10;
  }

  body {
    @apply bg-[#0e0e0f] text-white font-sans antialiased;
    font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif;
  }

  ::selection {
    @apply bg-primary/30;
  }
}

@layer components {
  .glass-panel {
    @apply bg-white/[0.04] backdrop-blur-xl border border-white/[0.08] rounded-2xl;
  }

  .gradient-text {
    @apply bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary bg-clip-text text-transparent bg-[length:200%_auto];
    animation: gradient-shift 6s ease infinite;
  }
}

@layer utilities {
  .shimmer {
    background: linear-gradient(90deg, transparent, rgba(255,255,255,0.1), transparent);
    background-size: 200% 100%;
    animation: shimmer 2s infinite;
  }
}

@keyframes shimmer {
  0% { background-position: -200% 0; }
  100% { background-position: 200% 0; }
}

@keyframes gradient-shift {
  0%, 100% { background-position: 0% center; }
  50% { background-position: 100% center; }
}

@keyframes float {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0px) translateX(0px); }
  50% { transform: translateY(-20px) translateX(10px); }
}

.float {
  animation: float 8s ease-in-out infinite;
}

🎯 WHAT YOU NOW HAVE
Component	Description	Reusable
Section	Base section with padding	✅
Container	Max-width container	✅
Grid	12-col grid system	✅
GlassPanel	Glass morphism card	✅
Button	Magnetic buttons with variants	✅
Heading	Title + subtitle	✅
Badge	Status/pill component	✅
Card	Extended glass panel	✅
BackgroundOrbs	Floating background elements	✅
IntelligenceField	Three.js particle field	✅
CursorSystem	Custom cursor	✅
Magnetic	Magnetic hover effect	✅
🔥 This is a production-grade, modular, scalable component system — exactly how Stripe, Vercel, and Linear structure their codebases. No empty spaces, no duplicated code, fully reusable.

      <div class="relative z-10 max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6">
        <div class="flex justify-center gap-8 mb-12">
          <div class="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full"><span class="text-xs text-white/60">Michelin Guide</span></div>
          <div class="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full"><span class="text-xs text-white/60">James Beard</span></div>
          <div class="glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full"><span class="text-xs text-white/60">Eater</span></div>
        </div>
        
        <h2 class="text-5xl md:text-6xl font-bold">Start using <span class="gradient-text">SUFI</span></h2>
        <p class="text-xl text-white/60 mt-4 max-w-2xl mx-auto">Join thousands of restaurants and diners using the intelligence layer for real-world decisions.</p>
        
        <div class="mt-8 flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-4 justify-center">
          <button class="px-8 py-4 bg-gradient-to-r from-[#a3a6ff] to-[#ff6daf] text-black rounded-2xl font-semibold text-lg hover:shadow-xl hover:shadow-[#a3a6ff]/20 transition-all active:scale-95">SUFI AI — For Diners</button>
          <button class="px-8 py-4 glass-panel rounded-2xl font-semibold text-lg hover:bg-white/10 transition-all active:scale-95">SUFI OS — For Restaurants</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="mt-8 flex justify-center gap-6 text-xs text-white/40">
          <span>✓ No credit card required</span>
          <span>✓ 14-day free trial</span>
          <span>✓ Cancel anytime</span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  </main>

  <script>
    // GSAP Animations
    gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger);
    
    // Animate sections on scroll
    gsap.utils.toArray('section').forEach(section => {
      gsap.from(section, {
        scrollTrigger: {
          trigger: section,
          start: 'top 80%',
          end: 'top 20%',
          scrub: 0.5,
        },
        opacity: 0,
        y: 50,
        duration: 0.8,
      });
    });
    
    // Hero metric animation
    let metric = 1.61;
    const metricEl = document.getElementById('metric');
    setInterval(() => {
      metric += 0.0003;
      if (metric > 1.89) metric = 1.61;
      if (metricEl) metricEl.textContent = metric.toFixed(3);
    }, 80);
    
    // Animate signal bars
    const signalBars = document.querySelectorAll('.signal-bar');
    setInterval(() => {
      signalBars.forEach(bar => {
        const newWidth = Math.random() * 60 + 40;
        bar.style.width = `${newWidth}%`;
      });
    }, 3000);
    
    // Reservation system
    let selectedSlot = null;
    const timeSlots = document.querySelectorAll('.time-slot');
    const confirmBtn = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');
    
    timeSlots.forEach((slot, index) => {
      if (!slot.classList.contains('cursor-not-allowed')) {
        slot.addEventListener('click', () => {
          timeSlots.forEach(s => s.classList.remove('bg-gradient-to-r', 'from-[#a3a6ff]', 'to-[#ff6daf]', 'text-black'));
          slot.classList.add('bg-gradient-to-r', 'from-[#a3a6ff]', 'to-[#ff6daf]', 'text-black');
          selectedSlot = slot.dataset.time;
          confirmBtn.disabled = false;
          confirmBtn.textContent = `Book for ${selectedSlot}`;
        });
      }
    });
    
    confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (!selectedSlot) return;
      confirmBtn.textContent = '✓ Confirmed!';
      setTimeout(() => {
        confirmBtn.textContent = 'Confirm Booking';
        timeSlots.forEach(s => s.classList.remove('bg-gradient-to-r', 'from-[#a3a6ff]', 'to-[#ff6daf]', 'text-black'));
        selectedSlot = null;
        confirmBtn.disabled = true;
      }, 2000);
    });
    
    // Party size selection
    const partyBtns = document.querySelectorAll('.party-size');
    partyBtns.forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        partyBtns.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('bg-gradient-to-r', 'from-[#a3a6ff]', 'to-[#ff6daf]', 'text-black'));
        btn.classList.add('bg-gradient-to-r', 'from-[#a3a6ff]', 'to-[#ff6daf]', 'text-black');
      });
    });
    
    // AI Chat
    const chatMessages = document.getElementById('chatMessages');
    const chatInput = document.getElementById('chatInput');
    const sendBtn = document.getElementById('sendBtn');
    
    function addMessage(type, content) {
      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = `flex ${type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`;
      div.innerHTML = `<div class="${type === 'user' ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-[#a3a6ff] to-[#ff6daf] text-black' : 'bg-white/5 text-white'} p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]"><p class="text-sm">${content}</p></div>`;
      chatMessages.appendChild(div);
      chatMessages.scrollTop = chatMessages.scrollHeight;
    }
    
    function streamResponse(text) {
      let i = 0;
      const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
      tempDiv.className = 'flex justify-start';
      tempDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]"><p class="text-sm typing-text"></p><span class="animate-pulse">▊</span></div>';
      chatMessages.appendChild(tempDiv);
      const typingText = tempDiv.querySelector('.typing-text');
      
      const interval = setInterval(() => {
        if (i < text.length) {
          typingText.textContent += text[i];
          i++;
          chatMessages.scrollTop = chatMessages.scrollHeight;
        } else {
          clearInterval(interval);
          tempDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]"><p class="text-sm">${text}</p></div>`;
        }
      }, 25);
    }
    
    function handleSend() {
      const message = chatInput.value.trim();
      if (!message) return;
      
      addMessage('user', message);
      chatInput.value = '';
      
      setTimeout(() => {
        let response = '';
        if (message.toLowerCase().includes('sushi')) {
          response = "I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks: Sushi Nakazawa (4.9★), Nobu (4.8★), and Sushi Yasuda (4.8★). Would you like me to book a table?";
        } else if (message.toLowerCase().includes('romantic')) {
          response = "Looking for a romantic dinner? These spots are perfect: One if by Land (4.9★), River Cafe (4.8★), and The Modern (4.8★). All have intimate ambiance and exceptional cuisine.";
        } else {
          response = "I found several great options based on your request. Sakura Hills (Japanese, 4.8★), La Piazza (Italian, 4.7★), and Spice Route (Indian, 4.9★) are top-rated near you. Want me to show you more details?";
        }
        streamResponse(response);
      }, 1000);
    }
    
    sendBtn.addEventListener('click', handleSend);
    chatInput.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Enter') handleSend();
    });
    
    document.querySelectorAll('.example-query').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        chatInput.value = btn.textContent;
        handleSend();
      });
    });
    
    // Owner dashboard live updates
    let bookingCount = 3;
    let occupancy = 68;
    let revenue = 4280;
    const bookingNames = ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim', 'Lisa Wong', 'Michael Chen', 'Emily Zhao'];
    
    setInterval(() => {
      bookingCount = Math.min(8, bookingCount + 1);
      occupancy = Math.min(95, occupancy + Math.random() * 3);
      revenue += Math.floor(Math.random() * 120);
      
      document.getElementById('bookingCount').textContent = bookingCount;
      document.getElementById('occupancy').textContent = Math.floor(occupancy) + '%';
      document.getElementById('revenue').textContent = '$' + revenue.toLocaleString();
      
      // Add new booking
      const newBooking = {
        name: bookingNames[Math.floor(Math.random() * bookingNames.length)],
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:${Math.random() > 0.5 ? '00' : '30'} PM`,
      };
      
      const bookingsList = document.getElementById('bookingsList');
      const newDiv = document.createElement('div');
      newDiv.className = 'flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all';
      newDiv.innerHTML = `
        <div><p class="font-medium text-sm">${newBooking.name}</p><p class="text-xs text-white/40">${newBooking.guests} guests</p></div>
        <div class="text-right"><p class="text-sm">${newBooking.time}</p><span class="text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 text-green-400">confirmed</span></div>
      `;
      bookingsList.insertBefore(newDiv, bookingsList.firstChild);
      if (bookingsList.children.length > 5) bookingsList.removeChild(bookingsList.lastChild);
      
      // Animation
      gsap.to(newDiv, { scale: 1.02, duration: 0.2, yoyo: true, repeat: 1, backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)' });
    }, 8000);
    
    // Custom cursor (desktop only)
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
      const cursor = document.getElementById('cursor');
      const cursorDot = document.getElementById('cursorDot');
      
      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
        gsap.to(cursor, { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY, duration: 0.2 });
        gsap.to(cursorDot, { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY, duration: 0.05 });
      });
      
      document.querySelectorAll('button, a, .glass-panel-hover').forEach(el => {
        el.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => gsap.to(cursor, { scale: 2.5, duration: 0.2 }));
        el.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => gsap.to(cursor, { scale: 1, duration: 0.2 }));
      });
    } else {
      cursor.style.display = 'none';
      cursorDot.style.display = 'none';
    }
    
    // Floating card animations
    gsap.to('.float-card', {
      y: 'random(-15,15)',
      duration: 'random(3,5)',
      repeat: -1,
      yoyo: true,
      stagger: 0.2,
      ease: 'sine.inOut'
    });
    
    // Hero search placeholder rotation
    const queries = ['romantic dinner with wine', 'rooftop sushi near me', 'quiet italian restaurant', 'business lunch in CBD'];
    let queryIndex = 0;
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
    setInterval(() => {
      queryIndex = (queryIndex + 1) % queries.length;
      gsap.to(searchInput, { opacity: 0, duration: 0.2, onComplete: () => {
        searchInput.placeholder = queries[queryIndex];
        gsap.to(searchInput, { opacity: 1, duration: 0.3 });
      }});
    }, 5000);
  </script>
</body>
</html>

// components/layout/Section.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface SectionProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  id?: string
}

export default function Section({ children, className = '', id }: SectionProps) {
  return (
    <section
      id={id}
      className={`relative py-32 overflow-hidden ${className}`}
    >
      {children}
    </section>
  )
}
tsx
// components/layout/Container.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface ContainerProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  maxWidth?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl' | '2xl' | 'full'
}

const maxWidths = {
  sm: 'max-w-screen-sm',
  md: 'max-w-screen-md',
  lg: 'max-w-screen-lg',
  xl: 'max-w-screen-xl',
  '2xl': 'max-w-screen-2xl',
  full: 'max-w-full',
}

export default function Container({ 
  children, 
  className = '', 
  maxWidth = 'xl' 
}: ContainerProps) {
  return (
    <div className={`relative z-10 mx-auto px-6 ${maxWidths[maxWidth]} ${className}`}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}
tsx
// components/layout/Grid.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface GridProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  cols?: 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 6 | 12
  gap?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
}

const colClasses = {
  1: 'grid-cols-1',
  2: 'grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2',
  3: 'grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3',
  4: 'grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-4',
  6: 'grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-6',
  12: 'grid-cols-12',
}

const gapClasses = {
  sm: 'gap-4',
  md: 'gap-6',
  lg: 'gap-8',
}

export default function Grid({ 
  children, 
  className = '', 
  cols = 12, 
  gap = 'md' 
}: GridProps) {
  return (
    <div className={`grid ${colClasses[cols]} ${gapClasses[gap]} ${className}`}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}
🎨 2️⃣ UI COMPONENTS (REUSABLE)
tsx
// components/ui/GlassPanel.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface GlassPanelProps {
  children: ReactNode
  className?: string
  hover?: boolean
  padding?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'none'
}

const paddingClasses = {
  sm: 'p-4',
  md: 'p-6',
  lg: 'p-8',
  none: '',
}

export default function GlassPanel({ 
  children, 
  className = '', 
  hover = false, 
  padding = 'md' 
}: GlassPanelProps) {
  return (
    <div
      className={`
        bg-white/[0.04] backdrop-blur-xl border border-white/[0.08] rounded-2xl
        ${paddingClasses[padding]}
        ${hover ? 'hover:bg-white/[0.08] hover:-translate-y-0.5 transition-all duration-300' : ''}
        ${className}
      `}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}
tsx
// components/ui/Button.tsx
import { ReactNode, forwardRef } from 'react'
import Magnetic from '@/components/core/Magnetic'

interface ButtonProps {
  children: ReactNode
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline'
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
  className?: string
  onClick?: () => void
  disabled?: boolean
  magnetic?: boolean
  type?: 'button' | 'submit' | 'reset'
}

const variantClasses = {
  primary: 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20 hover:shadow-xl hover:shadow-primary/30',
  secondary: 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/20',
  outline: 'border border-white/20 text-white hover:bg-white/10',
}

const sizeClasses = {
  sm: 'px-4 py-2 text-sm',
  md: 'px-6 py-3 text-base',
  lg: 'px-8 py-4 text-lg',
}

export default forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(function Button(
  { 
    children, 
    variant = 'primary', 
    size = 'md', 
    className = '', 
    onClick, 
    disabled = false, 
    magnetic = true,
    type = 'button'
  },
  ref
) {
  const button = (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      type={type}
      onClick={onClick}
      disabled={disabled}
      className={`
        rounded-xl font-semibold transition-all duration-200
        active:scale-95 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed
        ${variantClasses[variant]}
        ${sizeClasses[size]}
        ${className}
      `}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  )

  if (magnetic) {
    return <Magnetic>{button}</Magnetic>
  }

  return button
})
tsx
// components/ui/Heading.tsx
import { ReactNode } from 'react'

interface HeadingProps {
  title: string | ReactNode
  subtitle?: string | ReactNode
  align?: 'left' | 'center' | 'right'
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl'
  className?: string
  gradient?: boolean
}

const sizeClasses = {
  sm: { title: 'text-2xl md:text-3xl', subtitle: 'text-base' },
  md: { title: 'text-3xl md:text-4xl', subtitle: 'text-lg' },
  lg: { title: 'text-4xl md:text-5xl', subtitle: 'text-xl' },
  xl: { title: 'text-5xl md:text-6xl', subtitle: 'text-xl' },
}

const alignClasses = {
  left: 'text-left',
  center: 'text-center',
  right: 'text-right',
}

export default function Heading({
  title,
  subtitle,
  align = 'left',
  size = 'md',
  className = '',
  gradient = false,
}: HeadingProps) {
  return (
    <div className={`${alignClasses[align]} ${className}`}>
      <h2
        className={`
          font-bold tracking-tight
          ${sizeClasses[size].title}
          ${gradient ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary bg-clip-text text-transparent' : ''}
        `}
      >
        {title}
      </h2>
      {subtitle && (
        <p className={`mt-4 text-white/60 ${sizeClasses[size].subtitle}`}>
          {subtitle}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

  variant = 'primary', 
  size = 'sm',

}: BadgeProps) {
