// components/core/MotionProvider.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, ReactNode } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { ScrollTrigger } from 'gsap/ScrollTrigger'

export default function MotionProvider({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  useEffect(() => {
    gsap.registerPlugin(ScrollTrigger)

    gsap.defaults({
      ease: 'power3.out',
      duration: 0.6,
    })

    ScrollTrigger.defaults({
      scrub: 1.2,
      ease: 'power2.out',
    })
  }, [])

  return <>{children}</>
}
tsx
// components/core/Magnetic.tsx
'use client'

import { useRef, ReactNode } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function Magnetic({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  const handleMove = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!ref.current) return
    const rect = ref.current.getBoundingClientRect()
    const x = e.clientX - rect.left - rect.width / 2
    const y = e.clientY - rect.top - rect.height / 2

    gsap.to(ref.current, {
      x: x * 0.2,
      y: y * 0.2,
      duration: 0.3,
    })
  }

  const reset = () => {
    if (!ref.current) return
    gsap.to(ref.current, { x: 0, y: 0, duration: 0.3 })
  }

  return (
    <div ref={ref} onMouseMove={handleMove} onMouseLeave={reset}>
      {children}
    </div>
  )
}

// components/core/BackgroundOrbs.tsx
'use client'

interface BackgroundOrbsProps {
  count?: number
  variant?: 'default' | 'gradient'
}

export default function BackgroundOrbs({ count = 3, variant = 'default' }: BackgroundOrbsProps) {
  const orbs = [
    { color: 'primary', size: 500, top: -100, left: -100, blur: 120 },
    { color: 'tertiary', size: 400, bottom: -100, right: -100, blur: 100 },
    { color: 'secondary', size: 300, top: '50%', left: '50%', blur: 80, translate: true },
  ].slice(0, count)

  const colorMap = {
    primary: '#a3a6ff',
    tertiary: '#ff6daf',
    secondary: '#ac8aff',
  }

  return (
    <>
      {orbs.map((orb, i) => (
        <div
          key={i}
          className="absolute rounded-full animate-pulse-slow"
          style={{
            width: orb.size,
            height: orb.size,
            top: orb.top,
            left: orb.left,
            bottom: orb.bottom,
            right: orb.right,
            background: colorMap[orb.color as keyof typeof colorMap],
            opacity: 0.15,
            filter: `blur(${orb.blur}px)`,
            transform: orb.translate ? 'translate(-50%, -50%)' : undefined,
          }}
        />
      ))}
    </>
  )
}
tsx
// components/core/CursorSystem.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function CursorSystem() {
  const cursorRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  const cursorDotRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    const isMobile = window.innerWidth < 768
    if (isMobile) return

    const onMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, {
        x: e.clientX,
        y: e.clientY,
        duration: 0.2,
        ease: 'power2.out',
      })
      gsap.to(cursorDotRef.current, {
        x: e.clientX,
        y: e.clientY,
        duration: 0.05,
      })
    }

    const onHover = () => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 2.5, duration: 0.2 })
    }

    const onLeave = () => {
      gsap.to(cursorRef.current, { scale: 1, duration: 0.2 })
    }

    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)

    const interactiveElements = document.querySelectorAll('button, a, .interactive, [role="button"]')
    interactiveElements.forEach(el => {
      el.addEventListener('mouseenter', onHover)
      el.addEventListener('mouseleave', onLeave)
    })

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)
      interactiveElements.forEach(el => {
        el.removeEventListener('mouseenter', onHover)
        el.removeEventListener('mouseleave', onLeave)
      })
    }
  }, [])

  return (
    <>
      <div
        ref={cursorRef}
        className="fixed w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary rounded-full pointer-events-none z-50 mix-blend-difference hidden md:block"
        style={{ left: -16, top: -16 }}
      />
      <div
        ref={cursorDotRef}
        className="fixed w-2 h-2 bg-primary rounded-full pointer-events-none z-50 hidden md:block"
        style={{ left: -4, top: -4 }}
      />
    </>
  )
}

// components/core/IntelligenceField.tsx
'use client'

import { Canvas, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber'
import { useRef, useMemo } from 'react'
import * as THREE from 'three'

function EnergyField() {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Points>(null)

  const particles = useMemo(() => {
    const positions = new Float32Array(1500 * 3)
    for (let i = 0; i < 1500; i++) {
      positions[i * 3] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20
      positions[i * 3 + 1] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15
      positions[i * 3 + 2] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 - 5
    }
    return positions
  }, [])

  useFrame((state) => {
    if (meshRef.current) {
      meshRef.current.rotation.y = state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.03
      meshRef.current.rotation.x = Math.sin(state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.02) * 0.1
    }
  })

  return (
    <points ref={meshRef}>
      <bufferGeometry>
        <bufferAttribute
          attach="attributes-position"
          count={1500}
          array={particles}
          itemSize={3}
        />
      </bufferGeometry>
      <pointsMaterial color="#a3a6ff" size={0.05} transparent opacity={0.3} />
    </points>
  )
}

export default function IntelligenceField() {
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 -z-20 pointer-events-none">
      <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0, 5] }}>
        <ambientLight intensity={0.5} />
        <EnergyField />
      </Canvas>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-transparent via-background/50 to-background pointer-events-none" />
    </div>
  )
}

// components/core/DepthSystem.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function DepthSystem() {
  useEffect(() => {
    const onMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
      const x = e.clientX / window.innerWidth
      const y = e.clientY / window.innerHeight

      gsap.to('.layer-1', {
        x: (x - 0.5) * 10,
        y: (y - 0.5) * 10,
        duration: 1,
      })
      gsap.to('.layer-2', {
        x: (x - 0.5) * 20,
        y: (y - 0.5) * 20,
        duration: 1,
      })
    }

    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)
    return () => window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove)
  }, [])

  return null
}

            <button
              key={slot.time}
              onClick={() => slot.available && setSelectedSlot(i)}
              disabled={!slot.available}
              className={`
                relative py-3 rounded-xl font-medium transition-all text-sm
                ${selectedSlot === i
                  ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black shadow-lg shadow-primary/20'
                  : slot.available
                    ? 'glass-panel hover:bg-white/10'
                    : 'glass-panel text-white/30 cursor-not-allowed line-through'
                }
              `}
            >
              {slot.time}
              {slot.popular && slot.available && (
                <span className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 text-[9px] bg-tertiary text-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full font-bold">
                  HOT
                </span>
              )}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Party size */}
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-6">
          {[2, 4, 6, 8].map(size => (
            <button
              key={size}
              onClick={() => setPartySize(size)}
              className={`px-5 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition-all
                ${partySize === size
                  ? 'bg-white text-black'
                  : 'glass-panel hover:bg-white/10'
                }`}
            >
              {size}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Confirm button */}
        <div className="mt-8 max-w-md mx-auto">
          <Button
            onClick={handleConfirm}
            disabled={selectedSlot === null}
            size="lg"
            className="w-full"
          >
            {confirmed ? '✓ Confirmed!' : 'Confirm Booking'}
          </Button>
        </div>
      </Container>

      {/* Success overlay */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {confirmed && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.8 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none z-50"
          >
            <div className="bg-black/95 backdrop-blur-xl rounded-2xl p-8 text-center border border-white/20">
              <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-green-500/20 flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4">
                <svg className="w-8 h-8 text-green-500" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="currentColor">
                  <path strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" strokeWidth={2} d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" />
                </svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-xl font-semibold">Reservation Confirmed!</p>
              <p className="text-white/60 mt-2">Table for {partySize} at {selectedSlot !== null ? timeSlots[selectedSlot].time : ''}</p>
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </Section>
  )
}
tsx
// components/landing/AI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
}

export default function AI() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm your AI concierge. Tell me what you're craving." },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [streamingText, setStreamingText] = useState('')
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, streamingText])

  const streamResponse = (text: string) => {
    setStreamingText('')
    let i = 0
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (i < text.length) {
        setStreamingText(prev => prev + text[i])
        i++
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval)
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: text }])
        setStreamingText('')
        setIsTyping(false)
      }
    }, 25)
  }

  const handleSend = () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return

    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)

    setTimeout(() => {
      if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('sushi')) {
        streamResponse("I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks: Sushi Nakazawa (4.9★), Nobu (4.8★), and Sushi Yasuda (4.8★). Would you like me to book a table?")
      } else if (userInput.toLowerCase().includes('romantic')) {
        streamResponse("Looking for a romantic dinner? These spots are perfect: One if by Land (4.9★), River Cafe (4.8★), and The Modern (4.8★). All have intimate ambiance and exceptional cuisine.")
      } else {
        streamResponse("I found several great options based on your request. Sakura Hills (Japanese, 4.8★), La Piazza (Italian, 4.7★), and Spice Route (Indian, 4.9★) are top-rated near you. Want me to show you more details?")
      }
    }, 1200)
  }

  return (
    <Section>
      <BackgroundOrbs count={2} />

      <Container>
        <Grid>
          {/* Left column - Chat */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-[450px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}

                {streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]">
                      <p className="text-sm">{streamingText}<span className="animate-pulse">▊</span></p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}

                {isTyping && !streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>

              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder="Ask me anything..."
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>

          {/* Right column - Text content */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">AI CONCIERGE</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Just ask"
              subtitle="Natural language. Intelligent recommendations. Instant booking."
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />

            <div className="mt-6 space-y-2">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mb-2">TRY THESE:</p>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {['romantic dinner', 'best sushi', 'vegan options', 'rooftop bar'].map(example => (
                  <button
                    key={example}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setInput(example)
                      setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                    }}
                    className="px-3 py-1.5 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                  >
                    {example}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span>🧠</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">System learning</p>
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mt-1">
                    <span>Preference accuracy</span>
                    <span>94%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-1 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[94%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
tsx
// components/landing/Owner.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'
import BackgroundOrbs from '@/components/core/BackgroundOrbs'

interface Booking {
  name: string
  time: string
  guests: number
  status: 'confirmed' | 'pending'
}

export default function Owner() {
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState<Booking[]>([
    { name: 'Emma Watson', time: '7:00 PM', guests: 4, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'James Chen', time: '7:30 PM', guests: 2, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'Sofia Rodriguez', time: '8:00 PM', guests: 6, status: 'pending' },
  ])
  const [occupancy, setOccupancy] = useState(68)
  const [revenue, setRevenue] = useState(4280)

  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      const newBookings = [...bookings]
      const newBooking: Booking = {
        name: ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim', 'Lisa Wong'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:${Math.random() > 0.5 ? '00' : '30'} PM`,
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        status: 'confirmed',
      }
      setBookings(prev => [newBooking, ...prev.slice(0, 4)])
      setOccupancy(prev => Math.min(95, prev + Math.random() * 3))
      setRevenue(prev => prev + Math.floor(Math.random() * 120))

      gsap.to('.booking-item:first-child', {
        scale: 1.02,
        duration: 0.3,
        yoyo: true,
        repeat: 1,
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)',
      })
    }, 8000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [])

  return (
    <Section>
      <BackgroundOrbs count={2} />

      <Container>
        <div className="text-center mb-12">
          <Badge variant="secondary">OWNER OS</Badge>
          <Heading
            title="Control, not chaos"
            subtitle="Real-time operations. AI automation. Complete visibility."
            align="center"
            size="lg"
            className="mt-4"
          />
        </div>

        <Grid>
          {/* Dashboard - Main area */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8">
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
                <h3 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                  Live Dashboard
                </h3>
                <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Updated in real-time</span>
              </div>

              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6">
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{Math.floor(occupancy)}%</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Occupancy</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{bookings.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Active Bookings</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">${revenue.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Revenue Today</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-3">Recent Bookings</p>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {bookings.map((booking, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="booking-item flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all">
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">{booking.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{booking.guests} guests</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-sm">{booking.time}</p>
                        <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                          booking.status === 'confirmed'
                            ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400'
                            : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'
                        }`}>
                          {booking.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>

          {/* Side info - AI Suggestions */}
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
                <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                <h3 className="font-semibold">AI Automation</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="p-3 bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary mb-1">⚠️ No-Show Risk</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">High probability at 8 PM (42%)</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Overbook by 10%
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-tertiary/10 border border-tertiary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-tertiary mb-1">📈 Demand Spike</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">Weekend evenings up 35% vs last week</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Adjust pricing
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>

            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-3">Quick Stats</h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Table utilization</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">94%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg turn time</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">28min</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg cover</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">$89</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}

          </MotionProvider>

/* styles/globals.css */
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:opsz,wght@14..32,400;14..32,500;14..32,600;14..32,700;14..32,800&display=swap');

@tailwind base;
@tailwind components;
@tailwind utilities;

@layer base {
  * {
    @apply border-white/10;
  }

  body {
    @apply bg-[#0e0e0f] text-white font-sans antialiased;
    font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif;
  }

  ::selection {
    @apply bg-primary/30;
  }
}

@layer components {
  .glass-panel {
    @apply bg-white/[0.04] backdrop-blur-xl border border-white/[0.08] rounded-2xl;
  }

  .gradient-text {
    @apply bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary bg-clip-text text-transparent bg-[length:200%_auto];
    animation: gradient-shift 6s ease infinite;
  }
}

@layer utilities {
  .shimmer {
    background: linear-gradient(90deg, transparent, rgba(255,255,255,0.1), transparent);
    background-size: 200% 100%;
    animation: shimmer 2s infinite;
  }
  
  .animate-pulse-slow {
    animation: pulse-slow 4s ease-in-out infinite;
  }
  
  .animate-bounce-slow {
    animation: bounce 2s ease-in-out infinite;
  }
}

@keyframes shimmer {
  0% { background-position: -200% 0; }
  100% { background-position: 200% 0; }
}

@keyframes gradient-shift {
  0%, 100% { background-position: 0% center; }
  50% { background-position: 100% center; }
}

@keyframes pulse-slow {
  0%, 100% { opacity: 0.2; transform: scale(1); }
  50% { opacity: 0.4; transform: scale(1.05); }
}

@keyframes bounce {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }
  50% { transform: translateY(-8px); }
}
📦 7️⃣ TAILWIND CONFIG
javascript
// tailwind.config.js
/** @type {import('tailwindcss').Config} */
module.exports = {
  content: [
    './pages/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx,mdx}',
    './components/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx,mdx}',
    './app/**/*.{js,ts,jsx,tsx,mdx}',
  ],
  theme: {
    extend: {
      colors: {
        primary: '#a3a6ff',
        secondary: '#ac8aff',
        tertiary: '#ff6daf',
        background: '#0e0e0f',
      },
      fontFamily: {
        sans: ['Inter', 'sans-serif'],
      },
      animation: {
        'pulse-slow': 'pulse-slow 4s ease-in-out infinite',
        'gradient': 'gradient-shift 6s ease infinite',
      },
      keyframes: {
        'pulse-slow': {
          '0%, 100%': { opacity: '0.2', transform: 'scale(1)' },
          '50%': { opacity: '0.4', transform: 'scale(1.05)' },
        },
        'gradient-shift': {
          '0%, 100%': { backgroundPosition: '0% center' },
          '50%': { backgroundPosition: '100% center' },
        },
      },
    },
  },
  plugins: [],
}

🧠 1️⃣ WHAT “ADAPTIVE UI” REALLY MEANS

Not gimmicks like “dark mode”.

👉 Real adaptive UI =

User behavior → system learns → UI layout + content + emphasis changes
🔥 Example (SUFI):
User always searches “romantic places”
→ Hero changes tone
→ Discovery prioritizes ambiance
→ Colors shift slightly warmer
🏗️ 2️⃣ ADAPTIVE ENGINE ARCHITECTURE

import { useSufiStore } from "@/lib/state/sufiStore"

export function updateUserProfile(action) {
  const store = useSufiStore.getState()

  if (action.type === "SEARCH") {
    store.setIntent(action.payload)

    if (action.payload.includes("romantic")) {
      store.setMood("romantic")
    }
  }

  if (action.type === "BOOKING") {
    store.setActivity(1)
  }
}

🧠 1️⃣ ADAPTIVE ENGINE CORE
tsx
// lib/adaptive/adaptiveEngine.ts
import { useSufiStore } from "@/lib/state/sufiStore"

export type ActionType = 'SEARCH' | 'BOOKING' | 'CLICK' | 'VIEW' | 'CANCEL'

interface Action {
  type: ActionType
  payload: any
  timestamp: number
}

// Track user behavior patterns
export class AdaptiveEngine {
  private actionHistory: Action[] = []
  private preferences: Map<string, number> = new Map()

  constructor() {
    // Load saved preferences from localStorage
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem('sufi_preferences')
      if (saved) {
        this.preferences = new Map(JSON.parse(saved))
      }
    }
  }

  trackAction(action: Action) {
    this.actionHistory.push(action)
    
    // Update preferences based on action
    if (action.type === 'SEARCH') {
      const keyword = action.payload.toLowerCase()
      const currentCount = this.preferences.get(keyword) || 0
      this.preferences.set(keyword, currentCount + 1)
      
      // Detect mood from search patterns
      if (keyword.includes('romantic') || keyword.includes('date') || keyword.includes('cozy')) {
        useSufiStore.getState().setMood('romantic')
      } else if (keyword.includes('business') || keyword.includes('meeting') || keyword.includes('quick')) {
        useSufiStore.getState().setMood('fast')
      } else if (keyword.includes('luxury') || keyword.includes('fine dining') || keyword.includes('michelin')) {
        useSufiStore.getState().setMood('luxury')
      }
      
      useSufiStore.getState().setIntent(action.payload)
    }
    
    if (action.type === 'BOOKING') {
      useSufiStore.getState().setActivity(1)
      // Decay activity over time
      setTimeout(() => {
        useSufiStore.getState().setActivity(0.5)
      }, 30000)
    }
    
    if (action.type === 'CLICK') {
      // Track clicked categories
      const category = action.payload
      const currentCount = this.preferences.get(`category_${category}`) || 0
      this.preferences.set(`category_${category}`, currentCount + 1)
    }
    
    // Save preferences
    this.savePreferences()
  }
  
  getTopPreferences(limit: number = 3): string[] {
    const sorted = Array.from(this.preferences.entries())
      .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
      .slice(0, limit)
      .map(([key]) => key)
    return sorted.filter(k => !k.startsWith('category_'))
  }
  
  getFavoriteCategories(): string[] {
    const categories = Array.from(this.preferences.entries())
      .filter(([key]) => key.startsWith('category_'))
      .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
      .slice(0, 2)
      .map(([key]) => key.replace('category_', ''))
    return categories
  }
  
  private savePreferences() {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      localStorage.setItem('sufi_preferences', JSON.stringify(Array.from(this.preferences.entries())))
    }
  }
  
  getAdaptiveRanking(restaurants: any[]): any[] {
    const favoriteCategories = this.getFavoriteCategories()
    if (favoriteCategories.length === 0) return restaurants
    
    return [...restaurants].sort((a, b) => {
      const aMatch = favoriteCategories.some(cat => a.cuisine?.toLowerCase().includes(cat))
      const bMatch = favoriteCategories.some(cat => b.cuisine?.toLowerCase().includes(cat))
      if (aMatch && !bMatch) return -1
      if (!aMatch && bMatch) return 1
      return 0
    })
  }
}

export const adaptiveEngine = new AdaptiveEngine()
🧠 2️⃣ EXTENDED GLOBAL STATE
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware"

export type Mood = 'neutral' | 'romantic' | 'fast' | 'luxury'

interface SufiState {
  // Core state
  intent: string
  activity: number
  mood: Mood
  
  // User preferences
  preferredCuisines: string[]
  preferredVibes: string[]
  searchHistory: string[]
  bookingHistory: number
  
  // UI preferences
  uiDensity: 'compact' | 'comfortable' | 'relaxed'
  emphasisMode: 'discovery' | 'booking' | 'analytics'
  
  // Actions
  setIntent: (intent: string) => void
  setActivity: (level: number) => void
  setMood: (mood: Mood) => void
  addSearch: (query: string) => void
  addBooking: () => void
  addPreference: (type: 'cuisine' | 'vibe', value: string) => void
  resetPreferences: () => void
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      // Initial state
      intent: "romantic dinner",
      activity: 0.4,
      mood: "neutral",
      preferredCuisines: [],
      preferredVibes: [],
      searchHistory: [],
      bookingHistory: 0,
      uiDensity: "comfortable",
      emphasisMode: "discovery",
      
      // Actions
      setIntent: (intent) => set({ intent }),
      
      setActivity: (activity) => set({ activity }),
      
      setMood: (mood) => {
        set({ mood })
        // Auto-adjust UI density based on mood
        const { uiDensity } = get()
        if (mood === 'fast' && uiDensity !== 'compact') {
          set({ uiDensity: 'compact' })
        } else if (mood === 'luxury' && uiDensity !== 'relaxed') {
          set({ uiDensity: 'relaxed' })
        }
      },
      
      addSearch: (query) => {
        set((state) => ({
          searchHistory: [query, ...state.searchHistory].slice(0, 10)
        }))
      },
      
      addBooking: () => {
        set((state) => ({
          bookingHistory: state.bookingHistory + 1,
          activity: Math.min(1, state.activity + 0.1)
        }))
      },
      
      addPreference: (type, value) => {
        if (type === 'cuisine') {
          set((state) => ({
            preferredCuisines: [...new Set([...state.preferredCuisines, value])].slice(0, 5)
          }))
        } else {
          set((state) => ({
            preferredVibes: [...new Set([...state.preferredVibes, value])].slice(0, 5)
          }))
        }
      },
      
      resetPreferences: () => {
        set({
          preferredCuisines: [],
          preferredVibes: [],
          searchHistory: [],
          bookingHistory: 0,
          mood: 'neutral',
          uiDensity: 'comfortable'
        })
      }
    }),
    {
      name: 'sufi-user-preferences',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        preferredCuisines: state.preferredCuisines,
        preferredVibes: state.preferredVibes,
        searchHistory: state.searchHistory,
        bookingHistory: state.bookingHistory,
        mood: state.mood,
        uiDensity: state.uiDensity
      })
    }
  )
)
🎨 3️⃣ ADAPTIVE BACKGROUND SYSTEM
tsx
// components/core/AdaptiveBackground.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

const moodColors = {
  neutral: {
    primary: '#a3a6ff',
    secondary: '#ac8aff',
    tertiary: '#ff6daf',
    intensity: 0.15
  },
  romantic: {
    primary: '#ff6daf',
    secondary: '#ff9eb5',
    tertiary: '#ff4d8a',
    intensity: 0.25
  },
  fast: {
    primary: '#22c55e',
    secondary: '#4ade80',
    tertiary: '#16a34a',
    intensity: 0.2
  },
  luxury: {
    primary: '#a3a6ff',
    secondary: '#c4b5fd',
    tertiary: '#8b5cf6',
    intensity: 0.3
  }
}

export default function AdaptiveBackground() {
  const { mood, activity } = useSufiStore()
  const colors = moodColors[mood]
  const bgRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const tl = gsap.timeline()
    
    // Animate gradient based on mood
    tl.to(bgRef.current, {
      background: `radial-gradient(circle at 30% 40%, ${colors.primary} 0%, ${colors.secondary} 30%, transparent 70%)`,
      duration: 1,
      ease: 'power2.out'
    })
    
    // Pulse intensity based on activity
    gsap.to('.adaptive-glow', {
      opacity: colors.intensity * (0.5 + activity * 0.5),
      scale: 1 + activity * 0.3,
      duration: 1,
      repeat: -1,
      yoyo: true,
      ease: 'sine.inOut'
    })
  }, [mood, activity, colors])
  
  return (
    <>
      <div ref={bgRef} className="fixed inset-0 -z-10 transition-all duration-1000" />
      <div className="adaptive-glow fixed inset-0 -z-10 opacity-20 pointer-events-none" 
           style={{ background: `radial-gradient(circle at center, ${colors.primary} 0%, transparent 70%)` }} />
    </>
  )
}
🎬 4️⃣ ADAPTIVE HERO
tsx
// components/landing/AdaptiveHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { adaptiveEngine } from '@/lib/adaptive/adaptiveEngine'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'

export default function AdaptiveHero() {
  const { mood, activity, setMood, addSearch } = useSufiStore()
  const [personalizedQuery, setPersonalizedQuery] = useState('')
  
  // Personalized placeholder based on user history
  useEffect(() => {
    const topPrefs = adaptiveEngine.getTopPreferences(1)
    if (topPrefs.length > 0) {
      setPersonalizedQuery(topPrefs[0])
    } else {
      setPersonalizedQuery('romantic dinner with wine')
    }
  }, [])
  
  // Dynamic copy based on mood
  const heroCopy = {
    neutral: {
      title: "Find your next",
      highlight: "perfect meal",
      subtitle: "AI-powered discovery for every craving"
    },
    romantic: {
      title: "Create the",
      highlight: "perfect evening",
      subtitle: "Discover intimate spots for unforgettable moments"
    },
    fast: {
      title: "Quick. Smart.",
      highlight: "Instant booking",
      subtitle: "Find available tables near you in seconds"
    },
    luxury: {
      title: "Experience",
      highlight: "exceptional dining",
      subtitle: "Curated selections for discerning palates"
    }
  }
  
  const copy = heroCopy[mood]
  
  const handleSearch = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    const input = (e.currentTarget as any).querySelector('input')?.value
    if (input) {
      addSearch(input)
      adaptiveEngine.trackAction({ type: 'SEARCH', payload: input, timestamp: Date.now() })
      
      // Auto-detect mood from search
      if (input.toLowerCase().includes('romantic')) setMood('romantic')
      else if (input.toLowerCase().includes('quick')) setMood('fast')
      else if (input.toLowerCase().includes('luxury')) setMood('luxury')
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md">
          {mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic Mode' : 
           mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick Mode' : 
           mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury Mode' : '🧠 Adaptive Mode'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">SYSTEM ACTIVE</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{(activity * 1.5 + 0.5).toFixed(2)}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {copy.title}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">{copy.highlight}</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {copy.subtitle}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              type="text"
              placeholder={personalizedQuery}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button type="submit" className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                             bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                             font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                             transition-all duration-300">
              →
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {mood === 'romantic' ? 'romantic' : mood === 'fast' ? 'quick booking' : 'semantic search'}
          </Badge>
          <Badge variant={mood === 'fast' ? 'success' : 'secondary'}>
            {mood === 'fast' ? 'instant availability' : 'AI ranking'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
        
        {/* Personalized suggestions */}
        {adaptiveEngine.getFavoriteCategories().length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-8 flex justify-center gap-2">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Based on your taste:</span>
            {adaptiveEngine.getFavoriteCategories().map(cat => (
              <Badge key={cat} variant="tertiary" size="sm">
                {cat}
              </Badge>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 5️⃣ ADAPTIVE DISCOVERY
tsx
// components/landing/AdaptiveDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { adaptiveEngine } from '@/lib/adaptive/adaptiveEngine'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

const allRestaurants = [
  { name: 'Sakura Hills', cuisine: 'Japanese', rating: 4.8, vibe: 'Romantic', ambiance: 9, availability: 'busy', price: '$$$', signal: 92 },
  { name: 'La Piazza', cuisine: 'Italian', rating: 4.7, vibe: 'Casual', ambiance: 7, availability: 'available', price: '$$', signal: 88 },
  { name: 'Spice Route', cuisine: 'Indian', rating: 4.9, vibe: 'Vibrant', ambiance: 8, availability: 'available', price: '$$', signal: 96 },
  { name: 'The Grill', cuisine: 'Steakhouse', rating: 4.6, vibe: 'Upscale', ambiance: 9, availability: 'busy', price: '$$$$', signal: 82 },
  { name: 'Oceanside', cuisine: 'Seafood', rating: 4.8, vibe: 'Relaxed', ambiance: 8, availability: 'available', price: '$$$', signal: 90 },
  { name: 'Bistro Moderne', cuisine: 'French', rating: 4.7, vibe: 'Intimate', ambiance: 9, availability: 'limited', price: '$$$', signal: 86 },
]

export default function AdaptiveDiscovery() {
  const { mood, preferredCuisines, preferredVibes } = useSufiStore()
  const [rankedRestaurants, setRankedRestaurants] = useState(allRestaurants)
  const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState<'relevance' | 'ambiance' | 'availability'>('relevance')
  
  useEffect(() => {
    let sorted = [...allRestaurants]
    
    // Adapt based on mood
    if (mood === 'romantic') {
      setSortBy('ambiance')
      sorted.sort((a, b) => b.ambiance - a.ambiance)
    } else if (mood === 'fast') {
      setSortBy('availability')
      const availabilityOrder = { available: 0, limited: 1, busy: 2 }
      sorted.sort((a, b) => availabilityOrder[a.availability] - availabilityOrder[b.availability])
    } else if (mood === 'luxury') {
      setSortBy('relevance')
      sorted.sort((a, b) => b.price.length - a.price.length)
    }
    
    // Personalize based on user preferences
    if (preferredCuisines.length > 0) {
      sorted = sorted.filter(r => 
        preferredCuisines.some(c => r.cuisine.toLowerCase().includes(c))
      )
    }
    
    if (preferredVibes.length > 0) {
      sorted = sorted.filter(r => 
        preferredVibes.some(v => r.vibe.toLowerCase().includes(v))
      )
    }
    
    setRankedRestaurants(sorted)
    
    // Animate reorder
    gsap.to('.discovery-card', {
      y: () => gsap.utils.random(-8, 8),
      duration: 0.5,
      stagger: 0.03,
      ease: 'back.out(0.5)',
    })
  }, [mood, preferredCuisines, preferredVibes])
  
  const getSortLabel = () => {
    switch(sortBy) {
      case 'ambiance': return '✨ Sorted by ambiance'
      case 'availability': return '⚡ Sorted by availability'
      default: return '🎯 Most relevant'
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-10 bg-[radial-gradient(circle,rgba(255,255,255,0.1)_1px,transparent_1px)] bg-[size:40px_40px]" />
      
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">ADAPTIVE DISCOVERY</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={mood === 'romantic' ? "Find your perfect ambiance" : 
                     mood === 'fast' ? "Find available tables now" : 
                     "Search that understands you"}
              subtitle={mood === 'romantic' ? "Curated for intimate moments" :
                        mood === 'fast' ? "Quick booking options prioritized" :
                        "Personalized to your taste"}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">{getSortLabel()}</p>
              {preferredCuisines.length > 0 && (
                <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                  <span className="text-xs text-white/40">You like:</span>
                  {preferredCuisines.map(c => (
                    <Badge key={c} variant="tertiary" size="sm">{c}</Badge>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              {rankedRestaurants.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => (
                <GlassPanel 
                  key={rest.name} 
                  hover 
                  padding="md" 
                  className={i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''}
                  onClick={() => adaptiveEngine.trackAction({ type: 'CLICK', payload: rest.cuisine.toLowerCase(), timestamp: Date.now() })}
                >
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                    <div>
                      <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                        {rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                         rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : 
                         rest.name === 'Spice Route' ? '🍛' : '🍽️'}
                      </div>
                      <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                      <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                  </div>
                  
                  <div className="mt-4">
                    <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                      <span>Match score</span>
                      <span className="text-primary">{rest.signal}%</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                      <div className="h-full w-[92%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  
                  {mood === 'fast' && rest.availability === 'available' && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-400 mt-2">✓ Available now</p>
                  )}
                  {mood === 'romantic' && rest.ambiance > 8 && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-tertiary mt-2">✨ Perfect for date night</p>
                  )}
                  {mood === 'luxury' && rest.price === '$$$$' && (
                    <p className="text-xs text-primary mt-2">🌟 Michelin recommended</p>
                  )}
                </GlassPanel>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 6️⃣ ADAPTIVE AI CONCIERGE
tsx
// components/landing/AdaptiveAI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { adaptiveEngine } from '@/lib/adaptive/adaptiveEngine'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
}

const getAIResponse = (query: string, mood: string, preferences: string[]) => {
  const lowerQuery = query.toLowerCase()
  
  // Context-aware responses based on mood and preferences
  if (lowerQuery.includes('sushi')) {
    if (mood === 'romantic') {
      return "For a romantic sushi experience, I recommend Sushi Nakazawa with omakase counter seating. Would you like me to check availability for a cozy dinner for two?"
    } else if (mood === 'fast') {
      return "Looking for quick sushi? Sugarfish has express lunch sets with no wait time. Want me to book a table for you?"
    } else {
      return "I found 8 great sushi spots. Based on your preferences, here are the top picks: Sushi Nakazawa (4.9★), Nobu (4.8★), and Sushi Yasuda (4.8★)."
    }
  }
  
  if (lowerQuery.includes('romantic')) {
    return "For a romantic evening, these spots are perfect: One if by Land (4.9★) has intimate ambiance, River Cafe (4.8★) offers scenic views, and The Modern (4.8★) provides elegant dining. Which vibe speaks to you?"
  }
  
  if (preferences.length > 0) {
    return `Based on your love for ${preferences.join(', ')}, I found these recommendations that match your taste. Would you like to see them?`
  }
  
  return "I found several great options based on your request. Sakura Hills (Japanese, 4.8★), La Piazza (Italian, 4.7★), and Spice Route (Indian, 4.9★) are top-rated near you. Want me to show you more details?"
}

export default function AdaptiveAI() {
  const { mood, preferredCuisines } = useSufiStore()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: getAIResponse('', mood, preferredCuisines) },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const [streamingText, setStreamingText] = useState('')
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, streamingText])
  
  const streamResponse = (text: string) => {
    setStreamingText('')
    let i = 0
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      if (i < text.length) {
        setStreamingText(prev => prev + text[i])
        i++
      } else {
        clearInterval(interval)
        setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: text }])
        setStreamingText('')
        setIsTyping(false)
      }
    }, 25)
  }
  
  const handleSend = () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    adaptiveEngine.trackAction({ type: 'SEARCH', payload: input, timestamp: Date.now() })
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    setTimeout(() => {
      const response = getAIResponse(userInput, mood, preferredCuisines)
      streamResponse(response)
    }, 1000)
  }
  
  const getAIPersonality = () => {
    switch(mood) {
      case 'romantic': return '✨ Romantic Concierge'
      case 'fast': return '⚡ Quick Finder'
      case 'luxury': return '🌟 Elite Concierge'
      default: return '🧠 AI Concierge'
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">{getAIPersonality()}</span>
                  <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : mood === 'fast' ? 'success' : 'primary'} size="sm">
                    {mood}
                  </Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[450px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl max-w-[85%]">
                      <p className="text-sm">{streamingText}<span className="animate-pulse">▊</span></p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                
                {isTyping && !streamingText && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder={mood === 'romantic' ? "Looking for something special?" : 
                                 mood === 'fast' ? "Need a quick reservation?" : 
                                 "Ask me anything..."}
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">CONTEXT-AWARE AI</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Just ask"
              subtitle={mood === 'romantic' ? "I'll find the perfect spot for your special moments" :
                        mood === 'fast' ? "Quick, smart recommendations for when you're on the go" :
                        "Natural language. Intelligent recommendations."}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">PERSONALIZED SUGGESTIONS</p>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {preferredCuisines.length > 0 ? (
                  preferredCuisines.map(cuisine => (
                    <button
                      key={cuisine}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setInput(`Find ${cuisine} restaurants`)
                        setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                      }}
                      className="px-3 py-1.5 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                    >
                      {cuisine}
                    </button>
                  ))
                ) : (
                  ['romantic dinner', 'best sushi', 'vegan options', 'rooftop bar'].map(example => (
                    <button
                      key={example}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setInput(example)
                        setTimeout(() => handleSend(), 100)
                      }}
                      className="px-3 py-1.5 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
                    >
                      {example}
                    </button>
                  ))
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span>🧠</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">Learning your preferences</p>
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-white/40 mt-1">
                    <span>Preference accuracy</span>
                    <span>{Math.min(94, 60 + (preferredCuisines.length * 8))}%</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-1 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-[94%] bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🧑‍🍳 7️⃣ ADAPTIVE OWNER DASHBOARD
tsx
// components/landing/AdaptiveOwner.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Booking {
  name: string
  time: string
  guests: number
  status: 'confirmed' | 'pending'
}

export default function AdaptiveOwner() {
  const { activity, mood } = useSufiStore()
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState<Booking[]>([
    { name: 'Emma Watson', time: '7:00 PM', guests: 4, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'James Chen', time: '7:30 PM', guests: 2, status: 'confirmed' },
    { name: 'Sofia Rodriguez', time: '8:00 PM', guests: 6, status: 'pending' },
  ])
  const [occupancy, setOccupancy] = useState(68)
  const [revenue, setRevenue] = useState(4280)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const interval = setInterval(() => {
      const newBooking: Booking = {
        name: ['David Park', 'Sarah Kim', 'Lisa Wong'][Math.floor(Math.random() * 3)],
        time: `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 3) + 7}:${Math.random() > 0.5 ? '00' : '30'} PM`,
        guests: Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 2,
        status: 'confirmed',
      }
      setBookings(prev => [newBooking, ...prev.slice(0, 4)])
      setOccupancy(prev => Math.min(95, prev + Math.random() * 3))
      setRevenue(prev => prev + Math.floor(Math.random() * 120))
      
      gsap.to('.booking-item:first-child', {
        scale: 1.02,
        duration: 0.3,
        yoyo: true,
        repeat: 1,
        backgroundColor: 'rgba(163,166,255,0.1)',
      })
    }, 8000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [])
  
  // Adaptive highlighting based on activity
  const highlightLive = activity > 0.7
  const highlightAlert = occupancy > 85
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <div className="text-center mb-12">
          <Badge variant="secondary">ADAPTIVE OS</Badge>
          <Heading
            title={highlightLive ? "High Activity Mode" : "Control, not chaos"}
            subtitle={highlightLive ? "System is optimizing in real-time" : "Real-time operations. AI automation."}
            align="center"
            size="lg"
            className="mt-4"
          />
        </div>
        
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-8">
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className={highlightLive ? 'ring-2 ring-primary' : ''}>
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
                <h3 className="font-semibold flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse ${highlightLive ? 'bg-primary' : 'bg-green-500'}`} />
                  Live Dashboard
                  {highlightLive && <Badge variant="primary" size="sm">HIGH ACTIVITY</Badge>}
                </h3>
                <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Updated in real-time</span>
              </div>
              
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-6">
                <div className={`p-4 rounded-xl text-center transition-all ${highlightAlert ? 'bg-red-500/10' : 'bg-white/5'}`}>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{Math.floor(occupancy)}%</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Occupancy</p>
                  {highlightAlert && <p className="text-[10px] text-red-400 mt-1">near capacity</p>}
                </div>
                <div className={`p-4 rounded-xl text-center transition-all ${highlightLive ? 'bg-primary/10 scale-105' : 'bg-white/5'}`}>
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">{bookings.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Active Bookings</p>
                  {highlightLive && <p className="text-[10px] text-primary mt-1">peak hour</p>}
                </div>
                <div className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl text-center">
                  <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-primary">${revenue.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Revenue Today</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="mt-4">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-3">Recent Bookings</p>
                <div className="space-y-2">
                  {bookings.map((booking, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="booking-item flex justify-between items-center p-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-white/5 transition-all">
                      <div>
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">{booking.name}</p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{booking.guests} guests</p>
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-right">
                        <p className="text-sm">{booking.time}</p>
                        <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                          booking.status === 'confirmed'
                            ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400'
                            : 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400'
                        }`}>
                          {booking.status}
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-4">
                <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                <h3 className="font-semibold">AI Automation</h3>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className={`p-3 rounded-xl transition-all ${highlightAlert ? 'bg-red-500/20 border border-red-500/30' : 'bg-primary/10 border border-primary/20'}`}>
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary mb-1">⚠️ No-Show Risk</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">High probability at 8 PM ({highlightAlert ? '58' : '42'}%)</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Overbook by {highlightAlert ? '15' : '10'}%
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-tertiary/10 border border-tertiary/20 rounded-xl">
                  <p className="text-sm text-tertiary mb-1">📈 Demand Spike</p>
                  <p className="text-xs">Weekend evenings up {mood === 'fast' ? '45' : '35'}% vs last week</p>
                  <Button variant="secondary" size="sm" className="mt-2 w-full" magnetic={false}>
                    Adjust pricing
                  </Button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md">
              <h3 className="font-semibold mb-3">Quick Stats</h3>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Table utilization</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">94%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg turn time</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">28min</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/60">Avg cover</span>
                  <span className="font-mono">$89</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}

    <html lang="en">

        <ReactLenis root options={{ lerp: 0.08, wheelMultiplier: 0.8 }}>

            <CursorSystem />

            {children}
          </MotionProvider>

🎯 WHAT YOU NOW HAVE
Feature	Description
Adaptive Engine	Tracks user behavior, learns preferences
Global State	Intent, activity, mood, preferences
Adaptive Background	Changes color based on mood and activity
Adaptive Hero	Dynamic copy, personalized placeholders
Adaptive Discovery	Sorts by ambiance/availability based on mood
Adaptive AI	Context-aware responses, personality changes
Adaptive Dashboard	Highlights relevant metrics based on activity
Preference Learning	Remembers cuisines, vibes, search history
Feedback Loop	User action → system learns → UI adapts
🔥 SUFI is now a truly adaptive system where every user sees a slightly different interface based on their behavior, mood, and preferences. This is the real differentiator.

🧠 1️⃣ WHAT YOU ARE BUILDING

Core idea:

User intent → embedding → similarity search → ranking → UI adapts
🔥 Example:

User types:

“romantic dinner with wine”

System:

converts to embedding
compares with restaurant embeddings
ranks results
UI updates (hero + discovery + AI)

Frontend (Next.js)
  ↓
API (Node / FastAPI)
  ↓
Embedding Model (mxbai / OpenAI)
  ↓
Vector DB (Pinecone / Weaviate / Chroma)
  ↓
Ranking Engine
  ↓
Response → UI updates
🚀 3️⃣ EMBEDDING SETUP (CORE)

Since you mentioned earlier:

👉 you want mxbai-embed-large

Perfect.

📦 Install (Ollama)
ollama pull mxbai-embed-large
🔥 Generate embedding
# embedding.py
import requests

def embed(text):
    res = requests.post("http://localhost:11434/api/embeddings", json={
        "model": "mxbai-embed-large",
        "prompt": text
    })
    return res.json()["embedding"]
🧠 4️⃣ STORE RESTAURANTS AS VECTORS
Example data:
{
  "name": "Sky Lounge",
  "description": "rooftop romantic dinner with wine and city view"
}
Store:
vector = embed("rooftop romantic dinner with wine")

db.insert({
  "id": 1,
  "vector": vector,
  "metadata": {...}
})
🔍 5️⃣ SEARCH (SIMILARITY MATCH)
query_vec = embed("romantic dinner")

results = db.search(query_vec, top_k=5)

👉 This gives:

best matching restaurants

🧠 6️⃣ RANKING ENGINE (IMPORTANT)

Vector similarity alone is not enough.

🔥 Add scoring:
def rank(result):
    score = result.similarity

    if result.metadata["rating"] > 4.5:
        score += 0.1

    if result.metadata["available"]:
        score += 0.2

    return score

👉 This creates:

💀 real intelligence

🔁 7️⃣ API ENDPOINT
📂 /api/search
export async function POST(req) {
  const { query } = await req.json()

  const res = await fetch("http://localhost:8000/search", {
    method: "POST",
    body: JSON.stringify({ query })
  })

  const data = await res.json()

  return Response.json(data)
}
🎬 8️⃣ FRONTEND INTEGRATION (CRITICAL)
🔥 Connect to your system
const { setIntent, setBestMatch } = useSufiStore()

async function search(query) {
  setIntent(query)

  const res = await fetch("/api/search", {
    method: "POST",
    body: JSON.stringify({ query })
  })

  const data = await res.json()

  setBestMatch(data[0].id)
}

👉 Now:

Hero reacts
Discovery reorders
AI updates
🤖 9️⃣ AI CONCIERGE (RAG)

Instead of generic response:

def generate_response(query):
    results = search(query)

    context = "\n".join([r["description"] for r in results])

    prompt = f"""
    User wants: {query}

    Options:
    {context}

    Recommend best options conversationally.
    """

    return llm(prompt)

👉 This becomes:

🔥 real AI concierge

# backend/app.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException

    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["http://localhost:3000"],
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# Initialize ChromaDB
client = chromadb.PersistentClient(path="./chroma_db")
collection = client.get_or_create_collection(
    name="restaurants",
    embedding_function=embedding_functions.OllamaEmbeddingFunction(
        model_name="mxbai-embed-large",
        url="http://localhost:11434/api/embeddings"
    )
)

# Sample restaurant data
