# Initialize database with restaurant data
def init_db():
    for restaurant in RESTAURANTS:
        # Create text for embedding
        text = f"{restaurant['name']} {restaurant['description']} {restaurant['cuisine']} {' '.join(restaurant['tags'])}"
        
        collection.upsert(
            ids=[restaurant["id"]],
            documents=[text],
            metadatas=[{
                "name": restaurant["name"],
                "cuisine": restaurant["cuisine"],
                "rating": restaurant["rating"],
                "price": restaurant["price"],
                "vibe": restaurant["vibe"],
                "availability": restaurant["availability"],
                "location": restaurant["location"],
                "tags": restaurant["tags"]
            }]
        )

# Initialize on startup
@app.on_event("startup")
async def startup_event():
    init_db()

class SearchRequest(BaseModel):
    query: str
    top_k: Optional[int] = 10

class RestaurantResult(BaseModel):
    id: str
    name: str
    cuisine: str
    rating: float
    price: str
    vibe: str
    availability: str
    location: str
    tags: List[str]
    similarity: float
    score: float

def calculate_rank_score(result, query_embedding=None):
    """Multi-signal ranking engine"""
    metadata = result["metadata"]
    similarity = result["similarity"]
    
    # Base score from vector similarity
    score = similarity
    
    # Rating boost (0-0.2)
    rating_boost = (metadata["rating"] - 4.0) * 0.1
    score += max(0, min(0.2, rating_boost))
    
    # Availability boost
    availability_boost = {
        "available": 0.2,
        "limited": 0.1,
        "busy": 0
    }.get(metadata["availability"], 0)
    score += availability_boost
    
    # Price preference (higher for luxury, lower for casual)
    if "luxury" in query_embedding if query_embedding else []:
        price_boost = {"$$$$": 0.1, "$$$": 0.05, "$$": 0, "$": 0}.get(metadata["price"], 0)
        score += price_boost
    
    # Vibe matching
    vibe_weights = {
        "Romantic": {"romantic": 0.15, "date": 0.1},
        "Intimate": {"romantic": 0.1, "quiet": 0.1},
        "Upscale": {"luxury": 0.1, "elegant": 0.1},
        "Vibrant": {"lively": 0.1, "fun": 0.1},
        "Casual": {"casual": 0.1},
        "Relaxed": {"relaxed": 0.1}
    }
    
    return min(1.0, score)

@app.post("/api/search")
async def search(request: SearchRequest):
    """Vector similarity search with ranking"""
    try:
        # Query embedding via Ollama
        embed_response = requests.post(
            "http://localhost:11434/api/embeddings",
            json={"model": "mxbai-embed-large", "prompt": request.query}
        )
        
        if embed_response.status_code != 200:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Embedding service unavailable")
        
        embedding = embed_response.json()["embedding"]
        
        # Vector search
        results = collection.query(
            query_embeddings=[embedding],
            n_results=request.top_k,
            include=["documents", "metadatas", "distances"]
        )
        
        # Format and rank results
        ranked_results = []
        for i in range(len(results["ids"][0])):
            result = {
                "id": results["ids"][0][i],
                "metadata": results["metadatas"][0][i],
                "similarity": 1 - results["distances"][0][i],  # Convert distance to similarity
                "document": results["documents"][0][i]
            }
            
            score = calculate_rank_score(result, request.query)
            result["score"] = score
            
            ranked_results.append(result)
        
        # Sort by final score
        ranked_results.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)
        
        # Format response
        response = []
        for r in ranked_results:
            meta = r["metadata"]
            response.append({
                "id": r["id"],
                "name": meta["name"],
                "cuisine": meta["cuisine"],
                "rating": meta["rating"],
                "price": meta["price"],
                "vibe": meta["vibe"],
                "availability": meta["availability"],
                "location": meta["location"],
                "tags": meta["tags"],
                "similarity": r["similarity"],
                "score": r["score"]
            })
        
        return response
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Search error: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@app.post("/api/ai-concierge")
async def ai_concierge(request: SearchRequest):
    """RAG-powered AI concierge"""
    try:
        # First, search for relevant restaurants
        search_results = await search(request)
        
        # Build context from top 3 results
        context = "\n".join([
            f"- {r['name']}: {r.get('tags', [])} restaurant with {r['rating']}★ rating, {r['vibe']} vibe. Perfect for {request.query}"
            for r in search_results[:3]
        ])
        
        # Generate AI response using Ollama
        prompt = f"""You are SUFI AI, a helpful restaurant concierge.
        
User is looking for: {request.query}

Here are the top restaurant matches:
{context}

Provide a friendly, conversational recommendation. Suggest 2-3 options and ask if they'd like to book. Keep it concise but helpful."""

        response = requests.post(
            "http://localhost:11434/api/generate",
            json={
                "model": "llama3.2",
                "prompt": prompt,
                "stream": False
            }
        )
        
        if response.status_code != 200:
            # Fallback response
            ai_response = f"I found {len(search_results)} great options for '{request.query}'. {search_results[0]['name']} has {search_results[0]['rating']}★ rating and a {search_results[0]['vibe']} vibe. Would you like me to check availability?"
        else:
            ai_response = response.json()["response"]
        
        return {
            "message": ai_response,
            "recommendations": search_results[:5]
        }
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"AI error: {e}")
        return {
            "message": f"I found several great options for your request. Would you like to see the top recommendations?",
            "recommendations": []
        }

@app.get("/api/restaurants/{restaurant_id}")
async def get_restaurant(restaurant_id: str):
    """Get restaurant by ID"""
    result = collection.get(
        ids=[restaurant_id],
        include=["metadatas"]
    )
    
    if result["ids"]:
        return result["metadatas"][0]
    raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Restaurant not found")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    import uvicorn
    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8000)
🧠 2️⃣ FRONTEND API CLIENT
tsx
// lib/api/vectorSearch.ts
import axios from 'axios'

const API_URL = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:8000'

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  location: string
  tags: string[]
  similarity: number
  score: number
}

export interface AIConciergeResponse {
  message: string
  recommendations: Restaurant[]
}

export const vectorSearch = {
  search: async (query: string, topK: number = 10): Promise<Restaurant[]> => {
    const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/api/search`, { query, top_k: topK })
    return response.data
  },
  
  aiConcierge: async (query: string): Promise<AIConciergeResponse> => {
    const response = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/api/ai-concierge`, { query })
    return response.data
  },
  
  getRestaurant: async (id: string): Promise<Restaurant> => {
    const response = await axios.get(`${API_URL}/api/restaurants/${id}`)
    return response.data
  }
}
🔍 3️⃣ VECTOR SEARCH HOOK
tsx
// lib/hooks/useVectorSearch.ts
import { useState, useCallback } from 'react'
import { useQuery, useMutation } from '@tanstack/react-query'
import { vectorSearch, Restaurant, AIConciergeResponse } from '@/lib/api/vectorSearch'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export const useVectorSearch = () => {
  const { setIntent, setBestMatch, setMood } = useSufiStore()
  const [searchResults, setSearchResults] = useState<Restaurant[]>([])
  const [isSearching, setIsSearching] = useState(false)
  
  const performSearch = useCallback(async (query: string) => {
    if (!query.trim()) return []
    
    setIsSearching(true)
    setIntent(query)
    
    // Detect mood from query
    if (query.toLowerCase().includes('romantic') || query.toLowerCase().includes('date')) {
      setMood('romantic')
    } else if (query.toLowerCase().includes('quick') || query.toLowerCase().includes('fast')) {
      setMood('fast')
    } else if (query.toLowerCase().includes('luxury') || query.toLowerCase().includes('michelin')) {
      setMood('luxury')
    }
    
    try {
      const results = await vectorSearch.search(query)
      setSearchResults(results)
      
      if (results.length > 0) {
        setBestMatch(parseInt(results[0].id))
      }
      
      return results
    } finally {
      setIsSearching(false)
    }
  }, [setIntent, setBestMatch, setMood])
  
  const { data: aiResponse, mutate: getAIResponse, isLoading: isAILoading } = useMutation({
    mutationFn: (query: string) => vectorSearch.aiConcierge(query)
  })
  
  return {
    searchResults,
    isSearching,
    performSearch,
    aiResponse,
    getAIResponse,
    isAILoading
  }
}
🎬 4️⃣ ADAPTIVE HERO WITH VECTOR SEARCH
tsx
// components/landing/VectorHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'

export default function VectorHero() {
  const { mood, activity } = useSufiStore()
  const { performSearch, isSearching, searchResults } = useVectorSearch()
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState('')
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim()) return
    await performSearch(inputValue)
  }
  
  const heroCopy = {
    neutral: { title: "Find your next", highlight: "perfect meal", subtitle: "AI-powered discovery for every craving" },
    romantic: { title: "Create the", highlight: "perfect evening", subtitle: "Discover intimate spots for unforgettable moments" },
    fast: { title: "Quick. Smart.", highlight: "Instant booking", subtitle: "Find available tables near you in seconds" },
    luxury: { title: "Experience", highlight: "exceptional dining", subtitle: "Curated selections for discerning palates" }
  }
  
  const copy = heroCopy[mood]
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md">
          {mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic Mode' : 
           mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick Mode' : 
           mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury Mode' : '🧠 Vector Search'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">VECTOR SEARCH ACTIVE</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{(activity * 1.5 + 0.5).toFixed(2)}</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {copy.title}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">{copy.highlight}</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {copy.subtitle}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="romantic dinner with wine, rooftop sushi, quiet Italian..."
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={isSearching}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {isSearching ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        {/* Search results preview */}
        {searchResults.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-8 flex justify-center gap-3 flex-wrap">
            {searchResults.slice(0, 3).map((result) => (
              <Badge key={result.id} variant="secondary" size="md">
                {result.name} • {Math.round(result.similarity * 100)}% match
              </Badge>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            semantic search • vector similarity
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 5️⃣ RAG-POWERED AI CONCIERGE
tsx
// components/landing/RAGConcierge.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function RAGConcierge() {
  const { mood, preferredCuisines } = useSufiStore()
  const { getAIResponse, aiResponse, isAILoading } = useVectorSearch()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm SUFI AI. Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find the perfect restaurant using semantic search." },
  ])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])
  
  // Handle AI response when it arrives
  useEffect(() => {
    if (aiResponse && aiResponse.message) {
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { 
        id: prev.length + 1, 
        type: 'ai', 
        content: aiResponse.message,
        recommendations: aiResponse.recommendations
      }])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }
  }, [aiResponse])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping || isAILoading) return
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    // Trigger RAG search
    getAIResponse(userInput)
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">RAG-Powered AI Concierge</span>
                  <Badge variant="primary" size="sm">vector search</Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {/* Restaurant recommendations from RAG */}
                      {msg.recommendations && msg.recommendations.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                          <p className="text-xs text-white/60 mt-2">Top picks:</p>
                          {msg.recommendations.slice(0, 3).map((rec: any) => (
                            <div key={rec.id} className="bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all">
                              <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                                <div>
                                  <p className="font-medium text-sm">{rec.name}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{rec.cuisine} • {rec.vibe}</p>
                                </div>
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rec.rating}</span>
                                  <button className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg">
                                    Book
                                  </button>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              <div className="mt-1">
                                <div className="flex justify-between text-[10px] text-white/40">
                                  <span>Match score</span>
                                  <span>{Math.round(rec.similarity * 100)}%</span>
                                </div>
                                <div className="h-1 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-0.5 overflow-hidden">
                                  <div className="h-full w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" 
                                       style={{ width: `${rec.similarity * 100}%` }} />
                                </div>
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '0ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder="Find me a romantic rooftop with wine..."
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping || isAILoading} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  Powered by mxbai-embed-large • semantic vector search
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">RAG INTELLIGENCE</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Ask anything"
              subtitle="Semantic search understands what you really want, not just keywords"
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">SEMANTIC UNDERSTANDING</p>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="p-2 bg-white/5 rounded-lg">
                  <p className="text-xs text-primary">"romantic dinner with wine"</p>
                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">→ Finds: Sky Lounge, Bistro Moderne, The Rooftop Garden</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-2 bg-white/5 rounded-lg">
                  <p className="text-xs text-primary">"quick business lunch near financial district"</p>
                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">→ Finds: The Grill, La Piazza, Sakura Hills</p>
                </div>
                <div className="p-2 bg-white/5 rounded-lg">
                  <p className="text-xs text-primary">"authentic Japanese omakase"</p>
                  <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">→ Finds: Sakura Hills (98% match)</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span>🔍</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">Vector Search Active</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">mxbai-embed-large • 1024 dimensions</p>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-2 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 6️⃣ VECTOR SEARCH DISCOVERY
tsx
// components/landing/VectorDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function VectorDiscovery() {
  const { searchResults, performSearch } = useVectorSearch()
  const { mood, intent } = useSufiStore()
  const [showResults, setShowResults] = useState(false)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (intent && intent !== "romantic dinner") {
      performSearch(intent)
      setShowResults(true)
    }
  }, [intent, performSearch])
  
  const getSortLabel = () => {
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '✨ Sorted by ambiance & romantic vibe'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Sorted by availability'
    return '🎯 Sorted by semantic relevance'
  }
  
  const displayResults = showResults && searchResults.length > 0 ? searchResults : []
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">SEMANTIC DISCOVERY</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={mood === 'romantic' ? "Find your perfect ambiance" : 
                     mood === 'fast' ? "Find available tables now" : 
                     "Search that truly understands"}
              subtitle="Vector similarity + multi-signal ranking"
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">{getSortLabel()}</p>
              {intent && intent !== "romantic dinner" && (
                <div className="mt-2">
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Current search:</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary">"{intent}"</p>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            {displayResults.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {displayResults.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => (
                  <GlassPanel 
                    key={rest.id} 
                    hover 
                    padding="md" 
                    className={i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''}
                  >
                    <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                      <div>
                        <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                          {rest.name === 'Sky Lounge' ? '🌆' : 
                           rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                           rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : '🍽️'}
                        </div>
                        <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                        <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-4">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                        <span>Semantic match</span>
                        <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.similarity * 100)}%</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" 
                             style={{ width: `${rest.similarity * 100}%` }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                      {rest.tags?.slice(0, 3).map(tag => (
                        <span key={tag} className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full">
                          {tag}
                        </span>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    
                    {mood === 'romantic' && rest.vibe === 'Romantic' && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-tertiary mt-2">✨ Perfect for your mood</p>
                    )}
                    {mood === 'fast' && rest.availability === 'available' && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-green-400 mt-2">✓ Available now</p>
                    )}
                  </GlassPanel>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="glass-panel p-12 text-center">
                <p className="text-white/40">Try a search above to see semantic matching in action</p>
                <div className="mt-4 flex justify-center gap-2">
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"romantic dinner"</Badge>
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"quick lunch"</Badge>
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"sushi omakase"</Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}

🧱 2️⃣ DATA YOU MUST CAPTURE

Every interaction = signal.

🎯 Track this:
SEARCH → intent
CLICK → preference
BOOKING → strong signal
TIME SPENT → interest
SKIP → negative signal
🔥 Example:
{
  "user_id": "u123",
  "action": "BOOKING",
  "restaurant_id": 42,
  "tags": ["romantic", "wine"],
  "timestamp": 1710000000
}
🗄️ 3️⃣ USER PROFILE VECTOR (CORE IDEA)

Each user has:

🔥 their own embedding vector

🧠 Build it:
def update_user_vector(user_vector, item_vector, weight=0.2):
    return user_vector + weight * item_vector

👉 Meaning:

user books romantic places
→ their vector shifts toward “romantic”
🔍 4️⃣ PERSONALIZED SEARCH (IMPORTANT)

Instead of:

query → search
DO THIS:
(query vector + user vector) → search
🔥 Code:
final_query = query_vector + 0.3 * user_vector
results = db.search(final_query)

👉 Result:

💀 same query → different results per user

🤖 5️⃣ PERSONALIZED AI RESPONSES
Before:

“Here are some restaurants…”

After:
“You usually prefer quiet romantic places — here are the best options tonight.”
Code:
def generate_response(query, user_profile):
    if "romantic" in user_profile:
        tone = "romantic"

    return f"Based on your taste, here are the best {tone} options..."

🧠 1️⃣ USER PROFILE & BEHAVIOR TRACKING
tsx
// lib/state/userProfileStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware"

export interface UserAction {
  id: string
  type: 'SEARCH' | 'CLICK' | 'BOOKING' | 'VIEW' | 'SKIP'
  restaurantId?: string
  query?: string
  tags?: string[]
  timestamp: number
  timeSpent?: number
}

export interface UserProfile {
  userId: string
  vector: number[] // 1024-dim embedding
  preferences: {
    cuisines: Map<string, number> // cuisine -> weight
    vibes: Map<string, number>    // vibe -> weight
    pricePoints: Map<string, number>
    tags: Map<string, number>
  }
  history: UserAction[]
  totalBookings: number
  totalSearches: number
  lastActive: number
}

interface UserProfileState {
  profile: UserProfile | null
  isLoading: boolean
  actions: UserAction[]
  
  // Actions
  initializeProfile: (userId: string) => void
  trackAction: (action: Omit<UserAction, 'id' | 'timestamp'>) => Promise<void>
  updateUserVector: (itemVector: number[], weight: number) => void
  getPersonalizedVector: (queryVector: number[]) => number[]
  getPreferencesForUI: () => { topCuisines: string[], topVibes: string[], mood: string }
  resetProfile: () => void
}

// Helper to generate random user ID if not exists
const getOrCreateUserId = (): string => {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return 'anonymous'
  let userId = localStorage.getItem('sufi_user_id')
  if (!userId) {
    userId = `user_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`
    localStorage.setItem('sufi_user_id', userId)
  }
  return userId
}

export const useUserProfileStore = create<UserProfileState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      profile: null,
      isLoading: false,
      actions: [],

      initializeProfile: (userId: string) => {
        set({
          profile: {
            userId,
            vector: new Array(1024).fill(0), // Initialize with zero vector
            preferences: {
              cuisines: new Map(),
              vibes: new Map(),
              pricePoints: new Map(),
              tags: new Map(),
            },
            history: [],
            totalBookings: 0,
            totalSearches: 0,
            lastActive: Date.now(),
          },
          actions: []
        })
      },

      trackAction: async (action) => {
        const { profile, actions } = get()
        if (!profile) return

        const newAction: UserAction = {
          id: `${Date.now()}_${Math.random()}`,
          ...action,
          timestamp: Date.now(),
        }

        // Update profile based on action
        const updatedProfile = { ...profile }
        updatedProfile.lastActive = Date.now()

        if (action.type === 'SEARCH' && action.query) {
          updatedProfile.totalSearches++
          // Extract keywords for preference learning
          const keywords = action.query.toLowerCase().split(' ')
          const preferenceKeywords = ['romantic', 'cozy', 'intimate', 'casual', 'vibrant', 'upscale', 'fast', 'quick']
          keywords.forEach(word => {
            if (preferenceKeywords.includes(word)) {
              const current = updatedProfile.preferences.vibes.get(word) || 0
              updatedProfile.preferences.vibes.set(word, current + 1)
            }
          })
        }

        if (action.type === 'CLICK' && action.tags) {
          action.tags.forEach(tag => {
            const current = updatedProfile.preferences.tags.get(tag) || 0
            updatedProfile.preferences.tags.set(tag, current + 1)
          })
        }

        if (action.type === 'BOOKING' && action.tags) {
          updatedProfile.totalBookings++
          // Stronger weight for bookings
          action.tags.forEach(tag => {
            const current = updatedProfile.preferences.tags.get(tag) || 0
            updatedProfile.preferences.tags.set(tag, current + 3) // Booking = 3x weight
          })
          
          if (action.query) {
            const current = updatedProfile.preferences.vibes.get(action.query) || 0
            updatedProfile.preferences.vibes.set(action.query, current + 5)
          }
        }

        set({
          profile: updatedProfile,
          actions: [...actions, newAction].slice(-100) // Keep last 100 actions
        })

        // Send to backend for storage
        try {
          await fetch('/api/user/track', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
              userId: profile.userId,
              action: newAction,
              preferences: {
                cuisines: Array.from(updatedProfile.preferences.cuisines.entries()),
                vibes: Array.from(updatedProfile.preferences.vibes.entries()),
                tags: Array.from(updatedProfile.preferences.tags.entries()),
              }
            })
          })
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Failed to track action:', error)
        }
      },

      updateUserVector: (itemVector: number[], weight: number = 0.2) => {
        const { profile } = get()
        if (!profile) return

        const newVector = [...profile.vector]
        for (let i = 0; i < newVector.length; i++) {
          newVector[i] = newVector[i] + (itemVector[i] * weight)
        }

        set({
          profile: {
            ...profile,
            vector: newVector
          }
        })
      },

      getPersonalizedVector: (queryVector: number[]) => {
        const { profile } = get()
        if (!profile) return queryVector

        // Blend query with user profile (70% query, 30% user)
        const personalized = new Array(1024).fill(0)
        for (let i = 0; i < personalized.length; i++) {
          personalized[i] = (queryVector[i] * 0.7) + (profile.vector[i] * 0.3)
        }
        return personalized
      },

      getPreferencesForUI: () => {
        const { profile } = get()
        if (!profile) return { topCuisines: [], topVibes: [], mood: 'neutral' }

        // Get top preferences
        const topCuisines = Array.from(profile.preferences.cuisines.entries())
          .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
          .slice(0, 3)
          .map(([name]) => name)

        const topVibes = Array.from(profile.preferences.vibes.entries())
          .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
          .slice(0, 2)
          .map(([vibe]) => vibe)

        // Determine mood from top vibes
        let mood = 'neutral'
        if (topVibes.includes('romantic') || topVibes.includes('cozy') || topVibes.includes('intimate')) {
          mood = 'romantic'
        } else if (topVibes.includes('fast') || topVibes.includes('quick')) {
          mood = 'fast'
        } else if (topVibes.includes('upscale') || topVibes.includes('luxury')) {
          mood = 'luxury'
        }

        return { topCuisines, topVibes, mood }
      },

      resetProfile: () => {
        const userId = getOrCreateUserId()
        set({
          profile: {
            userId,
            vector: new Array(1024).fill(0),
            preferences: {
              cuisines: new Map(),
              vibes: new Map(),
              pricePoints: new Map(),
              tags: new Map(),
            },
            history: [],
            totalBookings: 0,
            totalSearches: 0,
            lastActive: Date.now(),
          },
          actions: []
        })
        localStorage.removeItem('sufi_user_id')
      }
    }),
    {
      name: 'sufi-user-profile',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        profile: state.profile ? {
          ...state.profile,
          preferences: {
            cuisines: Array.from(state.profile.preferences.cuisines.entries()),
            vibes: Array.from(state.profile.preferences.vibes.entries()),
            pricePoints: Array.from(state.profile.preferences.pricePoints.entries()),
            tags: Array.from(state.profile.preferences.tags.entries()),
          }
        } : null,
        actions: state.actions.slice(-20) // Keep last 20 actions in storage
      }),
      onRehydrateStorage: () => (state) => {
        if (state?.profile && state.profile.preferences) {
          // Convert arrays back to Maps
          const prefs = state.profile.preferences as any
          state.profile.preferences = {
            cuisines: new Map(prefs.cuisines || []),
            vibes: new Map(prefs.vibes || []),
            pricePoints: new Map(prefs.pricePoints || []),
            tags: new Map(prefs.tags || []),
          }
        }
      }
    }
  )
)

// Helper to initialize profile on app start
export const initUserProfile = () => {
  const userId = getOrCreateUserId()
  const { profile, initializeProfile } = useUserProfileStore.getState()
  if (!profile) {
    initializeProfile(userId)
  }
}
🔧 2️⃣ BACKEND USER PROFILE API
python
# backend/user_profile.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Dict, Any
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime

router = APIRouter()

# Simple JSON storage (upgrade to PostgreSQL later)
USER_DATA_FILE = "user_profiles.json"

def load_user_data():
    if os.path.exists(USER_DATA_FILE):
        with open(USER_DATA_FILE, 'r') as f:
            return json.load(f)
    return {}

def save_user_data(data):
    with open(USER_DATA_FILE, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(data, f)

class UserAction(BaseModel):
    userId: str
    action: Dict[str, Any]
    preferences: Dict[str, List]

@router.post("/user/track")
async def track_user_action(data: UserAction):
    """Store user action and update profile"""
    user_data = load_user_data()
    
    if data.userId not in user_data:
        user_data[data.userId] = {
            "profile": {},
            "history": [],
            "preferences": {
                "cuisines": [],
                "vibes": [],
                "tags": []
            }
        }
    
    # Update preferences
    prefs = user_data[data.userId]["preferences"]
    for cuisine, weight in data.preferences.get("cuisines", []):
        prefs["cuisines"].append({"name": cuisine, "weight": weight, "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()})
    
    for vibe, weight in data.preferences.get("vibes", []):
        prefs["vibes"].append({"name": vibe, "weight": weight, "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()})
    
    for tag, weight in data.preferences.get("tags", []):
        prefs["tags"].append({"name": tag, "weight": weight, "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()})
    
    # Keep only last 100 for each
    prefs["cuisines"] = prefs["cuisines"][-100:]
    prefs["vibes"] = prefs["vibes"][-100:]
    prefs["tags"] = prefs["tags"][-100:]
    
    # Store action
    user_data[data.userId]["history"].append({
        "action": data.action,
        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
    })
    user_data[data.userId]["history"] = user_data[data.userId]["history"][-100:]
    
    save_user_data(user_data)
    
    return {"status": "success"}

@router.get("/user/profile/{user_id}")
async def get_user_profile(user_id: str):
    """Get user profile for personalization"""
    user_data = load_user_data()
    
    if user_id not in user_data:
        return {
            "userId": user_id,
            "preferences": {
                "topCuisines": [],
                "topVibes": [],
                "topTags": []
            },
            "totalActions": 0
        }
    
    data = user_data[user_id]
    
    # Aggregate preferences
    cuisine_weights = {}
    vibe_weights = {}
    tag_weights = {}
    
    for c in data["preferences"]["cuisines"]:
        cuisine_weights[c["name"]] = cuisine_weights.get(c["name"], 0) + c["weight"]
    
    for v in data["preferences"]["vibes"]:
        vibe_weights[v["name"]] = vibe_weights.get(v["name"], 0) + v["weight"]
    
    for t in data["preferences"]["tags"]:
        tag_weights[t["name"]] = tag_weights.get(t["name"], 0) + t["weight"]
    
    return {
        "userId": user_id,
        "preferences": {
            "topCuisines": sorted(cuisine_weights.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5],
            "topVibes": sorted(vibe_weights.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:3],
            "topTags": sorted(tag_weights.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:10]
        },
        "totalActions": len(data["history"])
    }
🔍 3️⃣ PERSONALIZED SEARCH ENGINE
python
# backend/personalized_search.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Optional
import requests
import chromadb
from chromadb.utils import embedding_functions

router = APIRouter()

# Initialize ChromaDB
client = chromadb.PersistentClient(path="./chroma_db")
collection = client.get_collection("restaurants")

def embed(text: str) -> List[float]:
    """Generate embedding using mxbai-embed-large"""
    response = requests.post(
        "http://localhost:11434/api/embeddings",
        json={"model": "mxbai-embed-large", "prompt": text}
    )
    return response.json()["embedding"]

def get_user_vector(user_id: str) -> List[float]:
    """Get or create user preference vector"""
    # Load user profile
    import json
    import os
    
    user_file = "user_profiles.json"
    if os.path.exists(user_file):
        with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
            user_data = json.load(f)
        
        if user_id in user_data:
            # Build vector from preferences
            prefs = user_data[user_id]["preferences"]
            
            # Aggregate top preferences into a text
            top_tags = []
            for tag in prefs["tags"][-20:]:
                top_tags.append(tag["name"])
            
            if top_tags:
                pref_text = " ".join(top_tags)
                return embed(pref_text)
    
    # Default neutral vector
    return [0] * 1024

class PersonalizedSearchRequest(BaseModel):
    query: str
    user_id: str
    top_k: Optional[int] = 10

class PersonalizedSearchResponse(BaseModel):
    results: List[Dict]
    personalized: bool
    user_preferences: Dict

def calculate_personalized_score(result: Dict, user_vector: List[float], query_vector: List[float]) -> float:
    """Multi-signal ranking with personalization"""
    base_score = result["similarity"]
    
    # Personalization boost
    personalization = 0
    user_prefs = result.get("user_preferences", {})
    if user_prefs:
        # Boost if matches user preferences
        if user_prefs.get("match", False):
            personalization = 0.15
    
    # Booking history boost
    if result.get("booking_count", 0) > 0:
        personalization += min(0.1, result["booking_count"] * 0.02)
    
    return min(1.0, base_score + personalization)

@router.post("/api/personalized-search")
async def personalized_search(request: PersonalizedSearchRequest):
    """Search with personalization"""
    try:
        # Get query embedding
        query_embedding = embed(request.query)
        
        # Get user vector
        user_vector = get_user_vector(request.user_id)
        
        # Blend query with user profile (70% query, 30% user)
        personalized_vector = [
            (query_embedding[i] * 0.7) + (user_vector[i] * 0.3)
            for i in range(len(query_embedding))
        ]
        
        # Vector search with personalized query
        results = collection.query(
            query_embeddings=[personalized_vector],
            n_results=request.top_k,
            include=["documents", "metadatas", "distances"]
        )
        
        # Format and rank results
        ranked_results = []
        for i in range(len(results["ids"][0])):
            metadata = results["metadatas"][0][i]
            similarity = 1 - results["distances"][0][i]
            
            # Check if matches user preferences
            user_prefs = {
                "match": False,
                "matched_tags": []
            }
            
            # Simple matching logic
            if request.user_id:
                # Load user preferences
                import json
                import os
                user_file = "user_profiles.json"
                if os.path.exists(user_file):
                    with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
                        user_data = json.load(f)
                    
                    if request.user_id in user_data:
                        prefs = user_data[request.user_id]["preferences"]
                        user_tags = [t["name"] for t in prefs["tags"][-20:]]
                        restaurant_tags = metadata.get("tags", [])
                        
                        matches = set(user_tags) & set(restaurant_tags)
                        if matches:
                            user_prefs["match"] = True
                            user_prefs["matched_tags"] = list(matches)
            
            result = {
                "id": results["ids"][0][i],
                "name": metadata["name"],
                "cuisine": metadata["cuisine"],
                "rating": metadata["rating"],
                "price": metadata["price"],
                "vibe": metadata["vibe"],
                "availability": metadata["availability"],
                "location": metadata["location"],
                "tags": metadata["tags"],
                "similarity": similarity,
                "user_preferences": user_prefs,
                "personalized_score": calculate_personalized_score({
                    "similarity": similarity,
                    "user_preferences": user_prefs
                }, user_vector, query_embedding)
            }
            
            ranked_results.append(result)
        
        # Sort by personalized score
        ranked_results.sort(key=lambda x: x["personalized_score"], reverse=True)
        
        # Get user preferences summary
        user_prefs_summary = {}
        if request.user_id:
            import json
            import os
            user_file = "user_profiles.json"
            if os.path.exists(user_file):
                with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
                    user_data = json.load(f)
                
                if request.user_id in user_data:
                    prefs = user_data[request.user_id]["preferences"]
                    user_prefs_summary = {
                        "topTags": list(set([t["name"] for t in prefs["tags"][-20:]])),
                        "totalBookings": len([h for h in user_data[request.user_id]["history"] if h["action"]["type"] == "BOOKING"])
                    }
        
        return PersonalizedSearchResponse(
            results=ranked_results,
            personalized=any(user_vector),
            user_preferences=user_prefs_summary
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Personalized search error: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
🎬 4️⃣ PERSONALIZED UI COMPONENTS
tsx
// components/landing/PersonalizedHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore, initUserProfile } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function PersonalizedHero() {
  const { profile, getPreferencesForUI, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  const { setIntent, setMood } = useSufiStore()
  const { performSearch, isSearching } = useVectorSearch()
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState('')
  
  // Initialize profile on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    initUserProfile()
  }, [])
  
  // Get personalized copy based on user preferences
  const preferences = getPreferencesForUI()
  
  // Update mood based on preferences
  useEffect(() => {
    if (preferences.mood) {
      setMood(preferences.mood as any)
    }
  }, [preferences.mood, setMood])
  
  const getPersonalizedHeadline = () => {
    if (preferences.topVibes.length > 0) {
      const vibe = preferences.topVibes[0]
      if (vibe === 'romantic') return 'Find your perfect romantic evening'
      if (vibe === 'cozy') return 'Discover cozy spots you\'ll love'
      if (vibe === 'fast') return 'Quick, smart dining recommendations'
      if (vibe === 'upscale') return 'Experience exceptional dining'
    }
    return 'Find your next perfect meal'
  }
  
  const getPersonalizedSubtitle = () => {
    if (profile?.totalBookings && profile.totalBookings > 0) {
      return `Welcome back! Based on your ${profile.totalBookings} previous bookings, we've personalized your experience.`
    }
    return 'AI-powered discovery that learns your taste'
  }
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim()) return
    
    // Track search action
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: inputValue,
      tags: inputValue.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    await performSearch(inputValue)
  }
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md">
          {profile?.totalBookings ? `🎯 Personalized • ${profile.totalBookings} bookings` : '🧠 Learning your taste'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-green-500 rounded-full animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">PERSONALIZED SEARCH</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">
              {profile?.totalSearches || 0} searches • {profile?.totalBookings || 0} bookings
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {getPersonalizedHeadline()}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">personalized for you</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {getPersonalizedSubtitle()}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={preferences.topVibes.length > 0 ? 
                `${preferences.topVibes[0]} dinner with wine...` : 
                "romantic dinner with wine, rooftop sushi..."}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={isSearching}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {isSearching ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        {/* Personalized suggestions based on history */}
        {preferences.topCuisines.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-4 flex justify-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Based on your taste:</span>
            {preferences.topCuisines.map(cuisine => (
              <button
                key={cuisine}
                onClick={() => {
                  setInputValue(`${cuisine} restaurants`)
                  setTimeout(() => handleSearch(new Event('submit') as any), 100)
                }}
                className="px-3 py-1 glass-panel rounded-full text-xs hover:bg-white/10 transition-all"
              >
                {cuisine}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={preferences.mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {preferences.mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic mode active' : 
             preferences.mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick mode' : 
             preferences.mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury mode' : 
             '🎯 Personalized results'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 5️⃣ PERSONALIZED DISCOVERY
tsx
// components/landing/PersonalizedDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function PersonalizedDiscovery() {
  const { searchResults, performSearch } = useVectorSearch()
  const { profile, trackAction, getPreferencesForUI } = useUserProfileStore()
  const { intent } = useSufiStore()
  const [showResults, setShowResults] = useState(false)
  const [personalizedMessage, setPersonalizedMessage] = useState('')
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (intent && intent !== "romantic dinner") {
      performSearch(intent)
      setShowResults(true)
    }
  }, [intent, performSearch])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    // Generate personalized message based on preferences
    const prefs = getPreferencesForUI()
    if (prefs.topVibes.length > 0) {
      setPersonalizedMessage(`Based on your ${prefs.topVibes[0]} preference`)
    } else if (profile?.totalBookings && profile.totalBookings > 0) {
      setPersonalizedMessage(`Based on your ${profile.totalBookings} previous bookings`)
    } else {
      setPersonalizedMessage('AI-powered recommendations')
    }
  }, [profile, getPreferencesForUI])
  
  const handleRestaurantClick = (restaurant: any) => {
    trackAction({
      type: 'CLICK',
      restaurantId: restaurant.id,
      tags: restaurant.tags
    })
  }
  
  const getPersonalizedBadge = (restaurant: any) => {
    const prefs = getPreferencesForUI()
    if (prefs.topVibes.includes(restaurant.vibe?.toLowerCase())) {
      return <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full">Matches your vibe</span>
    }
    if (prefs.topCuisines.includes(restaurant.cuisine?.toLowerCase())) {
      return <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-primary/20 text-primary rounded-full">You like {restaurant.cuisine}</span>
    }
    return null
  }
  
  const displayResults = showResults && searchResults.length > 0 ? searchResults : []
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">PERSONALIZED DISCOVERY</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Results tailored to you"
              subtitle={personalizedMessage}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">🎯 How it works</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2">
                Every click, search, and booking teaches the system about your preferences.
                Your results improve over time.
              </p>
              {profile?.totalBookings && profile.totalBookings > 0 && (
                <div className="mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-white/10">
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Your activity:</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-primary">{profile.totalBookings} bookings • {profile.totalSearches} searches</p>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            {displayResults.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {displayResults.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => (
                  <GlassPanel 
                    key={rest.id} 
                    hover 
                    padding="md" 
                    className={i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''}
                    onClick={() => handleRestaurantClick(rest)}
                  >
                    <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                      <div>
                        <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                          {rest.name === 'Sky Lounge' ? '🌆' : 
                           rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                           rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : '🍽️'}
                        </div>
                        <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                        <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-4">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                        <span>Personalized match</span>
                        <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.personalized_score * 100)}%</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full" 
                             style={{ width: `${rest.personalized_score * 100}%` }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1 items-center">
                      {getPersonalizedBadge(rest)}
                      {rest.user_preferences?.matched_tags?.map((tag: string) => (
                        <span key={tag} className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full">
                          {tag}
                        </span>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    
                    {rest.user_preferences?.match && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-green-400 mt-2">✓ Based on your taste</p>
                    )}
                  </GlassPanel>
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="glass-panel p-12 text-center">
                <p className="text-white/40">Start searching to see personalized results</p>
                <div className="mt-4 flex justify-center gap-2">
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"romantic dinner"</Badge>
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"sushi omakase"</Badge>
                  <Badge variant="secondary">"quick lunch"</Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 6️⃣ PERSONALIZED AI CONCIERGE
tsx
// components/landing/PersonalizedAI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function PersonalizedAI() {
  const { profile, getPreferencesForUI, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  const { getAIResponse, aiResponse, isAILoading } = useVectorSearch()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  const preferences = getPreferencesForUI()
  
  // Personalized welcome message based on user history
  useEffect(() => {
    if (profile?.totalBookings && profile.totalBookings > 0) {
      setMessages([
        { 
          id: 1, 
          type: 'ai', 
          content: `Welcome back! I see you've booked ${profile.totalBookings} restaurants before. Based on your taste for ${preferences.topVibes[0] || 'great'} experiences, what are you in the mood for today?` 
        }
      ])
    } else {
      setMessages([
        { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: "Hi! I'm your personalized AI concierge. Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find restaurants that match your taste." }
      ])
    }
  }, [profile?.totalBookings])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (aiResponse && aiResponse.message) {
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { 
        id: prev.length + 1, 
        type: 'ai', 
        content: aiResponse.message,
        recommendations: aiResponse.recommendations
      }])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }
  }, [aiResponse])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping || isAILoading) return
    
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: input,
      tags: input.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    getAIResponse(userInput)
  }
  
  const getPersonalizedTone = () => {
    if (preferences.topVibes.includes('romantic')) return '❤️ Romantic Concierge'
    if (preferences.topVibes.includes('fast')) return '⚡ Quick Finder'
    if (preferences.topVibes.includes('luxury')) return '✨ Elite Concierge'
    return '🎯 Personalized AI'
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">{getPersonalizedTone()}</span>
                  <Badge variant="primary" size="sm">personalized</Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {msg.recommendations && msg.recommendations.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                          <p className="text-xs text-white/60">Personalized picks:</p>
                          {msg.recommendations.slice(0, 3).map((rec: any) => (
                            <div 
                              key={rec.id} 
                              className="bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all"
                              onClick={() => trackAction({ type: 'CLICK', restaurantId: rec.id, tags: rec.tags })}
                            >
                              <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                                <div>
                                  <p className="font-medium text-sm">{rec.name}</p>
                                  <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{rec.cuisine} • {rec.vibe}</p>
                                </div>
                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                  <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rec.rating}</span>
                                  <button className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg">
                                    Book
                                  </button>
                                </div>
                              </div>
                              {rec.user_preferences?.match && (
                                <p className="text-[10px] text-green-400 mt-1">✓ Matches your taste</p>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder={preferences.topVibes.length > 0 ? 
                      `Find a ${preferences.topVibes[0]} place...` : 
                      "Find a restaurant..."}
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping || isAILoading} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  Personalized with your taste • {profile?.totalSearches || 0} searches analyzed
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">PERSONALIZED AI</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Your taste, remembered"
              subtitle="Every conversation improves recommendations"
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">🧠 YOUR PROFILE</p>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/40">Bookings</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{profile?.totalBookings || 0}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/40">Searches</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{profile?.totalSearches || 0}</span>
                </div>
                {preferences.topVibes.length > 0 && (
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-1">Your vibe</p>
                    <div className="flex gap-2">
                      {preferences.topVibes.map(vibe => (
                        <Badge key={vibe} variant="tertiary" size="sm">{vibe}</Badge>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                {preferences.topCuisines.length > 0 && (
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-1">Favorite cuisines</p>
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                      {preferences.topCuisines.map(cuisine => (
                        <Badge key={cuisine} variant="secondary" size="sm">{cuisine}</Badge>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-primary/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                  <span>🔄</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">Feedback loop active</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Every interaction makes SUFI smarter</p>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-2 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full w-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary rounded-full animate-pulse" 
                         style={{ width: `${Math.min(100, (profile?.totalBookings || 0) * 5 + 50)}%` }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
