🌍 1️⃣ GLOBAL TREND TRACKING SYSTEM
python
# backend/global_trends.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, WebSocket, WebSocketDisconnect
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import asyncio
import json
from collections import defaultdict
import numpy as np

router = APIRouter()

# In-memory trend storage (replace with Redis/PostgreSQL in production)
class GlobalTrendTracker:
    def __init__(self):
        self.restaurant_metrics = defaultdict(lambda: {
            "search_count": 0,
            "click_count": 0,
            "booking_count": 0,
            "hourly_bookings": defaultdict(int),
            "last_updated": datetime.now()
        })
        self.global_metrics = {
            "total_searches": 0,
            "total_bookings": 0,
            "peak_hour": None,
            "trending_score": 0
        }
        self.recent_actions = []
        self.active_websockets = []
    
    def track_action(self, action: Dict):
        """Track user action and update metrics"""
        restaurant_id = action.get("restaurant_id")
        action_type = action.get("type")
        timestamp = datetime.fromisoformat(action.get("timestamp", datetime.now().isoformat()))
        
        self.recent_actions.append({
            **action,
            "timestamp": timestamp.isoformat()
        })
        
        # Keep last 10,000 actions for trend calculation
        if len(self.recent_actions) > 10000:
            self.recent_actions = self.recent_actions[-10000:]
        
        if restaurant_id:
            metrics = self.restaurant_metrics[restaurant_id]
            
            if action_type == "SEARCH":
                metrics["search_count"] += 1
            elif action_type == "CLICK":
                metrics["click_count"] += 1
            elif action_type == "BOOKING":
                metrics["booking_count"] += 1
                hour_key = timestamp.strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:00")
                metrics["hourly_bookings"][hour_key] += 1
                
                # Update global metrics
                self.global_metrics["total_bookings"] += 1
            
            metrics["last_updated"] = timestamp
        
        if action_type == "SEARCH":
            self.global_metrics["total_searches"] += 1
        
        # Calculate peak hour
        self._update_peak_hour()
        
        # Update trending score
        self._update_trending_score()
        
        # Broadcast to all connected websockets
        asyncio.create_task(self.broadcast_update())
    
    def _update_peak_hour(self):
        """Calculate current peak booking hour"""
        current_hour = datetime.now().hour
        hourly_counts = defaultdict(int)
        
        for action in self.recent_actions:
            if action.get("type") == "BOOKING":
                ts = datetime.fromisoformat(action["timestamp"])
                hourly_counts[ts.hour] += 1
        
        if hourly_counts:
            self.global_metrics["peak_hour"] = max(hourly_counts, key=hourly_counts.get)
    
    def _update_trending_score(self):
        """Calculate global trending score based on recent activity"""
        recent_bookings = sum(
            1 for action in self.recent_actions[-1000:]
            if action.get("type") == "BOOKING" and 
            datetime.fromisoformat(action["timestamp"]) > datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=1)
        )
        
        # Normalize to 0-1 range (max expected 100 bookings/hour)
        self.global_metrics["trending_score"] = min(1.0, recent_bookings / 100)
    
    def get_trend_score(self, restaurant_id: str) -> float:
        """Calculate normalized trend score for a restaurant"""
        metrics = self.restaurant_metrics.get(restaurant_id, {})
        
        if not metrics:
            return 0.0
        
        # Get counts with normalization
        search_count = min(1.0, metrics.get("search_count", 0) / 1000)
        click_count = min(1.0, metrics.get("click_count", 0) / 500)
        booking_count = min(1.0, metrics.get("booking_count", 0) / 100)
        
        # Calculate hourly trend
        current_hour = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:00")
        hourly_bookings = metrics.get("hourly_bookings", {}).get(current_hour, 0)
        hourly_trend = min(1.0, hourly_bookings / 20)
        
        # Weighted formula
        trend_score = (
            0.3 * search_count +
            0.2 * click_count +
            0.3 * booking_count +
            0.2 * hourly_trend
        )
        
        return min(1.0, trend_score)
    
    def get_global_metrics(self) -> Dict:
        """Get global platform metrics"""
        return {
            "total_searches": self.global_metrics["total_searches"],
            "total_bookings": self.global_metrics["total_bookings"],
            "peak_hour": self.global_metrics["peak_hour"],
            "trending_score": self.global_metrics["trending_score"],
            "active_users": len(set(
                a.get("user_id") for a in self.recent_actions[-1000:]
                if datetime.fromisoformat(a["timestamp"]) > datetime.now() - timedelta(minutes=5)
            ))
        }
    
    def get_top_trending(self, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict]:
        """Get top trending restaurants"""
        restaurants = []
        for restaurant_id in self.restaurant_metrics.keys():
            score = self.get_trend_score(restaurant_id)
            if score > 0:
                restaurants.append({
                    "restaurant_id": restaurant_id,
                    "trend_score": score
                })
        
        restaurants.sort(key=lambda x: x["trend_score"], reverse=True)
        return restaurants[:limit]
    
    async def broadcast_update(self):
        """Broadcast trend updates to all connected websockets"""
        data = {
            "type": "trend_update",
            "global_metrics": self.get_global_metrics(),
            "top_trending": self.get_top_trending(5),
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        
        for ws in self.active_websockets:
            try:
                await ws.send_json(data)
            except:
                pass  # Remove dead connections in cleanup

# Global instance
trend_tracker = GlobalTrendTracker()

# WebSocket manager
class ConnectionManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.active_connections: List[WebSocket] = []
    
    async def connect(self, websocket: WebSocket):
        await websocket.accept()
        self.active_connections.append(websocket)
        trend_tracker.active_websockets.append(websocket)
    
    def disconnect(self, websocket: WebSocket):
        if websocket in self.active_connections:
            self.active_connections.remove(websocket)
        if websocket in trend_tracker.active_websockets:
            trend_tracker.active_websockets.remove(websocket)
    
    async def broadcast(self, message: str):
        for connection in self.active_connections:
            try:
                await connection.send_text(message)
            except:
                pass

manager = ConnectionManager()

# API Endpoints
@router.post("/api/global/track")
async def track_global_action(action: Dict):
    """Track user action for global metrics"""
    trend_tracker.track_action(action)
    return {"status": "success"}

@router.get("/api/global/metrics")
async def get_global_metrics():
    """Get current global platform metrics"""
    return trend_tracker.get_global_metrics()

@router.get("/api/global/trending")
async def get_trending(limit: int = 10):
    """Get top trending restaurants"""
    return trend_tracker.get_top_trending(limit)

@router.get("/api/global/trend-score/{restaurant_id}")
async def get_restaurant_trend(restaurant_id: str):
    """Get trend score for specific restaurant"""
    return {
        "restaurant_id": restaurant_id,
        "trend_score": trend_tracker.get_trend_score(restaurant_id)
    }

@router.websocket("/ws/trends")
async def websocket_trends(websocket: WebSocket):
    """WebSocket for real-time trend updates"""
    await manager.connect(websocket)
    try:
        while True:
            # Keep connection alive
            await websocket.receive_text()
    except WebSocketDisconnect:
        manager.disconnect(websocket)
🧠 2️⃣ COMBINED RANKING ENGINE
python
# backend/ranking_engine.py
from typing import List, Dict, Any
import numpy as np

class RankingEngine:
    def __init__(self, trend_tracker):
        self.trend_tracker = trend_tracker
        
    def calculate_final_score(
        self,
        similarity: float,
        user_preference_score: float,
        restaurant_id: str,
        user_booking_count: int = 0
    ) -> float:
        """
        Calculate final ranking score combining:
        - Semantic similarity (embedding match)
        - User preference (personal history)
        - Global trend (real-time popularity)
        """
        
        # Get global trend score
        trend_score = self.trend_tracker.get_trend_score(restaurant_id)
        
        # User engagement boost (based on bookings)
        user_boost = min(0.15, user_booking_count * 0.03)
        
        # Final weighted score
        final_score = (
            0.5 * similarity +           # Semantic relevance
            0.2 * user_preference_score + # Personal taste
            0.2 * trend_score +           # Global popularity
            0.1 * user_boost              # User engagement
        )
        
        return min(1.0, final_score)
    
    def rank_results(
        self,
        results: List[Dict],
        user_id: str = None,
        user_preferences: Dict = None
    ) -> List[Dict]:
        """Rank search results with combined scoring"""
        ranked = []
        
        # Load user profile if available
        user_booking_counts = {}
        if user_id:
            import json
            import os
            user_file = "user_profiles.json"
            if os.path.exists(user_file):
                with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
                    user_data = json.load(f)
                    if user_id in user_data:
                        for action in user_data[user_id]["history"]:
                            if action["action"]["type"] == "BOOKING":
                                rid = action["action"].get("restaurant_id")
                                if rid:
                                    user_booking_counts[rid] = user_booking_counts.get(rid, 0) + 1
        
        for result in results:
            restaurant_id = result.get("id")
            similarity = result.get("similarity", 0.5)
            
            # Calculate user preference score
            user_preference_score = 0.5  # Default neutral
            if user_preferences:
                # Match restaurant tags with user preferences
                tags = result.get("tags", [])
                matches = 0
                for tag in tags:
                    if tag in user_preferences.get("topTags", []):
                        matches += 1
                if tags:
                    user_preference_score = 0.5 + (matches / len(tags)) * 0.3
            
            # Get user booking count for this restaurant
            user_booking_count = user_booking_counts.get(restaurant_id, 0)
            
            final_score = self.calculate_final_score(
                similarity=similarity,
                user_preference_score=user_preference_score,
                restaurant_id=restaurant_id,
                user_booking_count=user_booking_count
            )
            
            result["similarity_score"] = similarity
            result["personal_score"] = user_preference_score
            result["trend_score"] = self.trend_tracker.get_trend_score(restaurant_id)
            result["final_score"] = final_score
            result["trending"] = result["trend_score"] > 0.7
            
            ranked.append(result)
        
        # Sort by final score
        ranked.sort(key=lambda x: x["final_score"], reverse=True)
        return ranked
🔍 3️⃣ INTEGRATED SEARCH API
python
# backend/integrated_search.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel
from typing import List, Optional
import requests
import chromadb
from .global_trends import trend_tracker
from .ranking_engine import RankingEngine

router = APIRouter()

# Initialize ChromaDB
client = chromadb.PersistentClient(path="./chroma_db")
collection = client.get_collection("restaurants")
ranking_engine = RankingEngine(trend_tracker)

def embed(text: str) -> List[float]:
    """Generate embedding using mxbai-embed-large"""
    response = requests.post(
        "http://localhost:11434/api/embeddings",
        json={"model": "mxbai-embed-large", "prompt": text}
    )
    return response.json()["embedding"]

def get_user_preferences(user_id: str) -> Dict:
    """Get user preferences from profile"""
    import json
    import os
    
    user_file = "user_profiles.json"
    if os.path.exists(user_file):
        with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
            user_data = json.load(f)
            if user_id in user_data:
                prefs = user_data[user_id]["preferences"]
                return {
                    "topTags": list(set([t["name"] for t in prefs["tags"][-20:]])),
                    "topCuisines": list(set([c["name"] for c in prefs["cuisines"][-10:]])),
                    "totalBookings": len([h for h in user_data[user_id]["history"] if h["action"]["type"] == "BOOKING"])
                }
    return {"topTags": [], "topCuisines": [], "totalBookings": 0}

class IntegratedSearchRequest(BaseModel):
    query: str
    user_id: Optional[str] = None
    top_k: Optional[int] = 10

class IntegratedSearchResponse(BaseModel):
    results: List[Dict]
    global_metrics: Dict
    personalized: bool
    trending_context: Dict

@router.post("/api/integrated-search")
async def integrated_search(request: IntegratedSearchRequest):
    """Search with combined personal + global intelligence"""
    try:
        # Get query embedding
        query_embedding = embed(request.query)
        
        # Get user preferences if available
        user_preferences = {}
        if request.user_id:
            user_preferences = get_user_preferences(request.user_id)
        
        # Get user vector for personalization
        user_vector = [0] * 1024
        if request.user_id:
            import json
            import os
            user_file = "user_profiles.json"
            if os.path.exists(user_file):
                with open(user_file, 'r') as f:
                    user_data = json.load(f)
                    if request.user_id in user_data:
                        # Build vector from user preferences
                        prefs = user_data[request.user_id]["preferences"]
                        top_tags = [t["name"] for t in prefs["tags"][-20:]]
                        if top_tags:
                            user_vector = embed(" ".join(top_tags))
        
        # Blend with user vector (70% query, 30% user)
        personalized_vector = [
            (query_embedding[i] * 0.7) + (user_vector[i] * 0.3)
            for i in range(len(query_embedding))
        ]
        
        # Vector search
        results = collection.query(
            query_embeddings=[personalized_vector],
            n_results=request.top_k,
            include=["documents", "metadatas", "distances"]
        )
        
        # Format results
        formatted_results = []
        for i in range(len(results["ids"][0])):
            metadata = results["metadatas"][0][i]
            formatted_results.append({
                "id": results["ids"][0][i],
                "name": metadata["name"],
                "cuisine": metadata["cuisine"],
                "rating": metadata["rating"],
                "price": metadata["price"],
                "vibe": metadata["vibe"],
                "availability": metadata["availability"],
                "location": metadata["location"],
                "tags": metadata["tags"],
                "similarity": 1 - results["distances"][0][i]
            })
        
        # Apply combined ranking
        ranked_results = ranking_engine.rank_results(
            formatted_results,
            user_id=request.user_id,
            user_preferences=user_preferences
        )
        
        # Get global context for response
        global_metrics = trend_tracker.get_global_metrics()
        top_trending = trend_tracker.get_top_trending(3)
        
        return IntegratedSearchResponse(
            results=ranked_results,
            global_metrics=global_metrics,
            personalized=bool(request.user_id and user_preferences.get("totalBookings", 0) > 0),
            trending_context={
                "trending_score": global_metrics["trending_score"],
                "peak_hour": global_metrics["peak_hour"],
                "active_users": global_metrics["active_users"],
                "top_trending": top_trending
            }
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Integrated search error: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
📊 4️⃣ GLOBAL TRENDS FRONTEND STORE
tsx
// lib/state/globalTrendsStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"

interface GlobalMetrics {
  total_searches: number
  total_bookings: number
  peak_hour: number
  trending_score: number
  active_users: number
}

interface TrendingRestaurant {
  restaurant_id: string
  trend_score: number
}

interface GlobalTrendsState {
  metrics: GlobalMetrics
  trending: TrendingRestaurant[]
  isConnected: boolean
  lastUpdate: Date | null
  
  updateMetrics: (metrics: GlobalMetrics) => void
  updateTrending: (trending: TrendingRestaurant[]) => void
  setConnected: (connected: boolean) => void
}

export const useGlobalTrendsStore = create<GlobalTrendsState>((set) => ({
  metrics: {
    total_searches: 0,
    total_bookings: 0,
    peak_hour: 0,
    trending_score: 0,
    active_users: 0
  },
  trending: [],
  isConnected: false,
  lastUpdate: null,
  
  updateMetrics: (metrics) => set({ metrics, lastUpdate: new Date() }),
  updateTrending: (trending) => set({ trending }),
  setConnected: (isConnected) => set({ isConnected })
}))
🔌 5️⃣ WEBSOCKET CONNECTION FOR REAL-TIME TRENDS
tsx
// lib/hooks/useGlobalTrends.ts
import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import { useGlobalTrendsStore } from '@/lib/state/globalTrendsStore'

export function useGlobalTrends() {
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null)
  const { updateMetrics, updateTrending, setConnected } = useGlobalTrendsStore()
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:8000/ws/trends')
    wsRef.current = ws
    
    ws.onopen = () => {
      console.log('Connected to trend updates')
      setConnected(true)
    }
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data)
      if (data.type === 'trend_update') {
        updateMetrics(data.global_metrics)
        updateTrending(data.top_trending)
      }
    }
    
    ws.onclose = () => {
      console.log('Disconnected from trend updates')
      setConnected(false)
      // Attempt to reconnect after 5 seconds
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (wsRef.current?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
          useGlobalTrends()
        }
      }, 5000)
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (wsRef.current) {
        wsRef.current.close()
      }
    }
  }, [])
  
  return useGlobalTrendsStore()
}
🎬 6️⃣ ADAPTIVE UI WITH GLOBAL TRENDS
tsx
// components/landing/GlobalHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useGlobalTrends } from '@/lib/hooks/useGlobalTrends'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function GlobalHero() {
  const { metrics, isConnected } = useGlobalTrends()
  const { performSearch, isSearching } = useVectorSearch()
  const { profile, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState('')
  const [liveMetric, setLiveMetric] = useState(0)
  
  // Animate live metric like Stripe's GDP counter
  useEffect(() => {
    if (metrics.total_bookings !== liveMetric) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveMetric }, {
        value: metrics.total_bookings,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveMetric(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [metrics.total_bookings, liveMetric])
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim()) return
    
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: inputValue,
      tags: inputValue.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    await performSearch(inputValue)
  }
  
  const getActivityMessage = () => {
    if (metrics.trending_score > 0.8) return '🔥 Peak activity right now'
    if (metrics.trending_score > 0.5) return '📈 High activity'
    if (metrics.active_users > 50) return `👥 ${metrics.active_users} active users`
    return '🧠 Global intelligence active'
  }
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md" variant={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
          {isConnected ? '🌍 Live Network' : '🔄 Connecting...'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse ${metrics.trending_score > 0.5 ? 'bg-tertiary' : 'bg-green-500'}`} />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">{getActivityMessage()}</span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{liveMetric.toLocaleString()} bookings</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          What's trending
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">right now</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {metrics.active_users > 0 
            ? `${metrics.active_users} people are exploring restaurants right now. ${liveMetric} bookings today.`
            : 'Real-time intelligence from thousands of diners.'}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? "What's trending tonight?" : "romantic dinner with wine..."}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={isSearching}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {isSearching ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        {/* Live activity indicator */}
        {metrics.trending_score > 0.5 && (
          <div className="mt-4 flex justify-center gap-2">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
              <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse" />
              <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Trending now</span>
            </div>
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">•</span>
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Peak at {metrics.peak_hour}:00</span>
          </div>
        )}
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥 Trending mode' : '📊 Real-time insights'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔥 7️⃣ TRENDING DISCOVERY COMPONENT
tsx
// components/landing/TrendingDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useGlobalTrends } from '@/lib/hooks/useGlobalTrends'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function TrendingDiscovery() {
  const { metrics, trending } = useGlobalTrends()
  const { searchResults, performSearch } = useVectorSearch()
  const { profile, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  const [showResults, setShowResults] = useState(false)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    // Auto-search trending query when trending score is high
    if (metrics.trending_score > 0.7 && !showResults) {
      performSearch("trending restaurants")
      setShowResults(true)
    }
  }, [metrics.trending_score, performSearch])
  
  const handleRestaurantClick = (restaurant: any) => {
    trackAction({
      type: 'CLICK',
      restaurantId: restaurant.id,
      tags: restaurant.tags
    })
  }
  
  const getTrendingBadge = (restaurant: any) => {
    const isTrending = trending.some(t => t.restaurant_id === restaurant.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
    if (isTrending) {
      return <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse">🔥 Trending</span>
    }
    return null
  }
  
  const displayResults = showResults && searchResults.length > 0 ? searchResults : []
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="tertiary">GLOBAL INTELLIGENCE</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? "What's trending now" : "Discover what's popular"}
              subtitle={`Based on ${metrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()} bookings and ${metrics.total_searches.toLocaleString()} searches`}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">📊 LIVE PLATFORM METRICS</p>
              <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span>Active users</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{metrics.active_users}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span>Today's bookings</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{metrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span>Trending score</span>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="w-24 h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                      <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                           style={{ width: `${metrics.trending_score * 100}%` }} />
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(metrics.trending_score * 100)}%</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                {metrics.peak_hour && (
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                    <span>Peak hour</span>
                    <span className="text-primary">{metrics.peak_hour}:00</span>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            {displayResults.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {displayResults.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => {
                  const isTrending = trending.some(t => t.restaurant_id === rest.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
                  return (
                    <GlassPanel 
                      key={rest.id} 
                      hover 
                      padding="md" 
                      className={`${i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''} ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/50' : ''}`}
                      onClick={() => handleRestaurantClick(rest)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                        <div>
                          <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                            {rest.name === 'Sky Lounge' ? '🌆' : 
                             rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                             rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : '🍽️'}
                          </div>
                          <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-4">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                          <span>Combined score</span>
                          <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.final_score * 100)}%</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                          <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                               style={{ width: `${rest.final_score * 100}%` }} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1 items-center">
                        {getTrendingBadge(rest)}
                        {rest.trend_score > 0.7 && (
                          <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full">
                            {Math.round(rest.trend_score * 100)}% trend score
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      
                      {isTrending && (
                        <div className="mt-2 flex items-center gap-1">
                          <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                          <p className="text-xs text-tertiary">Trending right now</p>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </GlassPanel>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="glass-panel p-12 text-center">
                <p className="text-white/40">Waiting for live activity...</p>
                {metrics.active_users > 0 && (
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2">{metrics.active_users} active users</p>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 8️⃣ GLOBAL AI CONCIERGE
tsx
// components/landing/GlobalAI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useGlobalTrends } from '@/lib/hooks/useGlobalTrends'
import { useVectorSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useVectorSearch'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function GlobalAI() {
  const { metrics, trending } = useGlobalTrends()
  const { getAIResponse, aiResponse, isAILoading } = useVectorSearch()
  const { profile, getPreferencesForUI, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  const preferences = getPreferencesForUI()
  
  // Welcome message with global context
  useEffect(() => {
    const trendMessage = metrics.trending_score > 0.7 
      ? `🔥 Right now, ${metrics.active_users} people are exploring restaurants. ${trending.length} spots are trending!`
      : `📊 Currently ${metrics.active_users} active users on SUFI.`
    
    if (profile?.totalBookings && profile.totalBookings > 0) {
      setMessages([
        { 
          id: 1, 
          type: 'ai', 
          content: `Welcome back! ${trendMessage} Based on your ${profile.totalBookings} previous bookings, what are you in the mood for today?` 
        }
      ])
    } else {
      setMessages([
        { id: 1, type: 'ai', content: `Hi! I'm SUFI AI. ${trendMessage} Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find the best options — personalized and trending.` }
      ])
    }
  }, [profile?.totalBookings, metrics.active_users, metrics.trending_score, trending.length])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (aiResponse && aiResponse.message) {
      // Enhance AI response with global context if trending
      let finalMessage = aiResponse.message
      if (metrics.trending_score > 0.7 && !finalMessage.includes('trending')) {
        finalMessage = `🔥 These are trending right now! ${finalMessage}`
      }
      
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { 
        id: prev.length + 1, 
        type: 'ai', 
        content: finalMessage,
        recommendations: aiResponse.recommendations
      }])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }
  }, [aiResponse, metrics.trending_score])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping || isAILoading) return
    
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: input,
      tags: input.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    getAIResponse(userInput)
  }
  
  const getAIPersonality = () => {
    if (metrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Trendspotter AI'
    if (preferences.topVibes.includes('romantic')) return '❤️ Romantic Concierge'
    if (preferences.topVibes.includes('fast')) return '⚡ Quick Finder'
    return '🌍 Global Intelligence'
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🌍</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">{getAIPersonality()}</span>
                  <Badge variant={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'} size="sm">
                    {metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'trending mode' : 'global insights'}
                  </Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {msg.recommendations && msg.recommendations.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                          <p className="text-xs text-white/60">Top picks:</p>
                          {msg.recommendations.slice(0, 3).map((rec: any) => {
                            const isTrending = trending.some(t => t.restaurant_id === rec.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
                            return (
                              <div 
                                key={rec.id} 
                                className={`bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/30' : ''}`}
                                onClick={() => trackAction({ type: 'CLICK', restaurantId: rec.id, tags: rec.tags })}
                              >
                                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                                  <div>
                                    <p className="font-medium text-sm">{rec.name}</p>
                                    <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{rec.cuisine} • {rec.vibe}</p>
                                  </div>
                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rec.rating}</span>
                                    <button className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg">
                                      Book
                                    </button>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                                {isTrending && (
                                  <p className="text-[10px] text-tertiary mt-1">🔥 Trending now</p>
                                )}
                              </div>
                            )
                          })}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder={metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? "What's trending right now?" : "Find a restaurant..."}
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping || isAILoading} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  {metrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                    ? `🔥 ${metrics.active_users} active users • ${trending.length} trending spots`
                    : `🌍 ${metrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()} bookings today`}
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">GLOBAL INTELLIGENCE</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Live from the network"
              subtitle="Real-time insights from thousands of diners"
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">🌍 LIVE PLATFORM</p>
              <div className="space-y-3">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/40">Total bookings today</span>
                  <span className="text-primary font-mono">{metrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/40">Total searches</span>
                  <span className="text-primary font-mono">{metrics.total_searches.toLocaleString()}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-sm">
                  <span className="text-white/40">Active users</span>
                  <span className="text-primary font-mono">{metrics.active_users}</span>
                </div>
                {trending.length > 0 && (
                  <div className="pt-2 border-t border-white/10">
                    <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mb-2">🔥 Trending now</p>
                    <div className="space-y-1">
                      {trending.slice(0, 3).map(t => (
                        <div key={t.restaurant_id} className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                          <span>Restaurant {t.restaurant_id}</span>
                          <span className="text-tertiary">{Math.round(t.trend_score * 100)}%</span>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'bg-tertiary/20 animate-pulse' : 'bg-primary/20'}`}>
                  <span>{metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥' : '🌍'}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">
                    {metrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'Trending mode active' : 'Global intelligence'}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">
                    {metrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                      ? `${Math.round(metrics.trending_score * 100)}% activity spike`
                      : 'Real-time network insights'}
                  </p>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-2 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                         style={{ width: `${metrics.trending_score * 100}%` }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}

🎯 WHAT YOU NOW HAVE
Layer	Components
Personal Intelligence	User vectors, preferences, booking history
Global Intelligence	Real-time trends, aggregated metrics, WebSocket streaming
Combined Ranking	50% similarity + 20% personal + 30% global
Live Metrics	Active users, bookings, trending score (Stripe-style counter)
Trending Detection	Real-time popularity scoring
Adaptive UI	Hero changes with activity, trending badges, live counters
WebSocket Updates	Continuous trend updates to all clients
Global AI	Context-aware responses with trending context
🔥 SUFI is now a complete intelligence network: personal taste + global trends + real-time updates + adaptive UI. Every user sees what's trending, and the system evolves with every interaction.

🧠 1️⃣ UNIFIED GLOBAL STATE
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware"

export type Mood = 'neutral' | 'romantic' | 'fast' | 'luxury'

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  location: string
  tags: string[]
  similarity: number
  personal_score: number
  trend_score: number
  final_score: number
  trending: boolean
}

export interface GlobalMetrics {
  total_searches: number
  total_bookings: number
  peak_hour: number
  trending_score: number
  active_users: number
}

interface SufiState {
  // User state
  intent: string
  mood: Mood
  userVector: number[]
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: string[]
    topVibes: string[]
    totalBookings: number
  }
  
  // Search results
  searchResults: Restaurant[]
  bestMatch: Restaurant | null
  isSearching: boolean
  
  // Global trends
  globalMetrics: GlobalMetrics
  trendingRestaurants: { restaurant_id: string; trend_score: number }[]
  isConnected: boolean
  
  // UI state
  activeSection: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner'
  selectedRestaurant: Restaurant | null
  
  // Actions
  setIntent: (intent: string) => void
  setMood: (mood: Mood) => void
  setSearchResults: (results: Restaurant[]) => void
  setBestMatch: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  setIsSearching: (isSearching: boolean) => void
  updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics: GlobalMetrics) => void
  updateTrending: (trending: { restaurant_id: string; trend_score: number }[]) => void
  setConnected: (connected: boolean) => void
  setActiveSection: (section: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner') => void
  selectRestaurant: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  updateUserPreferences: (preferences: Partial<SufiState['userPreferences']>) => void
  reset: () => void
}

const initialState = {
  intent: "romantic dinner",
  mood: "neutral" as Mood,
  userVector: new Array(1024).fill(0),
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: [],
    topVibes: [],
    totalBookings: 0
  },
  searchResults: [],
  bestMatch: null,
  isSearching: false,
  globalMetrics: {
    total_searches: 0,
    total_bookings: 0,
    peak_hour: 0,
    trending_score: 0,
    active_users: 0
  },
  trendingRestaurants: [],
  isConnected: false,
  activeSection: 'hero' as const,
  selectedRestaurant: null
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      ...initialState,
      
      setIntent: (intent) => {
        set({ intent })
        // Auto-detect mood from intent
        const lowerIntent = intent.toLowerCase()
        if (lowerIntent.includes('romantic') || lowerIntent.includes('date') || lowerIntent.includes('cozy')) {
          set({ mood: 'romantic' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('quick') || lowerIntent.includes('fast') || lowerIntent.includes('business')) {
          set({ mood: 'fast' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('luxury') || lowerIntent.includes('fine dining') || lowerIntent.includes('michelin')) {
          set({ mood: 'luxury' })
        }
      },
      
      setMood: (mood) => set({ mood }),
      
      setSearchResults: (results) => {
        const bestMatch = results.length > 0 ? results[0] : null
        set({ searchResults: results, bestMatch })
      },
      
      setBestMatch: (bestMatch) => set({ bestMatch }),
      
      setIsSearching: (isSearching) => set({ isSearching }),
      
      updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics) => set({ globalMetrics: metrics }),
      
      updateTrending: (trending) => set({ trendingRestaurants: trending }),
      
      setConnected: (isConnected) => set({ isConnected }),
      
      setActiveSection: (activeSection) => set({ activeSection }),
      
      selectRestaurant: (selectedRestaurant) => set({ selectedRestaurant }),
      
      updateUserPreferences: (preferences) => set((state) => ({
        userPreferences: { ...state.userPreferences, ...preferences }
      })),
      
      reset: () => set(initialState)
    }),
    {
      name: 'sufi-unified-state',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        intent: state.intent,
        mood: state.mood,
        userPreferences: state.userPreferences,
        globalMetrics: state.globalMetrics
      })
    }
  )
)
🎬 2️⃣ UNIFIED HERO (DRIVES THE SYSTEM)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUnifiedSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function UnifiedHero() {
  const { 
    intent, setIntent, mood, globalMetrics, isConnected, 
    setActiveSection, setIsSearching 
  } = useSufiStore()
  const { performSearch, isSearching } = useUnifiedSearch()
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState(intent)
  const [liveMetric, setLiveMetric] = useState(0)
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  
  // Animate live metric like Stripe
  useEffect(() => {
    if (globalMetrics.total_bookings !== liveMetric) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveMetric }, {
        value: globalMetrics.total_bookings,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveMetric(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [globalMetrics.total_bookings, liveMetric])
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim() || isSearching) return
    
    // THIS DRIVES THE ENTIRE SYSTEM
    setIntent(inputValue)
    setIsSearching(true)
    setActiveSection('discovery')
    
    await performSearch(inputValue)
  }
  
  // Auto-focus input
  useEffect(() => {
    inputRef.current?.focus()
  }, [])
  
  const getHeroCopy = () => {
    switch(mood) {
      case 'romantic':
        return {
          title: "Create the",
          highlight: "perfect evening",
          subtitle: "Discover intimate spots for unforgettable moments"
        }
      case 'fast':
        return {
          title: "Quick. Smart.",
          highlight: "Instant booking",
          subtitle: "Find available tables near you in seconds"
        }
      case 'luxury':
        return {
          title: "Experience",
          highlight: "exceptional dining",
          subtitle: "Curated selections for discerning palates"
        }
      default:
        return {
          title: "Find your next",
          highlight: "perfect meal",
          subtitle: "AI-powered discovery that learns your taste"
        }
    }
  }
  
  const copy = getHeroCopy()
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md" variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
          {isConnected ? `🌍 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active` : '🔄 connecting...'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse ${globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.5 ? 'bg-tertiary' : 'bg-green-500'}`} />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">
              {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥 Trending mode' : '🎯 Personal AI'}
            </span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{liveMetric.toLocaleString()} bookings</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {copy.title}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">{copy.highlight}</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {copy.subtitle}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              ref={inputRef}
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={intent}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={isSearching}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {isSearching ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic mode' : 
             mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick mode' : 
             mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury mode' : '🎯 Personalized'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 3️⃣ UNIFIED DISCOVERY (REAL RANKING)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function UnifiedDiscovery() {
  const { 
    searchResults, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, trendingRestaurants,
    setActiveSection, selectRestaurant
  } = useSufiStore()
  
  // Animate cards when results update
  useEffect(() => {
    if (searchResults.length > 0) {
      gsap.fromTo('.result-card', 
        { opacity: 0, y: 30 },
        { opacity: 1, y: 0, duration: 0.4, stagger: 0.05 }
      )
    }
  }, [searchResults])
  
  const getRankingMessage = () => {
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '✨ Sorted by ambiance & romantic vibe'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Sorted by availability'
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Sorted by trending popularity'
    return '🎯 Sorted by personalized relevance'
  }
  
  const getTrendingBadge = (restaurant: any) => {
    const isTrending = trendingRestaurants.some(t => t.restaurant_id === restaurant.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
    if (isTrending) {
      return <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse">🔥 Trending</span>
    }
    return null
  }
  
  const handleCardClick = (restaurant: any) => {
    selectRestaurant(restaurant)
    setActiveSection('ai')
  }
  
  const displayResults = searchResults.length > 0 ? searchResults : []
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">INTELLIGENT RANKING</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={mood === 'romantic' ? "Perfect ambiance" : 
                     mood === 'fast' ? "Available now" : 
                     "Personalized for you"}
              subtitle={getRankingMessage()}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">📊 RANKING SIGNALS</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Semantic match</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">50% weight</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Personal taste</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">20% weight</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Global trends</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">30% weight</span>
                </div>
                {bestMatch && (
                  <div className="pt-2 mt-2 border-t border-white/10">
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-400">✨ Best match: {bestMatch.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">
                      {Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance
                    </p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            {displayResults.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {displayResults.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => {
                  const isBestMatch = bestMatch?.id === rest.id
                  const isTrending = trendingRestaurants.some(t => t.restaurant_id === rest.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
                  
                  return (
                    <GlassPanel 
                      key={rest.id} 
                      hover 
                      padding="md" 
                      className={`result-card ${i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''} ${isBestMatch ? 'ring-2 ring-primary' : ''} ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/50' : ''} cursor-pointer`}
                      onClick={() => handleCardClick(rest)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                        <div>
                          <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                            {rest.name === 'Sky Lounge' ? '🌆' : 
                             rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                             rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : '🍽️'}
                          </div>
                          <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-4">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                          <span>Combined score</span>
                          <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.final_score * 100)}%</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                          <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                               style={{ width: `${rest.final_score * 100}%` }} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1 items-center">
                        {getTrendingBadge(rest)}
                        {isBestMatch && (
                          <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-primary/20 text-primary rounded-full">
                            Best match
                          </span>
                        )}
                        {rest.trend_score > 0.7 && (
                          <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full">
                            {Math.round(rest.trend_score * 100)}% trend
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      
                      {isTrending && (
                        <div className="mt-2 flex items-center gap-1">
                          <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                          <p className="text-xs text-tertiary">Trending right now</p>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </GlassPanel>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="glass-panel p-12 text-center">
                <p className="text-white/40">Search to see intelligent rankings</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2">Personal + global signals combined</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ UNIFIED AI (REAL CONTEXT)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedAI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUnifiedSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function UnifiedAI() {
  const { 
    intent, searchResults, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, 
    userPreferences, selectedRestaurant, setActiveSection 
  } = useSufiStore()
  const { getAIResponse, aiResponse, isAILoading } = useUnifiedSearch()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  // Generate welcome message based on current state
  useEffect(() => {
    let welcomeMessage = ""
    
    if (selectedRestaurant) {
      welcomeMessage = `I see you're interested in ${selectedRestaurant.name}. It has ${selectedRestaurant.rating}★ and is known for ${selectedRestaurant.vibe} dining. Would you like to know more or book a table?`
    } else if (searchResults.length > 0 && bestMatch) {
      const trendContext = globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
        ? ` Right now, ${globalMetrics.active_users} people are exploring restaurants.`
        : ""
      welcomeMessage = `Based on your search for "${intent}", I found ${searchResults.length} great options. The top match is ${bestMatch.name} with a ${Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance score.${trendContext} Would you like to see more details?`
    } else if (userPreferences.topCuisines.length > 0) {
      welcomeMessage = `Welcome back! Based on your love for ${userPreferences.topCuisines.slice(0, 2).join(' and ')}, what are you in the mood for today?`
    } else {
      welcomeMessage = `Hi! I'm SUFI AI. Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find the perfect spot using personalization + global trends.`
    }
    
    setMessages([{ id: 1, type: 'ai', content: welcomeMessage }])
  }, [selectedRestaurant, searchResults, bestMatch, intent, globalMetrics.trending_score, globalMetrics.active_users, userPreferences.topCuisines])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (aiResponse && aiResponse.message) {
      let finalMessage = aiResponse.message
      
      // Add context if trending
      if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 && !finalMessage.includes('trending')) {
        finalMessage = `🔥 These are trending right now! ${finalMessage}`
      }
      
      // Add personal context
      if (userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 && !finalMessage.includes('based on your')) {
        finalMessage = `Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} previous bookings, ${finalMessage.toLowerCase()}`
      }
      
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { 
        id: prev.length + 1, 
        type: 'ai', 
        content: finalMessage,
        recommendations: aiResponse.recommendations
      }])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }
  }, [aiResponse, globalMetrics.trending_score, userPreferences.totalBookings])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping || isAILoading) return
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    // AI gets full context: query + results + user preferences
    getAIResponse(userInput)
  }
  
  const getAIPersonality = () => {
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Trendspotter AI'
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '❤️ Romantic Concierge'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Quick Finder'
    if (userPreferences.totalBookings > 3) return '🎯 Personal Guide'
    return '🌍 Global Intelligence'
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">{getAIPersonality()}</span>
                  <Badge variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'} size="sm">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'trending mode' : 'context-aware'}
                  </Badge>
                  {bestMatch && (
                    <Badge variant="secondary" size="sm">
                      🎯 {bestMatch.name}
                    </Badge>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {msg.recommendations && msg.recommendations.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                          <p className="text-xs text-white/60">Top picks:</p>
                          {msg.recommendations.slice(0, 3).map((rec: any) => {
                            const isTrending = globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7
                            return (
                              <div 
                                key={rec.id} 
                                className={`bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/30' : ''}`}
                                onClick={() => setActiveSection('discovery')}
                              >
                                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                                  <div>
                                    <p className="font-medium text-sm">{rec.name}</p>
                                    <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{rec.cuisine} • {rec.vibe}</p>
                                  </div>
                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rec.rating}</span>
                                    <button className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg">
                                      Book
                                    </button>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                                {isTrending && (
                                  <p className="text-[10px] text-tertiary mt-1">🔥 Trending now</p>
                                )}
                              </div>
                            )
                          })}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder={bestMatch ? `Tell me more about ${bestMatch.name}...` : "Ask me anything..."}
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping || isAILoading} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                    ? `🔥 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active users • ${globalMetrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()} bookings today`
                    : `🎯 Personalized for you • ${userPreferences.totalBookings} past bookings`}
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">CONTEXT-AWARE AI</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Knows what you want"
              subtitle={`${userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 ? `Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings` : "Real-time personalization"} + global trends`}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">🎯 CURRENT CONTEXT</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Intent</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">"{intent}"</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Mood</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{mood}</span>
                </div>
                {bestMatch && (
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                    <span>Top match</span>
                    <span className="text-primary">{bestMatch.name}</span>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Global activity</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100)}%</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'bg-tertiary/20 animate-pulse' : 'bg-primary/20'}`}>
                  <span>{globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥' : '🧠'}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'Trending mode active' : 'Personal + global signals'}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                      ? `${Math.round(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100)}% activity spike`
                      : `${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings analyzed`}
                  </p>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-2 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                         style={{ width: `${Math.max(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100, userPreferences.totalBookings * 5)}%` }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🧠 5️⃣ UNIFIED SEARCH HOOK
tsx
// lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch.ts
import { useCallback } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'

export function useUnifiedSearch() {
  const { setSearchResults, setIsSearching, setActiveSection } = useSufiStore()
  const { profile, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  
  const performSearch = useCallback(async (query: string) => {
    if (!query.trim()) return
    
    setIsSearching(true)
    
    // Track search action
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: query,
      tags: query.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    try {
      // Call integrated search API
      const response = await fetch('/api/integrated-search', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          query: query,
          user_id: profile?.userId,
          top_k: 10
        })
      })
      
      const data = await response.json()
      
      if (data.results) {
        setSearchResults(data.results)
        setActiveSection('discovery')
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Search failed:', error)
    } finally {
      setIsSearching(false)
    }
  }, [profile?.userId, trackAction, setSearchResults, setIsSearching, setActiveSection])
  
  const getAIResponse = useCallback(async (query: string) => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-concierge', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          query: query,
          user_id: profile?.userId
        })
      })
      
      return await response.json()
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('AI request failed:', error)
      return { message: "I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again." }
    }
  }, [profile?.userId])
  
  return {
    performSearch,
    getAIResponse,
    isSearching: useSufiStore((state) => state.isSearching),
    isAILoading: false
  }
}
🔌 6️⃣ WEBSOCKET CONNECTION
tsx
// lib/hooks/useWebSocketConnection.ts
import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export function useWebSocketConnection() {
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null)
  const { updateGlobalMetrics, updateTrending, setConnected } = useSufiStore()
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:8000/ws/trends')
    wsRef.current = ws
    
    ws.onopen = () => {
      console.log('Connected to global intelligence')
      setConnected(true)
    }
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data)
      if (data.type === 'trend_update') {
        updateGlobalMetrics(data.global_metrics)
        updateTrending(data.top_trending)
      }
    }
    
    ws.onclose = () => {
      console.log('Disconnected from global intelligence')
      setConnected(false)
      // Reconnect after 5 seconds
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (wsRef.current?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
          useWebSocketConnection()
        }
      }, 5000)
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (wsRef.current) {
        wsRef.current.close()
      }
    }
  }, [])
}
