🧠 1️⃣ THE SUFI BRAIN (COMPLETE ZUSTAND STORE)
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware"

export type Mood = 'neutral' | 'romantic' | 'fast' | 'luxury'

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  location: string
  tags: string[]
  similarity: number
  personal_score: number
  trend_score: number
  final_score: number
  trending: boolean
}

export interface GlobalTrend {
  restaurant_id: string
  trend_score: number
  booking_count?: number
}

export interface GlobalMetrics {
  total_searches: number
  total_bookings: number
  peak_hour: number
  trending_score: number
  active_users: number
}

interface SufiState {
  // Core
  intent: string
  results: Restaurant[]
  bestMatch: Restaurant | null
  loading: boolean
  error: string | null
  
  // Intelligence
  mood: Mood
  userVector: number[]
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: string[]
    topVibes: string[]
    totalBookings: number
    totalSearches: number
  }
  
  // Global
  globalMetrics: GlobalMetrics
  trendingRestaurants: GlobalTrend[]
  isConnected: boolean
  
  // UI
  activeSection: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner'
  selectedRestaurant: Restaurant | null
  
  // Actions
  setIntent: (intent: string) => void
  setMood: (mood: Mood) => void
  setResults: (results: Restaurant[]) => void
  setBestMatch: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  setLoading: (loading: boolean) => void
  setError: (error: string | null) => void
  
  // Core Intelligence
  search: (query: string, userId?: string) => Promise<void>
  getAIResponse: (query: string, context?: any) => Promise<string>
  
  // Global updates
  updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics: GlobalMetrics) => void
  updateTrending: (trending: GlobalTrend[]) => void
  setConnected: (connected: boolean) => void
  
  // UI actions
  setActiveSection: (section: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner') => void
  selectRestaurant: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  
  // User
  updateUserPreferences: (prefs: Partial<SufiState['userPreferences']>) => void
  reset: () => void
}

const initialState = {
  intent: "romantic dinner",
  results: [],
  bestMatch: null,
  loading: false,
  error: null,
  mood: "neutral" as Mood,
  userVector: new Array(1024).fill(0),
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: [],
    topVibes: [],
    totalBookings: 0,
    totalSearches: 0
  },
  globalMetrics: {
    total_searches: 0,
    total_bookings: 0,
    peak_hour: 0,
    trending_score: 0,
    active_users: 0
  },
  trendingRestaurants: [],
  isConnected: false,
  activeSection: 'hero' as const,
  selectedRestaurant: null
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      ...initialState,
      
      setIntent: (intent) => {
        set({ intent })
        const lowerIntent = intent.toLowerCase()
        if (lowerIntent.includes('romantic') || lowerIntent.includes('date') || lowerIntent.includes('cozy')) {
          set({ mood: 'romantic' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('quick') || lowerIntent.includes('fast') || lowerIntent.includes('business')) {
          set({ mood: 'fast' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('luxury') || lowerIntent.includes('fine dining') || lowerIntent.includes('michelin')) {
          set({ mood: 'luxury' })
        }
      },
      
      setMood: (mood) => set({ mood }),
      setResults: (results) => set({ results, bestMatch: results[0] || null }),
      setBestMatch: (bestMatch) => set({ bestMatch }),
      setLoading: (loading) => set({ loading }),
      setError: (error) => set({ error }),
      
      // 🔥 THE BRAIN - SEARCH ACTION
      search: async (query: string, userId?: string) => {
        set({ loading: true, intent: query, error: null })
        
        try {
          const response = await fetch('/api/search', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ 
              query, 
              user_id: userId || (typeof window !== 'undefined' ? localStorage.getItem('sufi_user_id') : null)
            })
          })
          
          if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Search failed')
          
          const data = await response.json()
          
          set({ 
            results: data.results || [],
            bestMatch: data.results?.[0] || null,
            mood: data.mood || get().mood,
            loading: false
          })
          
          set({ activeSection: 'discovery' })
          
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Search error:', error)
          set({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Search failed', loading: false })
        }
      },
      
      // 🤖 AI RESPONSE
      getAIResponse: async (query: string, context?: any) => {
        const { intent, results } = get()
        
        try {
          const response = await fetch('/api/ai', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ 
              query, 
              intent,
              context: context || results.slice(0, 5)
            })
          })
          
          const data = await response.json()
          return data.message || "I found some great options. Would you like to see them?"
          
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('AI error:', error)
          return "I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again."
        }
      },
      
      updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics) => set({ globalMetrics: metrics }),
      updateTrending: (trending) => set({ trendingRestaurants: trending }),
      setConnected: (isConnected) => set({ isConnected }),
      setActiveSection: (activeSection) => set({ activeSection }),
      selectRestaurant: (selectedRestaurant) => set({ selectedRestaurant }),
      updateUserPreferences: (prefs) => set((state) => ({
        userPreferences: { ...state.userPreferences, ...prefs }
      })),
      reset: () => set(initialState)
    }),
    {
      name: 'sufi-brain',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        intent: state.intent,
        mood: state.mood,
        userPreferences: state.userPreferences
      })
    }
  )
)
🎬 2️⃣ HERO COMPONENT (DRIVES THE SYSTEM)
tsx
// components/landing/Hero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function Hero() {
  const { 
    intent, search, loading, mood, globalMetrics, isConnected, 
    userPreferences, setActiveSection 
  } = useSufiStore()
  
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState(intent)
  const [liveMetric, setLiveMetric] = useState(0)
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (globalMetrics.total_bookings !== liveMetric) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveMetric }, {
        value: globalMetrics.total_bookings,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveMetric(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [globalMetrics.total_bookings, liveMetric])
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim() || loading) return
    await search(inputValue)
    setActiveSection('discovery')
  }
  
  useEffect(() => {
    inputRef.current?.focus()
  }, [])
  
  const copy = {
    romantic: { title: "Create the", highlight: "perfect evening", subtitle: "Discover intimate spots for unforgettable moments" },
    fast: { title: "Quick. Smart.", highlight: "Instant booking", subtitle: "Find available tables near you in seconds" },
    luxury: { title: "Experience", highlight: "exceptional dining", subtitle: "Curated selections for discerning palates" },
    neutral: { title: "Find your next", highlight: "perfect meal", subtitle: "AI-powered discovery that learns your taste" }
  }[mood]
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md" variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
          {isConnected ? `🌍 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active` : '🔄 connecting...'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse ${globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.5 ? 'bg-tertiary' : 'bg-green-500'}`} />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">
              {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥 Trending mode' : '🎯 Personal AI'}
            </span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{liveMetric.toLocaleString()} bookings</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {copy.title}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">{copy.highlight}</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">{copy.subtitle}</p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              ref={inputRef}
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={intent}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={loading}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {loading ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        {userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 && (
          <div className="mt-4 flex justify-center gap-2">
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">Based on your {userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings</span>
          </div>
        )}
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic mode' : 
             mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick mode' : 
             mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury mode' : '🎯 Personalized'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 3️⃣ DISCOVERY COMPONENT (REAL RESULTS)
tsx
// components/landing/Discovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function Discovery() {
  const { results, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, trendingRestaurants, setActiveSection, selectRestaurant } = useSufiStore()
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (results.length > 0) {
      gsap.fromTo('.result-card', 
        { opacity: 0, y: 30 },
        { opacity: 1, y: 0, duration: 0.4, stagger: 0.05 }
      )
    }
  }, [results])
  
  const getRankingMessage = () => {
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '✨ Sorted by ambiance & romantic vibe'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Sorted by availability'
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Sorted by trending popularity'
    return '🎯 Sorted by personalized relevance'
  }
  
  if (results.length === 0) {
    return (
      <Section className="-mt-20">
        <Container>
          <div className="glass-panel p-16 text-center">
            <p className="text-white/40 text-lg">Search to see intelligent rankings</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2">Personal + global signals combined</p>
          </div>
        </Container>
      </Section>
    )
  }
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">INTELLIGENT RANKING</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={mood === 'romantic' ? "Perfect ambiance" : mood === 'fast' ? "Available now" : "Personalized for you"}
              subtitle={getRankingMessage()}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">📊 RANKING SIGNALS</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Semantic match</span><span className="text-primary">50% weight</span></div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Personal taste</span><span className="text-primary">20% weight</span></div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Global trends</span><span className="text-primary">30% weight</span></div>
                {bestMatch && (
                  <div className="pt-2 mt-2 border-t border-white/10">
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-400">✨ Best match: {bestMatch.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">{Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              {results.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => {
                const isBestMatch = bestMatch?.id === rest.id
                const isTrending = trendingRestaurants.some(t => t.restaurant_id === rest.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
                
                return (
                  <GlassPanel 
                    key={rest.id} 
                    hover 
                    padding="md" 
                    className={`result-card ${i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''} ${isBestMatch ? 'ring-2 ring-primary' : ''} ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/50' : ''} cursor-pointer`}
                    onClick={() => { selectRestaurant(rest); setActiveSection('ai'); }}
                  >
                    <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                      <div>
                        <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                          {['🌆', '🍣', '🍝', '🍛', '🍽️'][i % 5]}
                        </div>
                        <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                        <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-4">
                      <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                        <span>Combined score</span>
                        <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.final_score * 100)}%</span>
                      </div>
                      <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                        <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" style={{ width: `${rest.final_score * 100}%` }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="mt-2 flex gap-1">
                      {isTrending && <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full">🔥 Trending</span>}
                      {isBestMatch && <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-primary/20 text-primary rounded-full">Best match</span>}
                    </div>
                  </GlassPanel>
                )
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ AI CONCIERGE (REAL CONTEXT)
tsx
// components/landing/AI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function AI() {
  const { intent, results, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, userPreferences, selectedRestaurant, getAIResponse } = useSufiStore()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    let welcome = ""
    if (selectedRestaurant) {
      welcome = `I see you're interested in ${selectedRestaurant.name}. It has ${selectedRestaurant.rating}★ and is known for ${selectedRestaurant.vibe} dining. Would you like to know more?`
    } else if (results.length > 0 && bestMatch) {
      const trendContext = globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? ` Right now, ${globalMetrics.active_users} people are exploring restaurants.` : ""
      welcome = `Based on your search for "${intent}", I found ${results.length} great options. The top match is ${bestMatch.name} with a ${Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance score.${trendContext} Would you like to see more details?`
    } else if (userPreferences.totalBookings > 0) {
      welcome = `Welcome back! Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings, what are you in the mood for today?`
    } else {
      welcome = `Hi! I'm SUFI AI. Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find the perfect spot using personalization + global trends.`
    }
    setMessages([{ id: 1, type: 'ai', content: welcome }])
  }, [selectedRestaurant, results, bestMatch, intent, globalMetrics.trending_score, globalMetrics.active_users, userPreferences.totalBookings])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages, isTyping])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping) return
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    const response = await getAIResponse(userInput)
    
    let finalMessage = response
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 && !finalMessage.includes('trending')) {
      finalMessage = `🔥 These are trending right now! ${finalMessage}`
    }
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'ai', content: finalMessage }])
    setIsTyping(false)
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥 Trendspotter AI' : 
                     mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic Concierge' :
                     mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick Finder' : '🎯 Personal Guide'}
                  </span>
                  <Badge variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'} size="sm">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'trending mode' : 'context-aware'}
                  </Badge>
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black' : 'bg-white/5 text-white'}`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl"><div className="flex gap-1"><span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" /><span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} /><span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} /></div></div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input type="text" value={input} onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)} onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()} placeholder={bestMatch ? `Tell me more about ${bestMatch.name}...` : "Ask me anything..."} className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50" />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping} size="sm" magnetic={false}>Send</Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? `🔥 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active users • ${globalMetrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()} bookings today` : `🎯 Personalized for you • ${userPreferences.totalBookings} past bookings`}
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">CONTEXT-AWARE AI</Badge>
            <Heading title="Knows what you want" subtitle={`${userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 ? `Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings` : "Real-time personalization"} + global trends`} size="lg" className="mt-4" />
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">🎯 CURRENT CONTEXT</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Intent</span><span className="text-primary">"{intent}"</span></div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Mood</span><span className="text-primary">{mood}</span></div>
                {bestMatch && <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Top match</span><span className="text-primary">{bestMatch.name}</span></div>}
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs"><span>Global activity</span><span className="text-primary">{Math.round(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100)}%</span></div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🌌 5️⃣ ADAPTIVE BACKGROUND (REACTS TO INTELLIGENCE)
tsx
// components/core/AdaptiveBackground.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import { Canvas, useFrame } from '@react-three/fiber'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import * as THREE from 'three'

const moodColors = {
  neutral: '#a3a6ff',
  romantic: '#ff6daf',
  fast: '#22c55e',
  luxury: '#a3a6ff'
}

function EnergyField() {
  const meshRef = useRef<THREE.Points>(null)
  const { mood, globalMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  
  useFrame((state) => {
    if (meshRef.current) {
      meshRef.current.rotation.y = state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.03
      meshRef.current.rotation.x = Math.sin(state.clock.getElapsedTime() * 0.02) * 0.1
      const material = meshRef.current.material as THREE.PointsMaterial
      material.color.set(moodColors[mood])
      material.opacity = 0.3 + globalMetrics.trending_score * 0.4
    }
  })
  
  const particles = new Float32Array(2000 * 3)
  for (let i = 0; i < 2000; i++) {
    particles[i*3] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 20
    particles[i*3+1] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15
    particles[i*3+2] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 - 5
  }
  
  return (
    <points ref={meshRef}>
      <bufferGeometry>
        <bufferAttribute attach="attributes-position" count={2000} array={particles} itemSize={3} />
      </bufferGeometry>
      <pointsMaterial color={moodColors.neutral} size={0.05} transparent opacity={0.3} />
    </points>
  )
}

export default function AdaptiveBackground() {
  const { mood, globalMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 -z-20 pointer-events-none">
      <Canvas camera={{ position: [0, 0, 5] }}>
        <ambientLight intensity={0.5} />
        <EnergyField />
      </Canvas>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 transition-all duration-1000" style={{ background: `radial-gradient(circle at 30% 40%, ${moodColors[mood]}20, transparent 70%)`, opacity: 0.3 + globalMetrics.trending_score * 0.3 }} />
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b from-transparent via-background/50 to-background" />
    </div>
  )
}
🔌 6️⃣ API ROUTES
tsx
// app/api/search/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { query, user_id } = await request.json()
    const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/api/integrated-search', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ query, user_id, top_k: 10 })
    })
    const data = await response.json()
    return NextResponse.json(data)
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Search failed', results: [] }, { status: 500 })
  }
}
tsx
// app/api/ai/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { query, intent, context } = await request.json()
    const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/api/ai-concierge', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ query, intent, context })
    })
    const data = await response.json()
    return NextResponse.json(data)
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json({ message: "I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again." }, { status: 200 })
  }
}
tsx
// app/api/trends/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('http://localhost:8000/api/global/metrics')
    const data = await response.json()
    return NextResponse.json(data)
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json({ total_searches: 0, total_bookings: 0, peak_hour: 0, trending_score: 0, active_users: 0 })
  }
}
🔁 7️⃣ REAL-TIME TRENDS HOOK
tsx
// lib/hooks/useRealTimeTrends.ts
import { useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export function useRealTimeTrends() {
  const { updateGlobalMetrics, updateTrending, setConnected } = useSufiStore()
  
  useEffect(() => {
    let interval: NodeJS.Timeout
    const fetchTrends = async () => {
      try {
        const response = await fetch('/api/trends')
        const data = await response.json()
        updateGlobalMetrics(data)
        setConnected(true)
      } catch { setConnected(false) }
    }
    fetchTrends()
    interval = setInterval(fetchTrends, 5000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [updateGlobalMetrics, updateTrending, setConnected])
}

🎯 FINAL SYSTEM SUMMARY
Component	What It Does
Zustand Brain	Single source of truth, connects everything
Hero	Drives system via search() action
Discovery	Shows real ranked results from backend
AI	Uses intent + results for context-aware responses
AdaptiveBackground	Reacts to mood + global activity
API Routes	Connect to Python ML backend
Real-Time Trends	Updates global metrics every 5 seconds
🔥 ONE BRAIN. ONE SYSTEM. EVERYTHING CONNECTED. REAL AI. REAL-TIME.



 SUFI OS — COMPLETE UNIFIED SYSTEM
I'll merge everything into ONE connected state where every component reacts to the same intelligence layer.

🧠 1️⃣ UNIFIED GLOBAL STATE
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"
import { persist } from "zustand/middleware"

export type Mood = 'neutral' | 'romantic' | 'fast' | 'luxury'

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  location: string
  tags: string[]
  similarity: number
  personal_score: number
  trend_score: number
  final_score: number
  trending: boolean
}

export interface GlobalMetrics {
  total_searches: number
  total_bookings: number
  peak_hour: number
  trending_score: number
  active_users: number
}

interface SufiState {
  // User state
  intent: string
  mood: Mood
  userVector: number[]
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: string[]
    topVibes: string[]
    totalBookings: number
  }
  
  // Search results
  searchResults: Restaurant[]
  bestMatch: Restaurant | null
  isSearching: boolean
  
  // Global trends
  globalMetrics: GlobalMetrics
  trendingRestaurants: { restaurant_id: string; trend_score: number }[]
  isConnected: boolean
  
  // UI state
  activeSection: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner'
  selectedRestaurant: Restaurant | null
  
  // Actions
  setIntent: (intent: string) => void
  setMood: (mood: Mood) => void
  setSearchResults: (results: Restaurant[]) => void
  setBestMatch: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  setIsSearching: (isSearching: boolean) => void
  updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics: GlobalMetrics) => void
  updateTrending: (trending: { restaurant_id: string; trend_score: number }[]) => void
  setConnected: (connected: boolean) => void
  setActiveSection: (section: 'hero' | 'discovery' | 'ai' | 'owner') => void
  selectRestaurant: (restaurant: Restaurant | null) => void
  updateUserPreferences: (preferences: Partial<SufiState['userPreferences']>) => void
  reset: () => void
}

const initialState = {
  intent: "romantic dinner",
  mood: "neutral" as Mood,
  userVector: new Array(1024).fill(0),
  userPreferences: {
    topCuisines: [],
    topVibes: [],
    totalBookings: 0
  },
  searchResults: [],
  bestMatch: null,
  isSearching: false,
  globalMetrics: {
    total_searches: 0,
    total_bookings: 0,
    peak_hour: 0,
    trending_score: 0,
    active_users: 0
  },
  trendingRestaurants: [],
  isConnected: false,
  activeSection: 'hero' as const,
  selectedRestaurant: null
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>()(
  persist(
    (set, get) => ({
      ...initialState,
      
      setIntent: (intent) => {
        set({ intent })
        // Auto-detect mood from intent
        const lowerIntent = intent.toLowerCase()
        if (lowerIntent.includes('romantic') || lowerIntent.includes('date') || lowerIntent.includes('cozy')) {
          set({ mood: 'romantic' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('quick') || lowerIntent.includes('fast') || lowerIntent.includes('business')) {
          set({ mood: 'fast' })
        } else if (lowerIntent.includes('luxury') || lowerIntent.includes('fine dining') || lowerIntent.includes('michelin')) {
          set({ mood: 'luxury' })
        }
      },
      
      setMood: (mood) => set({ mood }),
      
      setSearchResults: (results) => {
        const bestMatch = results.length > 0 ? results[0] : null
        set({ searchResults: results, bestMatch })
      },
      
      setBestMatch: (bestMatch) => set({ bestMatch }),
      
      setIsSearching: (isSearching) => set({ isSearching }),
      
      updateGlobalMetrics: (metrics) => set({ globalMetrics: metrics }),
      
      updateTrending: (trending) => set({ trendingRestaurants: trending }),
      
      setConnected: (isConnected) => set({ isConnected }),
      
      setActiveSection: (activeSection) => set({ activeSection }),
      
      selectRestaurant: (selectedRestaurant) => set({ selectedRestaurant }),
      
      updateUserPreferences: (preferences) => set((state) => ({
        userPreferences: { ...state.userPreferences, ...preferences }
      })),
      
      reset: () => set(initialState)
    }),
    {
      name: 'sufi-unified-state',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        intent: state.intent,
        mood: state.mood,
        userPreferences: state.userPreferences,
        globalMetrics: state.globalMetrics
      })
    }
  )
)
🎬 2️⃣ UNIFIED HERO (DRIVES THE SYSTEM)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedHero.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUnifiedSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function UnifiedHero() {
  const { 
    intent, setIntent, mood, globalMetrics, isConnected, 
    setActiveSection, setIsSearching 
  } = useSufiStore()
  const { performSearch, isSearching } = useUnifiedSearch()
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState(intent)
  const [liveMetric, setLiveMetric] = useState(0)
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  
  // Animate live metric like Stripe
  useEffect(() => {
    if (globalMetrics.total_bookings !== liveMetric) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveMetric }, {
        value: globalMetrics.total_bookings,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveMetric(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [globalMetrics.total_bookings, liveMetric])
  
  const handleSearch = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault()
    if (!inputValue.trim() || isSearching) return
    
    // THIS DRIVES THE ENTIRE SYSTEM
    setIntent(inputValue)
    setIsSearching(true)
    setActiveSection('discovery')
    
    await performSearch(inputValue)
  }
  
  // Auto-focus input
  useEffect(() => {
    inputRef.current?.focus()
  }, [])
  
  const getHeroCopy = () => {
    switch(mood) {
      case 'romantic':
        return {
          title: "Create the",
          highlight: "perfect evening",
          subtitle: "Discover intimate spots for unforgettable moments"
        }
      case 'fast':
        return {
          title: "Quick. Smart.",
          highlight: "Instant booking",
          subtitle: "Find available tables near you in seconds"
        }
      case 'luxury':
        return {
          title: "Experience",
          highlight: "exceptional dining",
          subtitle: "Curated selections for discerning palates"
        }
      default:
        return {
          title: "Find your next",
          highlight: "perfect meal",
          subtitle: "AI-powered discovery that learns your taste"
        }
    }
  }
  
  const copy = getHeroCopy()
  
  return (
    <Section className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center text-center">
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 z-20">
        <Badge size="md" variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
          {isConnected ? `🌍 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active` : '🔄 connecting...'}
        </Badge>
      </div>
      
      <Container maxWidth="2xl">
        <div className="mb-6">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 glass-panel px-4 py-2 rounded-full">
            <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full animate-pulse ${globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.5 ? 'bg-tertiary' : 'bg-green-500'}`} />
            <span className="text-xs text-white/40">
              {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥 Trending mode' : '🎯 Personal AI'}
            </span>
            <span className="text-sm font-mono text-primary">{liveMetric.toLocaleString()} bookings</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl font-bold tracking-tight">
          {copy.title}
          <br />
          <span className="gradient-text">{copy.highlight}</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg md:text-xl text-white/60 mt-6 max-w-2xl mx-auto">
          {copy.subtitle}
        </p>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSearch} className="mt-8 w-full max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="relative group">
            <input
              ref={inputRef}
              type="text"
              value={inputValue}
              onChange={(e) => setInputValue(e.target.value)}
              placeholder={intent}
              className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                       text-white placeholder:text-white/40 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                       focus:border-primary/50 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-primary/20
                       transition-all duration-300 group-hover:bg-white/10"
            />
            <button 
              type="submit" 
              disabled={isSearching}
              className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 px-5 py-2 
                       bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black rounded-xl 
                       font-medium text-sm hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-primary/20 
                       transition-all duration-300 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {isSearching ? '...' : '→'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
        
        <div className="flex justify-center gap-2 mt-3">
          <Badge variant={mood === 'romantic' ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'}>
            {mood === 'romantic' ? '❤️ Romantic mode' : 
             mood === 'fast' ? '⚡ Quick mode' : 
             mood === 'luxury' ? '✨ Luxury mode' : '🎯 Personalized'}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🔍 3️⃣ UNIFIED DISCOVERY (REAL RANKING)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedDiscovery.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import gsap from 'gsap'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'

export default function UnifiedDiscovery() {
  const { 
    searchResults, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, trendingRestaurants,
    setActiveSection, selectRestaurant
  } = useSufiStore()
  
  // Animate cards when results update
  useEffect(() => {
    if (searchResults.length > 0) {
      gsap.fromTo('.result-card', 
        { opacity: 0, y: 30 },
        { opacity: 1, y: 0, duration: 0.4, stagger: 0.05 }
      )
    }
  }, [searchResults])
  
  const getRankingMessage = () => {
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '✨ Sorted by ambiance & romantic vibe'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Sorted by availability'
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Sorted by trending popularity'
    return '🎯 Sorted by personalized relevance'
  }
  
  const getTrendingBadge = (restaurant: any) => {
    const isTrending = trendingRestaurants.some(t => t.restaurant_id === restaurant.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
    if (isTrending) {
      return <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse">🔥 Trending</span>
    }
    return null
  }
  
  const handleCardClick = (restaurant: any) => {
    selectRestaurant(restaurant)
    setActiveSection('ai')
  }
  
  const displayResults = searchResults.length > 0 ? searchResults : []
  
  return (
    <Section className="-mt-20">
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">INTELLIGENT RANKING</Badge>
            <Heading
              title={mood === 'romantic' ? "Perfect ambiance" : 
                     mood === 'fast' ? "Available now" : 
                     "Personalized for you"}
              subtitle={getRankingMessage()}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">📊 RANKING SIGNALS</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Semantic match</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">50% weight</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Personal taste</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">20% weight</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Global trends</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">30% weight</span>
                </div>
                {bestMatch && (
                  <div className="pt-2 mt-2 border-t border-white/10">
                    <p className="text-xs text-green-400">✨ Best match: {bestMatch.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-white/40 mt-1">
                      {Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance
                    </p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            {displayResults.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {displayResults.slice(0, 3).map((rest, i) => {
                  const isBestMatch = bestMatch?.id === rest.id
                  const isTrending = trendingRestaurants.some(t => t.restaurant_id === rest.id && t.trend_score > 0.7)
                  
                  return (
                    <GlassPanel 
                      key={rest.id} 
                      hover 
                      padding="md" 
                      className={`result-card ${i === 0 ? 'col-span-2' : ''} ${isBestMatch ? 'ring-2 ring-primary' : ''} ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/50' : ''} cursor-pointer`}
                      onClick={() => handleCardClick(rest)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                        <div>
                          <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-xl bg-primary/20 mb-3 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl">
                            {rest.name === 'Sky Lounge' ? '🌆' : 
                             rest.name === 'Sakura Hills' ? '🍣' : 
                             rest.name === 'La Piazza' ? '🍝' : '🍽️'}
                          </div>
                          <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold">{rest.name}</h3>
                          <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{rest.cuisine} • {rest.price}</p>
                        </div>
                        <span className="text-yellow-400">★ {rest.rating}</span>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-4">
                        <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
                          <span>Combined score</span>
                          <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(rest.final_score * 100)}%</span>
                        </div>
                        <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
                          <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                               style={{ width: `${rest.final_score * 100}%` }} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      
                      <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-1 items-center">
                        {getTrendingBadge(rest)}
                        {isBestMatch && (
                          <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-primary/20 text-primary rounded-full">
                            Best match
                          </span>
                        )}
                        {rest.trend_score > 0.7 && (
                          <span className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-tertiary/20 text-tertiary rounded-full">
                            {Math.round(rest.trend_score * 100)}% trend
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      
                      {isTrending && (
                        <div className="mt-2 flex items-center gap-1">
                          <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 bg-tertiary rounded-full animate-pulse" />
                          <p className="text-xs text-tertiary">Trending right now</p>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </GlassPanel>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="glass-panel p-12 text-center">
                <p className="text-white/40">Search to see intelligent rankings</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2">Personal + global signals combined</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ UNIFIED AI (REAL CONTEXT)
tsx
// components/landing/UnifiedAI.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUnifiedSearch } from '@/lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch'
import Section from '@/components/layout/Section'
import Container from '@/components/layout/Container'
import Grid from '@/components/layout/Grid'
import Heading from '@/components/ui/Heading'
import Badge from '@/components/ui/Badge'
import GlassPanel from '@/components/ui/GlassPanel'
import Button from '@/components/ui/Button'

interface Message {
  id: number
  type: 'user' | 'ai'
  content: string
  recommendations?: any[]
}

export default function UnifiedAI() {
  const { 
    intent, searchResults, bestMatch, mood, globalMetrics, 
    userPreferences, selectedRestaurant, setActiveSection 
  } = useSufiStore()
  const { getAIResponse, aiResponse, isAILoading } = useUnifiedSearch()
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [isTyping, setIsTyping] = useState(false)
  const chatEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
  
  // Generate welcome message based on current state
  useEffect(() => {
    let welcomeMessage = ""
    
    if (selectedRestaurant) {
      welcomeMessage = `I see you're interested in ${selectedRestaurant.name}. It has ${selectedRestaurant.rating}★ and is known for ${selectedRestaurant.vibe} dining. Would you like to know more or book a table?`
    } else if (searchResults.length > 0 && bestMatch) {
      const trendContext = globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
        ? ` Right now, ${globalMetrics.active_users} people are exploring restaurants.`
        : ""
      welcomeMessage = `Based on your search for "${intent}", I found ${searchResults.length} great options. The top match is ${bestMatch.name} with a ${Math.round(bestMatch.final_score * 100)}% relevance score.${trendContext} Would you like to see more details?`
    } else if (userPreferences.topCuisines.length > 0) {
      welcomeMessage = `Welcome back! Based on your love for ${userPreferences.topCuisines.slice(0, 2).join(' and ')}, what are you in the mood for today?`
    } else {
      welcomeMessage = `Hi! I'm SUFI AI. Tell me what you're looking for, and I'll find the perfect spot using personalization + global trends.`
    }
    
    setMessages([{ id: 1, type: 'ai', content: welcomeMessage }])
  }, [selectedRestaurant, searchResults, bestMatch, intent, globalMetrics.trending_score, globalMetrics.active_users, userPreferences.topCuisines])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    chatEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' })
  }, [messages])
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (aiResponse && aiResponse.message) {
      let finalMessage = aiResponse.message
      
      // Add context if trending
      if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 && !finalMessage.includes('trending')) {
        finalMessage = `🔥 These are trending right now! ${finalMessage}`
      }
      
      // Add personal context
      if (userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 && !finalMessage.includes('based on your')) {
        finalMessage = `Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} previous bookings, ${finalMessage.toLowerCase()}`
      }
      
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, { 
        id: prev.length + 1, 
        type: 'ai', 
        content: finalMessage,
        recommendations: aiResponse.recommendations
      }])
      setIsTyping(false)
    }
  }, [aiResponse, globalMetrics.trending_score, userPreferences.totalBookings])
  
  const handleSend = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || isTyping || isAILoading) return
    
    setMessages(prev => [...prev, { id: prev.length + 1, type: 'user', content: input }])
    const userInput = input
    setInput('')
    setIsTyping(true)
    
    // AI gets full context: query + results + user preferences
    getAIResponse(userInput)
  }
  
  const getAIPersonality = () => {
    if (globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7) return '🔥 Trendspotter AI'
    if (mood === 'romantic') return '❤️ Romantic Concierge'
    if (mood === 'fast') return '⚡ Quick Finder'
    if (userPreferences.totalBookings > 3) return '🎯 Personal Guide'
    return '🌍 Global Intelligence'
  }
  
  return (
    <Section>
      <Container>
        <Grid>
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-7">
            <GlassPanel padding="none" className="overflow-hidden">
              <div className="border-b border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-primary text-lg">🤖</span>
                  <span className="font-medium">{getAIPersonality()}</span>
                  <Badge variant={globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'tertiary' : 'primary'} size="sm">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'trending mode' : 'context-aware'}
                  </Badge>
                  {bestMatch && (
                    <Badge variant="secondary" size="sm">
                      🎯 {bestMatch.name}
                    </Badge>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div className="h-[500px] overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-4">
                {messages.map((msg) => (
                  <div key={msg.id} className={`flex ${msg.type === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}>
                    <div className={`max-w-[85%] p-4 rounded-2xl ${
                      msg.type === 'user'
                        ? 'bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary text-black'
                        : 'bg-white/5 text-white'
                    }`}>
                      <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{msg.content}</p>
                      
                      {msg.recommendations && msg.recommendations.length > 0 && (
                        <div className="mt-3 space-y-2">
                          <p className="text-xs text-white/60">Top picks:</p>
                          {msg.recommendations.slice(0, 3).map((rec: any) => {
                            const isTrending = globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7
                            return (
                              <div 
                                key={rec.id} 
                                className={`bg-white/10 rounded-lg p-2 cursor-pointer hover:bg-white/20 transition-all ${isTrending ? 'ring-1 ring-tertiary/30' : ''}`}
                                onClick={() => setActiveSection('discovery')}
                              >
                                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                                  <div>
                                    <p className="font-medium text-sm">{rec.name}</p>
                                    <p className="text-xs opacity-60">{rec.cuisine} • {rec.vibe}</p>
                                  </div>
                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {rec.rating}</span>
                                    <button className="px-2 py-1 bg-primary text-black text-xs rounded-lg">
                                      Book
                                    </button>
                                  </div>
                                </div>
                                {isTrending && (
                                  <p className="text-[10px] text-tertiary mt-1">🔥 Trending now</p>
                                )}
                              </div>
                            )
                          })}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                {isTyping && (
                  <div className="flex justify-start">
                    <div className="bg-white/5 p-4 rounded-2xl">
                      <div className="flex gap-1">
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '150ms' }} />
                        <span className="w-2 h-2 bg-white/40 rounded-full animate-bounce" style={{ animationDelay: '300ms' }} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div ref={chatEndRef} />
              </div>
              
              <div className="border-t border-white/10 p-4">
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={input}
                    onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
                    onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSend()}
                    placeholder={bestMatch ? `Tell me more about ${bestMatch.name}...` : "Ask me anything..."}
                    className="flex-1 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                             text-white placeholder:text-white/40 focus:outline-none focus:border-primary/50"
                  />
                  <Button onClick={handleSend} disabled={isTyping || isAILoading} size="sm" magnetic={false}>
                    Send
                  </Button>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-white/40 mt-2 text-center">
                  {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                    ? `🔥 ${globalMetrics.active_users} active users • ${globalMetrics.total_bookings.toLocaleString()} bookings today`
                    : `🎯 Personalized for you • ${userPreferences.totalBookings} past bookings`}
                </p>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
          
          <div className="col-span-12 lg:col-span-5">
            <Badge variant="primary">CONTEXT-AWARE AI</Badge>
            <Heading
              title="Knows what you want"
              subtitle={`${userPreferences.totalBookings > 0 ? `Based on your ${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings` : "Real-time personalization"} + global trends`}
              size="lg"
              className="mt-4"
            />
            
            <div className="mt-6 p-4 glass-panel">
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">🎯 CURRENT CONTEXT</p>
              <div className="space-y-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Intent</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">"{intent}"</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Mood</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{mood}</span>
                </div>
                {bestMatch && (
                  <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                    <span>Top match</span>
                    <span className="text-primary">{bestMatch.name}</span>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs">
                  <span>Global activity</span>
                  <span className="text-primary">{Math.round(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100)}%</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <GlassPanel padding="md" className="mt-6">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'bg-tertiary/20 animate-pulse' : 'bg-primary/20'}`}>
                  <span>{globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? '🔥' : '🧠'}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 ? 'Trending mode active' : 'Personal + global signals'}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">
                    {globalMetrics.trending_score > 0.7 
                      ? `${Math.round(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100)}% activity spike`
                      : `${userPreferences.totalBookings} bookings analyzed`}
                  </p>
                  <div className="h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-2 overflow-hidden">
                    <div className="h-full bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-tertiary rounded-full" 
                         style={{ width: `${Math.max(globalMetrics.trending_score * 100, userPreferences.totalBookings * 5)}%` }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </GlassPanel>
          </div>
        </Grid>
      </Container>
    </Section>
  )
}
🧠 5️⃣ UNIFIED SEARCH HOOK
tsx
// lib/hooks/useUnifiedSearch.ts
import { useCallback } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import { useUserProfileStore } from '@/lib/state/userProfileStore'

export function useUnifiedSearch() {
  const { setSearchResults, setIsSearching, setActiveSection } = useSufiStore()
  const { profile, trackAction } = useUserProfileStore()
  
  const performSearch = useCallback(async (query: string) => {
    if (!query.trim()) return
    
    setIsSearching(true)
    
    // Track search action
    trackAction({
      type: 'SEARCH',
      query: query,
      tags: query.toLowerCase().split(' ')
    })
    
    try {
      // Call integrated search API
      const response = await fetch('/api/integrated-search', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          query: query,
          user_id: profile?.userId,
          top_k: 10
        })
      })
      
      const data = await response.json()
      
      if (data.results) {
        setSearchResults(data.results)
        setActiveSection('discovery')
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Search failed:', error)
    } finally {
      setIsSearching(false)
    }
  }, [profile?.userId, trackAction, setSearchResults, setIsSearching, setActiveSection])
  
  const getAIResponse = useCallback(async (query: string) => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-concierge', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          query: query,
          user_id: profile?.userId
        })
      })
      
      return await response.json()
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('AI request failed:', error)
      return { message: "I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again." }
    }
  }, [profile?.userId])
  
  return {
    performSearch,
    getAIResponse,
    isSearching: useSufiStore((state) => state.isSearching),
    isAILoading: false
  }
}
🔌 6️⃣ WEBSOCKET CONNECTION
tsx
// lib/hooks/useWebSocketConnection.ts
import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export function useWebSocketConnection() {
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null)
  const { updateGlobalMetrics, updateTrending, setConnected } = useSufiStore()
  
  useEffect(() => {
    const ws = new WebSocket('ws://localhost:8000/ws/trends')
    wsRef.current = ws
    
    ws.onopen = () => {
      console.log('Connected to global intelligence')
      setConnected(true)
    }
    
    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
      const data = JSON.parse(event.data)
      if (data.type === 'trend_update') {
        updateGlobalMetrics(data.global_metrics)
        updateTrending(data.top_trending)
      }
    }
    
    ws.onclose = () => {
      console.log('Disconnected from global intelligence')
      setConnected(false)
      // Reconnect after 5 seconds
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (wsRef.current?.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
          useWebSocketConnection()
        }
      }, 5000)
    }
    
    return () => {
      if (wsRef.current) {
        wsRef.current.close()
      }
    }
  }, [])
}

🧠 1️⃣ THE BRAIN (MINIMAL, POWERFUL)
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  reasoning: string
  final_score: number
}

interface SufiState {
  intent: string
  results: Restaurant[]
  bestMatch: Restaurant | null
  loading: boolean
  globalMetrics: { bookings_last_hour: number; trending_locations: number }
  
  search: (query: string) => Promise<void>
  updateMetrics: (metrics: any) => void
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>((set) => ({
  intent: "",
  results: [],
  bestMatch: null,
  loading: false,
  globalMetrics: { bookings_last_hour: 0, trending_locations: 0 },
  
  search: async (query) => {
    set({ loading: true, intent: query })
    
    // Real API call
    const res = await fetch('/api/search', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ query })
    })
    const data = await res.json()
    
    set({
      results: data.results,
      bestMatch: data.results[0],
      loading: false
    })
  },
  
  updateMetrics: (metrics) => set({ globalMetrics: metrics })
}))
🎬 2️⃣ HERO — CONTROL THE SYSTEM
tsx
// components/landing/Hero.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function Hero() {
  const { search, results, loading, globalMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [liveBookings, setLiveBookings] = useState(0)
  
  // Animate live metric
  useEffect(() => {
    if (globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour !== liveBookings) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveBookings }, {
        value: globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveBookings(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour])
  
  const handleSearch = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && input.trim()) {
      search(input)
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <section className="min-h-screen flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-6">
      {/* Top-left */}
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 text-sm text-white/30">
        SUFI OS
      </div>
      
      {/* Center */}
      <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto text-center">
        <h1 className="text-6xl md:text-7xl font-semibold tracking-tight mb-4">
          Decisions, resolved
          <br />
          <span className="text-white/60">instantly</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-lg text-white/40 mb-10 max-w-xl mx-auto">
          SUFI understands intent, behavior, and real-time signals to rank what matters.
        </p>
        
        {/* Input */}
        <div className="relative max-w-xl mx-auto">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={handleSearch}
            placeholder="Find rooftop dinner with wine"
            className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                     text-white placeholder:text-white/30 text-lg focus:outline-none 
                     focus:border-white/20 transition-all"
          />
          {loading && (
            <div className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2">
              <div className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-white/20 border-t-white rounded-full animate-spin" />
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        {/* Live results preview */}
        {results.length > 0 && !loading && (
          <div className="mt-8 space-y-2 max-w-xl mx-auto">
            {results.slice(0, 3).map((r, i) => (
              <div
                key={r.id}
                className={`p-4 rounded-xl transition-all cursor-pointer
                  ${i === 0 ? 'bg-white/10 border-l-2 border-l-primary' : 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10'}`}
              >
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{r.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{r.cuisine} • {r.vibe}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-sm text-yellow-400">★ {r.rating}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-white/40">{r.availability}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        
        {/* Live metric */}
        <div className="mt-10 text-sm text-white/30">
          {liveBookings} bookings in the last hour
          {globalMetrics.trending_locations > 0 && (
            <> • {globalMetrics.trending_locations} trending locations</>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}

🤖 5️⃣ AI CONCIERGE — USEFUL, NOT FLASHY
tsx
// components/landing/AIConcierge.tsx
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export default function AIConcierge() {
  const { results, bestMatch, userPreferences } = useSufiStore()
  const [message, setMessage] = useState('')
  const [response, setResponse] = useState('')
  
  if (results.length === 0) return null
  
  const handleAsk = async () => {
    if (!message.trim()) return
    
    const res = await fetch('/api/ai', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify({ 
        query: message, 
        context: results.slice(0, 3),
        preferences: userPreferences 
      })
    })
    const data = await res.json()
    setResponse(data.message)
  }
  
  return (
    <section className="py-20 px-6 border-t border-white/5">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <p className="text-sm text-white/40 uppercase tracking-wide">AI Concierge</p>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-medium mt-2">Ask about these results</h2>
        </div>
        
        {/* Preview cards */}
        <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 mb-8">
          {results.slice(0, 2).map(r => (
            <div key={r.id} className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium">{r.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{r.cuisine} • {r.vibe}</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {r.rating}</span>
              </div>
              <p className="text-sm text-white/50">{r.reasoning}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        
        {/* Chat */}
        <div className="bg-white/5 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="p-4 border-b border-white/10">
            <p className="text-sm text-white/60">
              {bestMatch ? 
                `You usually prefer ${bestMatch.vibe.toLowerCase()} places. This matches your taste.` :
                "Ask about any restaurant"}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-4">
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={message}
                onChange={(e) => setMessage(e.target.value)}
                onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAsk()}
                placeholder="Ask about availability, pricing, or vibe..."
                className="flex-1 bg-transparent border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                         text-white placeholder:text-white/30 text-sm focus:outline-none"
              />
              <button
                onClick={handleAsk}
                className="px-5 py-2 bg-white/10 rounded-xl text-sm hover:bg-white/20 transition-all"
              >
                Ask
              </button>
            </div>
            {response && (
              <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-lg">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/80">{response}</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
📊 6️⃣ LIVE SYSTEM — REAL-TIME INTELLIGENCE
tsx
// components/landing/LiveSystem.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function LiveSystem() {
  const { globalMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState(0)
  const [trending, setTrending] = useState(0)
  
  useEffect(() => {
    gsap.to({ value: bookings }, {
      value: globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour,
      duration: 1,
      onUpdate: function() {
        setBookings(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
      }
    })
    gsap.to({ value: trending }, {
      value: globalMetrics.trending_locations,
      duration: 1,
      onUpdate: function() {
        setTrending(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
      }
    })
  }, [globalMetrics])
  
  return (
    <section className="py-20 px-6 border-t border-white/5">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto text-center">
        <p className="text-sm text-white/40 uppercase tracking-wide mb-4">Live System</p>
        <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-8">
          <div className="p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-2xl">
            <p className="text-4xl font-semibold">{bookings}</p>
            <p className="text-white/40 text-sm">bookings in the last hour</p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-2xl">
            <p className="text-4xl font-semibold">{trending}</p>
            <p className="text-white/40 text-sm">trending locations</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}

// app/page.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import Hero from '@/components/landing/Hero'
import Discovery from '@/components/landing/Discovery'
import SystemFlow from '@/components/landing/SystemFlow'
import AIConcierge from '@/components/landing/AIConcierge'
import LiveSystem from '@/components/landing/LiveSystem'
import OwnerSide from '@/components/landing/OwnerSide'
import CTA from '@/components/landing/CTA'

export default function LandingPage() {
  const { updateMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  
  // Real-time metrics polling
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchMetrics = async () => {
      const res = await fetch('/api/trends')
      const data = await res.json()
      updateMetrics(data)
    }
    fetchMetrics()
    const interval = setInterval(fetchMetrics, 10000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [updateMetrics])
  
  return (
    <main className="bg-[#0a0a0a] text-white">
      <Hero />
      <Discovery />
      <SystemFlow />
      <AIConcierge />
      <LiveSystem />
      <OwnerSide />
      <CTA />
    </main>
  )
}
