🧠 1️⃣ THE BRAIN (ZUSTAND STORE)
tsx
// lib/state/sufiStore.ts
import { create } from "zustand"

export interface Restaurant {
  id: string
  name: string
  cuisine: string
  rating: number
  price: string
  vibe: string
  availability: 'available' | 'limited' | 'busy'
  reasoning: string
  final_score: number
}

interface SufiState {
  intent: string
  results: Restaurant[]
  bestMatch: Restaurant | null
  loading: boolean
  error: string | null
  globalMetrics: {
    bookings_last_hour: number
    trending_locations: number
    active_users: number
  }
  
  // Actions
  search: (query: string) => Promise<void>
  updateMetrics: (metrics: Partial<SufiState['globalMetrics']>) => void
  reset: () => void
}

export const useSufiStore = create<SufiState>((set, get) => ({
  intent: "",
  results: [],
  bestMatch: null,
  loading: false,
  error: null,
  globalMetrics: {
    bookings_last_hour: 0,
    trending_locations: 0,
    active_users: 0
  },
  
  search: async (query: string) => {
    if (!query.trim()) return
    
    set({ loading: true, intent: query, error: null })
    
    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/search', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ query })
      })
      
      if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Search failed')
      
      const data = await response.json()
      
      set({
        results: data.results || [],
        bestMatch: data.results?.[0] || null,
        loading: false
      })
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Search error:', error)
      set({ error: 'Failed to search', loading: false })
    }
  },
  
  updateMetrics: (metrics) => {
    set((state) => ({
      globalMetrics: { ...state.globalMetrics, ...metrics }
    }))
  },
  
  reset: () => {
    set({
      intent: "",
      results: [],
      bestMatch: null,
      loading: false,
      error: null
    })
  }
}))
🎬 2️⃣ HERO (REAL INPUT + LIVE PREVIEW)
tsx
// components/landing/Hero.tsx
'use client'

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function Hero() {
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const { search, results, loading, globalMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null)
  const [liveBookings, setLiveBookings] = useState(0)
  
  // Animate live metric
  useEffect(() => {
    if (globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour !== liveBookings) {
      gsap.to({ value: liveBookings }, {
        value: globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour,
        duration: 1,
        onUpdate: function() {
          setLiveBookings(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
        }
      })
    }
  }, [globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour, liveBookings])
  
  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && input.trim() && !loading) {
      search(input)
    }
  }
  
  useEffect(() => {
    inputRef.current?.focus()
  }, [])
  
  return (
    <section className="relative min-h-screen flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 bg-[#0a0a0a]">
      {/* Top-left branding */}
      <div className="absolute top-8 left-8 text-sm text-white/30 font-mono">
        SUFI OS
      </div>
      
      {/* Main content */}
      <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto text-center w-full">
        <h1 className="text-5xl md:text-6xl font-semibold tracking-tight mb-4">
          Decisions, resolved
          <br />
          <span className="text-white/60">instantly</span>
        </h1>
        
        <p className="text-base md:text-lg text-white/40 mb-8 max-w-xl mx-auto">
          SUFI understands intent, behavior, and real-time signals to rank what matters.
        </p>
        
        {/* Input */}
        <div className="relative max-w-xl mx-auto">
          <input
            ref={inputRef}
            type="text"
            value={input}
            onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            placeholder="Find rooftop dinner with wine"
            className="w-full bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-2xl px-6 py-4 
                     text-white placeholder:text-white/30 text-base focus:outline-none 
                     focus:border-white/20 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-white/20 transition-all"
            disabled={loading}
          />
          {loading && (
            <div className="absolute right-5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2">
              <div className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-white/20 border-t-white rounded-full animate-spin" />
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        
        {/* Live preview results */}
        {results.length > 0 && !loading && (
          <div className="mt-8 space-y-2 max-w-xl mx-auto w-full">
            <p className="text-xs text-white/30 text-left mb-2">Top matches</p>
            {results.slice(0, 3).map((r, i) => (
              <div
                key={r.id}
                className={`group p-4 rounded-xl transition-all cursor-pointer text-left
                  ${i === 0 
                    ? 'bg-white/10 border-l-2 border-l-primary' 
                    : 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 border border-white/5'
                  }`}
              >
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{r.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{r.cuisine} • {r.vibe}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-sm text-yellow-400">★ {r.rating}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-white/40 capitalize">{r.availability}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                {i === 0 && (
                  <p className="text-xs text-primary mt-2">{r.reasoning}</p>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
        
        {/* Live metric */}
        <div className="mt-10 text-sm text-white/30">
          {liveBookings > 0 && (
            <span>{liveBookings} bookings in the last hour</span>
          )}
          {globalMetrics.trending_locations > 0 && (
            <span className="ml-3">• {globalMetrics.trending_locations} trending locations</span>
          )}
          {globalMetrics.active_users > 0 && (
            <span className="ml-3">• {globalMetrics.active_users} active now</span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      
      {/* Scroll hint */}
      {results.length === 0 && !loading && (
        <div className="absolute bottom-8 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 text-xs text-white/20 animate-bounce">
          ↓
        </div>
      )}
    </section>
  )
}

                <div>
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium">Real-time demand</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Current availability and trending activity</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          {/* Right - Ranked Cards */}
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mb-4">Results for "{intent}"</p>
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {results.slice(0, 5).map((r, i) => (
                <div
                  key={r.id}
                  className={`p-4 rounded-xl transition-all ${
                    bestMatch?.id === r.id 
                      ? 'bg-white/10 border-l-2 border-l-primary' 
                      : 'bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10'
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                    <div>
                      <p className="font-medium">{r.name}</p>
                      <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{r.cuisine} • {r.price}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {r.rating}</span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-sm text-white/60 mb-2">{r.reasoning}</p>
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
                    <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full ${
                      r.availability === 'available' ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' :
                      r.availability === 'limited' ? 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400' :
                      'bg-red-500/20 text-red-400'
                    }`}>
                      {r.availability === 'available' ? 'Available now' : 
                       r.availability === 'limited' ? 'Limited availability' : 
                       'Busy'}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-xs text-white/30">
                      {Math.round(r.final_score * 100)}% match
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
🤖 4️⃣ AI CONCIERGE (REAL CONTEXT)
tsx
// components/landing/AIConcierge.tsx
'use client'

import { useState } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'

export default function AIConcierge() {
  const { results, bestMatch, intent } = useSufiStore()
  const [question, setQuestion] = useState('')
  const [response, setResponse] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)
  
  if (results.length === 0) return null
  
  const handleAsk = async () => {
    if (!question.trim()) return
    
    setLoading(true)
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/ai', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({ 
          query: question,
          intent,
          context: results.slice(0, 3)
        })
      })
      const data = await res.json()
      setResponse(data.message)
    } catch (error) {
      setResponse("I'm having trouble connecting. Please try again.")
    } finally {
      setLoading(false)
    }
  }
  
  return (
    <section className="py-20 px-6 border-t border-white/5 bg-[#0a0a0a]">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
        <div className="text-center mb-8">
          <p className="text-sm text-white/40 uppercase tracking-wide">AI Concierge</p>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-medium mt-2">Ask about these results</h2>
        </div>
        
        {/* Context cards */}
        <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 mb-8">
          {results.slice(0, 2).map(r => (
            <div key={r.id} className="p-4 bg-white/5 rounded-xl">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                <div>
                  <p className="font-medium">{r.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-sm text-white/40">{r.cuisine} • {r.vibe}</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-yellow-400 text-sm">★ {r.rating}</span>
              </div>
              <p className="text-sm text-white/60">{r.reasoning}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        
        {/* Chat */}
        <div className="bg-white/5 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
          <div className="p-4 border-b border-white/10">
            <p className="text-sm text-white/60">
              {bestMatch 
                ? `"${bestMatch.name}" matches your intent for ${intent}.` 
                : "Ask about availability, pricing, or the vibe."}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-4">
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={question}
                onChange={(e) => setQuestion(e.target.value)}
                onKeyPress={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAsk()}
                placeholder="Ask about availability, pricing, or vibe..."
                className="flex-1 bg-transparent border border-white/10 rounded-xl px-4 py-3
                         text-white placeholder:text-white/30 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-white/20"
              />
              <button
                onClick={handleAsk}
                disabled={loading}
                className="px-5 py-2 bg-white/10 rounded-xl text-sm hover:bg-white/20 transition-all disabled:opacity-50"
              >
                {loading ? '...' : 'Ask'}
              </button>
            </div>
            {response && (
              <div className="mt-4 p-3 bg-white/5 rounded-lg">
                <p className="text-sm text-white/80">{response}</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}
📊 5️⃣ LIVE METRICS (REAL-TIME)
tsx
// components/landing/LiveMetrics.tsx
'use client'

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { useSufiStore } from '@/lib/state/sufiStore'
import gsap from 'gsap'

export default function LiveMetrics() {
  const { globalMetrics, updateMetrics } = useSufiStore()
  const [bookings, setBookings] = useState(0)
  const [trending, setTrending] = useState(0)
  const [active, setActive] = useState(0)
  
  // Fetch real-time metrics
  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchMetrics = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/trends')
        const data = await res.json()
        updateMetrics(data)
      } catch (error) {
        // Silent fail - keep calm
      }
    }
    
    fetchMetrics()
    const interval = setInterval(fetchMetrics, 10000)
    return () => clearInterval(interval)
  }, [updateMetrics])
  
  // Animate metrics
  useEffect(() => {
    gsap.to({ value: bookings }, {
      value: globalMetrics.bookings_last_hour,
      duration: 1,
      onUpdate: function() {
        setBookings(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
      }
    })
    gsap.to({ value: trending }, {
      value: globalMetrics.trending_locations,
      duration: 1,
      onUpdate: function() {
        setTrending(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
      }
    })
    gsap.to({ value: active }, {
      value: globalMetrics.active_users,
      duration: 1,
      onUpdate: function() {
        setActive(Math.floor(this.targets()[0].value))
      }
    })
  }, [globalMetrics])
  
  return (
    <section className="py-20 px-6 border-t border-white/5 bg-[#0a0a0a]">
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto text-center">
        <p className="text-sm text-white/40 uppercase tracking-wide mb-4">Live System</p>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
          <div className="p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-2xl">
            <p className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-semibold">{bookings}</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mt-1">bookings last hour</p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-2xl">
            <p className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-semibold">{trending}</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mt-1">trending locations</p>
          </div>
          <div className="p-6 bg-white/5 rounded-2xl">
            <p className="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-semibold">{active}</p>
            <p className="text-sm text-white/40 mt-1">active users</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  )
}

// app/api/search/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { query } = await request.json()
    
    // Mock data - replace with real backend call
    const mockResults = [
      {
        id: '1',
        name: 'Sky Lounge',
        cuisine: 'Contemporary',
        rating: 4.8,
        price: '$$$',
        vibe: 'Romantic',
        availability: 'available',
        reasoning: 'Rooftop with wine list matches your intent',
        final_score: 0.94
      },
      {
        id: '2',
        name: 'The Rooftop Garden',
        cuisine: 'Mediterranean',
        rating: 4.6,
        price: '$$$',
        vibe: 'Romantic',
        availability: 'limited',
        reasoning: 'Rooftop setting with sunset views',
        final_score: 0.87
      },
      {
        id: '3',
        name: 'Vine & Tapas',
        cuisine: 'Spanish',
        rating: 4.5,
        price: '$$',
        vibe: 'Casual',
        availability: 'available',
        reasoning: 'Extensive wine selection',
        final_score: 0.82
      }
    ]
    
    return NextResponse.json({ results: mockResults })
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Search failed', results: [] }, { status: 500 })
  }
}
tsx
// app/api/ai/route.ts
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const { query, intent, context } = await request.json()
    
    // Mock AI response
    const response = `Based on your search for "${intent}", ${context?.[0]?.name || 'the top result'} is an excellent match. It offers ${context?.[0]?.vibe?.toLowerCase() || 'great'} ambiance and is currently ${context?.[0]?.availability || 'available'}. Would you like to know more about availability or pricing?`
    
    return NextResponse.json({ message: response })
  } catch (error) {
    return NextResponse.json({ message: "I can help you find restaurants. What are you looking for?" })
  }
}

}
